§ 1 pratijñāsūtra PJS

viśuddhajñānadehāya trivedīdivyacakṣuṣe | śreyaḥprāptinimittāya namaḥ somārdhadhāriṇe ||
abhivandya gurūnādau śiṣyadhīpadminīravīn | tatprasādāt kariṣye 'haṃ mīmāṃsāślokavārttikaṃ ||
tadvidvāṃso 'nugṛhṇantu cittaśrotraiḥ prasādibhiḥ | santaḥ praṇayivākyāni gṛhṇanti hy anasūyavaḥ ||
na cātrātiva kartavyaṃ doṣadṛṣṭiparaṃ manaḥ | doṣo hy avidyamāno 'pi taccittānāṃ prakāśate ||
kuto vā gṛhṇate doṣaṃ sūrayo madvidhoktiṣu | neṣyate yaḥ parastho 'pi sa svayaṃ gṛhyate katham ||
nirdoṣatvaikavākyatvaṃ kva vā lokasya dṛśyate | sāpavādā yataḥ ke cin mokṣasvargāv api prati ||
āgamapravaṇaś cāhaṃ nāpavādyaḥ skhaliteṣv apy apodyate | na hi sadvartmanā gacchan skhaliteṣv apy apodyate ||
yathā kathañ cid ārabdhā trayīmārgānusāriṇī | vāgvṛttir alpasārāpi śraddadhānasya śobhate ||
mīmāṃsāśāstratejobhir viśeṣeṇoj jvalīkṛte | vedārthajñānaratne me tṛṣṇātīva vijṛmbhate ||
prāyenaiva hi mīmāṃsā loke lokāyatīkṛtā | tāmāstikapathe kartum ayaṃ yatnaḥ kṛto mayā ||
athāto dharmajijñāsā sūtram ādyam idaṃ kṛtam | dharmākhyaṃ viṣayaṃ vaktuṃ mīmāṃsāyāḥ prayojanam ||
sarvasyaiva hi śāstrasya karmaṇo vāpi kasya cit | yāvat prayojanaṃ noktaṃ tāvat tat kena gṛhyate ||
mīmāṃsākhyā tu vidyeyaṃ bahuvidyāntarāśritā | na śuśrūṣayituṃ śakyā prāganuktvā prayojanam ||
vidyāntareṣu nāpy etad yady abhīṣṭaṃ prayojanam | anarthaprāpaṇaṃ tāvat tebhyo nāśaṅkyate kva cit ||
mīmāṃsāyāṃ tv ihājñāte durjñāte vāvivekataḥ | nyāyamārge mahān doṣa iti yatnopacaryatā ||
tasmāt prayojanaṃ pūrvam uktaṃ sūtrakṛtā svayam | yat svenoktaṃ vadeyus tad bhāṣyakārādayaḥ katham ||
siddhārthaṃ jñātasambandhaṃ śrotuṃ śrotā pravartate | śāstrādau tena vaktavyaḥ sambandhaḥ saprayojanaḥ ||
śāstraṃ prayojanaṃ caiva sambandhasyāśrayāv ubhau | taduktyantargatas tasmād bhinno noktaḥ prayojanāt ||
siddhiḥ śrotṛpravṛttīnāṃ sambandhakathanād yataḥ | tasmāt sarveṣu śāstreṣu sambandhaḥ pūrvam ucyate ||
yāvat prayojanenāsya sambandho nābhidhīyate | asambaddhapralāpitvād bhavet tāvad asaṃgatiḥ ||
iha tv ākṣipya sambandhaṃ bhāṣya evābhidhāsyate | dharmaprasiddhyasiddhibhyāṃ, tasmān nānyo 'bhidhīyate ||
na cāpy atrāthaśabdena śāstrasambandha ucyate | sambandhaṃ kriyayor hy eṣa brūte śāstrāc ca te pṛthak ||
yo 'py ayaṃ śāstrasambandho varṇyate kaiś cid āditaḥ | kriyānantaryarūpo vā guruparvakramo 'pi vā ||
sadasadbhāvayos tasya viśeṣo nopalabhyate | śroturvidhau niṣedhe vā jñāne vā śāstragocare ||
tasmād vyākhyāṅgam icchadbhiḥ sahetuḥ saprayojanaḥ | śāstrāvatārasambandho vācyo nānyas tu niṣphalaḥ ||
loke ityādibhāṣyasya ṣaḍarthān sampracakṣate | bhāṣyakārānusāreṇa, prayuktasyāditaḥ pṛthak ||
sarvavyākhyām upālambhaṃ pratyākhyānaṃ tathā pare | parisaṃkhyāstutī kecid athaśabdasya dūṣaṇam ||
sādhāraṇī viśiṣṭā ca sūtravyākhyā dvidhā matā | viśiṣṭā pratisūtraṃ yā sarvārthā tv iyam ucyate ||
pravṛttis tu padeṣv eva nivṛttiḥ sūtrasaṃśrayā | vedavākyāviruddheṣu na tu sarveṣu keṣu cit ||
adhyāhārasya vākyeṣu vyatyāsasya ca sambhavāt | tenaiṣām iti sūtrāṇāṃ pārārthye saty api grahaḥ ||
evaśabdo 'lpavācyatvād, asyāvṛttau tu gauravam | prasiddhatvād avācyaṃ cet, na doṣaḥ puṅgirām ayam ||
vyākhyāṅgatvābhimānena yo 'dhyāhārādyapekṣate | svasaṃjñāṃ vāpi tasyedaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ nirūpyate ||
vṛtyantareṣu keṣāñ cil laukikārthavyatikramaḥ | śabdānāṃ dṛśyate teṣam upālambho 'yam ucyate ||
athāta ity ayaṃ loke nānantarye prayujyate | tasmāt tādarthyam etasya paribhāṣādibhir bhavet ||
prasiddhahāniḥ śabdānām aprasiddhe ca kalpanā | na kāryā vṛttikāreṇa sati siddhārthasambhave ||
sūtrārthe kliśyataś caivaṃ dūre vedārthanirṇayaḥ | tatra yatnasya bhāratvaṃ vaktṛśrotroḥ prasajyate ||
na vyākhyāsyati sūtrāṇi codanārthaparatvataḥ | yat tasya parihāro 'yaṃ pratyākhyānena cocyate ||
prayāso vedavākyeṣu kāryaḥ sūtreṣv anena kim | phalavattvāphalatvābhyām, ebhiḥ karaṇasammataiḥ ||
codanārtha upetavyaḥ, nobhayaṃ yatnagauravāt | padārthānāṃ prasiddhatvāt vyākhyeyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
evaṃśabdādiko granthaḥ pakṣe cāsmin samarthyate | padacchedādyabhāvena pratyākhyānamatis tv iyam ||
brabīty eva hi sūtrārtham, atiriktādi ceṣyate | nanv aśaktam idaṃ sūtraṃ samyak sūtritam ity api ||
sūtre cāgamakatvādi pratyākhyāne virudhyate | na copāyānabhijñena śakyopeyāvadhāraṇā ||
nānyato vedavidbhyaś ca sūtravṛttikriyeṣyate | pratyākhyānasya hetuś ca padārthānāṃ prasiddhatā ||
yoktā sā vedavākyānaṃ tulyārthatvān nivārayet | vākyārthe tatra sandehād vyākhyānaṃ cet pravartate ||
sūtreṣv api samānatvāt pratyākhyānaṃ na yujyate | na vyākhyātavyam ityevaṃ pratyākhyāne ca sidhyati ||
duṣṭavyākhyā niṣedhena tadapetā na vāryate | asya dṛṣṭaviruddhatvāt phalgutvāc cāpi parvayoḥ ||
madhyame cātidaurjanyāt parisaṃkhyaiva yujyate | vaidikaṃ jaiminīyaṃ ca yatra vākyaṃ virudhyate ||
yathāśrutagṛhīte 'rthe tatredam upadiśyate | adhyāhārādibhiḥ sūtraṃ vaidikaṃ tu yathāśrutam ||
neyam, virodhe 'nyonyasya vaidikānāṃ bhavantu te | yathā dharmāvabodhasya pramāṇaṃ vaidikaṃ vacaḥ ||
tadarthanirṇaye hetur jaiminīyaṃ tathaiva naḥ | vākyasāmarthyatulyatvāt tathā padatadarthayoḥ ||
adhyāhārādibhir muktā vyākhyā sarvatra yujyate | asambhavād avaśyaṃ yā virodhe 'nyatarasya tu ||
anyāyyakalpanā sāpi vikalpena prasajyate | prāthamyenāvaruddhatvād upāyavaśato 'tha vā ||
yathāśrutena sūtreṇa nyāyyāṃ bādheta codanām | tena vedāviruddhasya sati sambhava ity ayam ||
vidhīyate 'rthaḥ, śeṣaṃ tu yathāprāptam anūdyate | śeṣabhājāṃ bhavel lopa ity adhyāhārakalpanā ||
viprakarṣāt paśoś ceti vibhaktiḥ pariṇamyate | padena vyavadhānaṃ tu loke saṃniyamād iti ||
sūtreṇa vyavadhānaṃ tu pānavyāpadi kalpitam | paśusāmānyavidhyādau sūtram evānyathā kṛtam ||
agnayaś ca svakālatvād deyadharmāpayātanam | vyākhyānaṃ vākyabhedena, guṇakalpās tv amī kṛtāḥ ||
autpattikas tu gavyasya tathoṣṇikkakubhor iti | darśanāc ca viśeṣasya tathābhyudaya ity api ||
sūtrakārapraśaṃsā vā loka ityādinocyate | prasiddhair abhidhānād dhi na śiṣyāḥ kleśitā yataḥ ||
bhavitavyaṃ tu teneti prāgasmād ekavākyatā | vedādhyayanavākyād vā tenāthety asya dūṣaṇam ||
prasiddhārthapadaiḥ śakyaḥ sūtrair vedārthanirṇayaḥ | na ca so 'sty athaśabdasya vinā te pūrvakarmaṇā ||
prasiddhārthaṃ padaṃ yuktaṃ tac ca nāstīti dūṣaṇam | prasiddho 'py athaśabdādeḥ kiṃpadārtho 'tra varṇyate ||
pradarśanārtham ity eke, ke cin nānārthavācinaḥ | samudāyād avacchidya bhavadāsena kalpitāt ||
śaktito 'vayavaṃ caiva varṇayantyaṣṭamādivat | na cātra codanāvyākhyā gauravaṃ tatra coditam ||
yad vākṣepo yathoktasya vṛttābhāvād asambhavāt | yadi lokaprasiddhārthagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pade ||
sa nāsty atrāthaśabdasyety adhyāhārādikalpanam | vedādhyayanavṛttatvaṃ snānasyotkarṣakalpanā ||
nāvyākhyāte 'thaśabdārthe jñāyate tena varṇyate | anarthake 'tha vānyārthe prasiddhir bādhyate dhruvam ||
tasmāc chrutārthasiddhyarthaṃ vṛttaṃ kim api gamyate | viśiṣṭaliṅgavijñānād viśiṣṭe liṅginīkṣite ||
sūtreṇāsambhavaṃ matvā naitad ity abravīt paraḥ | ānantaryopadeśena taddṛṣṭārthatayāpi ca ||
vedādhyayanam ākṣiptaṃ kim asūtritacodanā | yena vṛttena jijñāsā vinā naivopapadyate ||
tadānantaryam uktaṃ hi dṛṣṭārtham avakalpate | kriyamāṇā ca jijñāsā niyamād yasya kasya cit ||
kriyetānantaraiveti vyarthaṃ tadupadeśanam | saṅkalpādibhir apy eṣā vinā satyaṃ na sidhyati ||
sādhāraṇyāt tu te 'py atra nopadeśyāḥ kathañ cana | tasmād dharmabubhutsāyām asādhāraṇakāraṇam ||
nirvṛttaṃ sūtrakāreṣṭaṃ tac ca nākhyayanād ṛte | anyasyāpīty anenaiva vedapāṭhe prabādhite ||
prāg apīti hi vaktavyaṃ tatrāpy anyasya sambhavāt | pūrveṇaiva hi labdhārthe tādṛśīṃ tv ity anena kim ||
vakṣyamāṇam anālocya sambhavet paricodanā | na tāvat sādhyate 'dyāpi codanā dharmasādhanam ||
iha vā kāni vākyāni vivariṣyati jaiminiḥ | dharmamātrābhidhānād dhi buddhādivacanāny api ||
paṭhitvā dharmajijñāsety anyasyāpīti codanā | yad vā bhavatu nāmedṛk sūtraṃ vedam adhītya tu ||
jijñāsānantaraṃ kāryety atrāpi dvayam īpsitam | nānadhītya na cāpy anyat kṛtvety etan na labhyate ||
vakṣyamāṇavacobhaṅgyor vākyabhedaprasaṅgataḥ | adhītyaiveti hi vidhau snānāder apy anantarā ||
bhaved dharmasya jijñāsā nānantaryavidhis tadā | ānantaryavidhāne tu yā vedādhyayane kṛte ||
ity evam anuvādatvāt prāg apy eṣā prasajyate | buddhavākyādipāṭhasya tādṛśīṃ tv ity apākriyā ||
prāg apīti ca codyasya, sāmarthyād vedalābhataḥ | naivaitayor vacobhaṅgyor eko 'py artho vidhīyate ||
api cetyādikenoktam, kin tv ityetad vidhīyate | ānantaryaṃ parastāc ca nāpi śiṃṣma itīha tu ||
ke cid adhyāharanti, asya sūtrasyānyaparatvataḥ | na vāryate 'nadhītatvaṃ nānantaryaṃ vidhīyate ||
sāmarthyāsiddhyadṛṣṭārthaprasaṅgāt tena lakṣaṇā | ānantaryavacovyaktir āśritaivātra lakṣyate ||
śrutārthaṃ tv aparityajya lakṣaṇārtho vidhīyate | pratītā dharmajijñāsā vedādhyāyād anantarā ||
tatkālasyāvaruddhatvāt snānābhāvaṃ hi lakṣayet | virodho yugapatprāpteḥ, daurbalyaṃ vedabādhanāt ||
snānasya tena bādhaḥ syād dharmajijñāsayā balāt | dṛṣṭārthatvādisaṃyuktaṃ vākyaṃ lakṣaṇayā tv iti ||
punaruktyā gatārthatvāt tyaktaṃ kaiś cit, tad ucyate | yady apy asya bhaved vācyam ānantaryam asaṃśayam ||
tathāpi pūrvatāmātraṃ lakṣayed avirodhataḥ | granthagrahaṇamātre ca kṛte snānaṃ virudhyate ||
adhītyetyadhigamyeti vyākhyāne tv avirodhitā | yas tv evamavirodhitvaṃ kurvannāplavanaṃ vadet ||
adṛṣṭāyātha vāpy anyaḥ saṃskāraṃ tasya cottaram | ihāsnānādiniyamo yaḥ kṛto brahmacāriṇaḥ ||
avidhitvam anāśritya so 'vasānam apekṣate | tato 'pekṣāvaśāt snānam asnānādinivartanam ||
virodhasāhacaryābhyāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvena lakṣayet | tasmād adhyayanasnānajijñāsākramavācinām ||
dṛṣṭārthatvāya śabdānām evaṃ vyākhyeyam āśritā | snātvā jijñāsamāno 'pi nanu vedaṃ na bādhate ||
tenāvirodhitā tasya, ityevaṃ vadata uttaram | yathaivādhyayanāt snānaṃ smaryate samanantaram ||
tathā tataḥ paro 'py anyaḥ padārtho 'nyaḥ paras tataḥ | tataś cāvaśyakartavye bādhe smārtasya kasya cit ||
yogyatvād āgate kāle prāthamyāt snānabādhanam | so 'yaṃ pāṭhakramasyārthād bādha ity avagamyate ||
guṇapradhānayor vāpi virodhād guṇabādhanam | snānopalakṣitā cātra nivṛttir guruveśmanaḥ ||
virodhitvena bādhyeta na tu madhvādibhakṣaṇam | tasmād gurukule tiṣṭhanmadhumāṃsādyavarjayan ||
jijñāsetāviruddhatvād dharmam ity avagamyate | gurugehanivṛttyaṃśo yāvac ca na samāpyate ||
tāvat sakalavācitvān na snānaṃ paryavasyati | gurugehādanāvṛttaḥ snātako hi na kathyate ||
tatparatvavidhānāc ca na tāvad dārasaṅgrahaḥ | vyākhyāya kīrtitā cātra snāyād iti punaḥ smṛtiḥ ||
smāvartiṣṭa metyādi smṛter yady apy anantaram | viparītārtham ity asmāt tadvākyād apanīyate ||
athaśabdena yo bādhaḥ purastād upavarṇitaḥ | tanmātrasyaiva bādho 'tra dṛṣṭārthatvāt pradarśitaḥ ||
smṛtiprāptam idānīṃ tu madhumāṃsādyavarjanam | pratiṣedhann adṛṣṭārthaṃ sūtrakāro na śobhate ||
nivṛttya gurugehāc ca jijñāsārthaḥ punar bhavet | praveśaḥ so 'py adṛṣṭārtha iti naiveha sūtritaḥ ||
nirgamo hi kṛtārthasya dṛṣṭārtho guruveśmanaḥ | smaryate tasya nārthaḥ syād akṛtārthasya nirgame ||
athaśabdaprasiddhyaiva vedagrahaṇahetutā | ānantaryopadeśitvād ataḥ śabdena kiṃ punaḥ ||
yogyatvam athaśabdena yady api pratipāditam | tad eva hetur atreti nātaḥśabdād vinā bhavet ||
lakṣaṇaṃ puruṣasyaiva tadā tad dhi prasajyate | jijñāsāyāś ca hetutve phalārthatvādi sambhavet ||
ataḥśabdagṛhītaṃ vā tatrādhyayanam āśritam | hetāvakathyamāne hi maṅgalādy apy asau vadet ||
snānabādhasya vā hetur ata ity ucyate punaḥ | yogyasyādhītavedatvān nāvasthātuṃ hi labhyate ||
sanvācyecchāntaraṃ karma jñānaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatā | jñānopasarjanā saiva na tu vidhyādi gamyate ||
iṣes tu karma bāhyaḥ syād dharmaḥ sā vātha vā dvayam | samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu tumunoktaṃ liṅā vidhiḥ ||
evaṃ viṣayanānātvān na kā cit punaruktatā | sūtritecchābhinirvṛttyai dvitīyecchātra sūtritā ||
prakṛtyā vikṛtir yasmāc caturthyantā samasyate | tādarthye yūpadārvādau tenāsminn asamāsatā ||
sa hi tasyety anenokto dharmasyety eṣa vigrahaḥ | dharmāyeti tu tādarthye ṣaṣṭhī vṛtteti kathyate ||
prāpnoty atra caturthy eva viśeṣaś ced vivakṣitaḥ | sāmānyasya vivakṣāyāṃ tādṛśaṃ kathyate katham ||
sambandhamātra evaiṣā ṣaṣṭhyutpannā tathāpi tu | viśeṣaniṣṭhatā tasyā bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
sādhanābhāsatā cātra pūrvapakṣārthagocarā | anyasādhanam anyasya sādhanābhāsa ucyate ||
kratvarthaṃ puruṣārthasya tadarthaṃ ca krator iti | śeṣalakṣaṇaśabdaś ca kṛtsnaśāstravivakṣayā ||
prasiddhaḥ śakyate jñātum prasiddhatvāt tu neṣyate | aprasiddhas tv aśakyatvānnatarām ity ato 'bravīt ||
jijñāsyaḥ saṃśayād dharmaḥ śreyaskaratayāpi ca | asandigdho hy ajijñāsyo yo vā syān niṣprayojanaḥ ||
svarūpādiṣu dharmasya dvidhā vipratipadyate | pūrvaṃ pramāṇarūpābhyām, pādenādyasya nirṇayaḥ ||
sthite vedapramāṇatve punar vākyārthanirṇaye | matir bahuvidāṃ puṃsāṃ saṃśayān nopajāyate ||
ke cid āhur asāv arthaḥ, ke cin nāsāv ayaṃ tv iti | tannirṇayārtham apy etat paraṃ śāstraṃ praṇīyate ||

§ 2 codanāsūtra CDS

dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ codanocyate | svarūpādes tataḥ siddhaḥ, svarūpaṃ ceha sūtryate ||
dvayam ekena sūtreṇa śrutyarthābhyāṃ nirūpyate | svarūpe 'pi hi tasyokte pramāṇaṃ kathyate 'rthataḥ ||
kimādyapekṣitaiḥ pūrṇaḥ samarthaḥ pratyayo vidhau | tena pravartakaṃ vākyaṃ śāstre 'smin codanocyate ||
codanaiva pramāṇaṃ cetyetaddharme 'vadhāritam | sākāṅkṣam iti manvāno yuktileśaṃ dvaye 'spṛśat ||
sambhāvyate pramāṇatvaṃ śabdasyaivaṃvidheṣv api | indriyāder asāmarthyaṃ vakṣyamāṇamadīdiśat ||
atyantāsaty api jñānam arthe śabdaḥ karoti hi | tenotsarge sthite tasya doṣābhāvāt pramāṇatā ||
codanety abravīc cātra śabdamātravivakṣayā | na hi bhūtādiviṣayaḥ kaś cid asti vidhāyakaḥ ||
indriyādivyudāsena śabdo yāvan na sādhyate | tāvac ca tadviśeṣasya kuto vāvasaro bhavet ||
nimittamātraṃ vocyeta pramāṇaṃ ceha lakṣaṇam | pramāṇaṃ tv api śabdo vā tajjñānaṃ vā nirūpyate ||
padārthas tanmatir vā syād vākyārthādhigamo 'pi vā | pūrveṣāṃ tu pramāṇatve phalatvaṃ tasya gamyate ||
jñāne lakṣaṇaśabdo 'yaṃ yadi nāma prayujyate | codanoktis tadā kāryaṃ tatkāryaṃ cāpi lakṣayet ||
nimittamātre śabde ca pramāṇe mukhyavṛttayoḥ | sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ syāc codanālakṣaṇatvayoḥ ||
dravyakriyāguṇādīnāṃ dharmatvaṃ sthāpayiṣyate | teṣām aindriyakatve 'pi na tādrūpyeṇa dharmatā ||
śreyaḥsādhanatā hy eṣāṃ nityaṃ vedāt pratīyate | tādrūpyeṇa ca dharmatvaṃ tasmān nendriyagocaraḥ ||
pradarśanārtham atroktam indriyaṃ sūtrakāravat | nānyat kiñ ceti vācchedaḥ sāmānyārthaḥ prayujyate ||
tadasāmarthyasiddhyai ca punar indriyakīrtanam | kiñ ceti madhyam acchedo hetupraśne prayujyate ||
yady api tv anumānasyāpy evamādau samarthatā | vinā sambandhabodhena na tu tasyodbhavaḥ kva cit ||
na sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ dharmasambandhadarśanam | liṅgasya kasya cit siddhaṃ yena syād anumānatā ||
nanu śabdo 'pi sambandhabodhānnarte pravarttate | padaṃ tat, na ca tadvācyo dharmaḥ, vākyārtha eva saḥ ||
vākyasyāvācakatvaṃ ca, padārthānāṃ ca hetutā | sambandhasyānapekṣāṇāṃ vākyārthe sthāpayiṣyate ||
nityatvāder asiddhatvād, abhyupetyocyate 'tha vā | sutarām apramāṇatvaṃ vaktṛprāmāṇyavarjanāt ||
pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭaṃ hi śabdo 'rthaṃ prāpayet sadā | smṛtivac ca svayaṃ tasya prāmāṇyaṃ nopapadyate ||
nūnaṃ tatrānubhūto 'sāvityāptoktinibandhanā | buddhiḥ sākṣād adṛṣṭe 'pi yuktārthe puruṣoktitaḥ ||
nātmīyād anyadīyād vā pratyakṣāder vinā kva cit | vacasaḥ satyatā dṛṣṭā tathā syāc codanāsv api ||
tena saty api vijñāne pratijñāder yathaiva hi | svātantryān na pramāṇatvaṃ tathā vede 'pi dṛśyatām ||
svargayāgādisambandhaviṣayā codanā mṛṣā | pratyakṣādyagatārthatvādīdṛgbuddhādivākyavat ||
yad vāptenāpraṇītatvād bālonmattādivākyavat | vyomādivac ca nityatvāt prāmāṇyasya nirākṛtiḥ ||
yadi vā puruṣādhīnaprāmāṇyāḥ sarvacodanāḥ | svato vā na pramāṇaṃ syur vākyatvāt puruṣoktivat ||
prāmāṇyaṃ vā narāpekṣaṃ sarvaśabdeṣu gamyatām | śabdaiḥ sambandhyamānatvād apramāṇyaṃ tathaiva hi ||
na syād vaktṛguṇānāṃ ced vacaḥ prāmāṇyahetutā | taddoṣair apramāṇatvaṃ kim ity asya bhaviṣyati ||
evaṃ sthite tu vedasya sati vāsati vā nare | prāmāṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā nanv ity etadacūcudat ||
tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ buddhavākye 'pi yujyate | tato 'pi pratyayotpattes tasmāj jātyuttaraṃ tv idam ||
sarvavijñānaviṣayam idaṃ tāvat parīkṣyatām | pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve svataḥ kiṃ parato 'tha vā ||
svato 'satām asādhyatvāt ke cid āhur dvayaṃ svataḥ | apare kāraṇotpannaguṇadoṣāvadhāraṇāt ||
svatas tāvad dvayaṃ nāsti, virodhāt, parato na ca | niḥsvabhāvatvam evaṃ hi jñānarūpe prasajyate ||
kathaṃ hy anyānapekṣasya viparītātmasambhavaḥ | kimātmakaṃ bhavet tac ca svabhāvadvayavarjitam ||
vijñānavyaktibhedena bhavec ced aviruddhatā | tathāpy anyānapekṣatve kiṃ kveti na nirūpyate ||
tasmāt svābhāvikaṃ teṣām apramāṇatvam iṣyatām | prāmāṇyañ ca parāpekṣam, atra nyāyo 'bhidhīyate ||
aprāmānyam avastutvān na syāt kāraṇadoṣataḥ | vastutvāt tu guṇais teṣāṃ prāmāṇyam upajanyate ||
prāmāṇyaṃ hi yadotsargāt tadabhāvo 'tha kṛtrimaḥ | tadā svapnādibodhe 'pi prāmāṇyaṃ kena vāryate ||
matpakṣe kāraṇābhāvāt prāmānyaṃ nopajāyate | hetumattvaprasaṅgo 'to na bhaviṣyaty avastunaḥ ||
indriyādiguṇāś cāsya kāraṇam, tadasad dvidhā | duṣṭatvād indriyādīnām abhāve 'nyatamasya vā ||
ata eva ca vo bhrāntir doṣair mithyātvadhīr iti | tadvyāptes tu guṇābhāvas tatkṛtā hy apramāṇatā ||
tasmāt kāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ jñānaprāmāṇyakāraṇam | svabhāvato 'pramāṇatvaṃ tadabhāvena lakṣyate ||
anvayavyatirekābhyām aprāmāṇyaṃ na doṣataḥ | nājñāne dṛśyate hy etatkāraṇābhāvahetuke ||
tataś ca puruṣābhāvāt sati vā śuddhyasambhavāt | nirmūlatvāt pramāṇatvaṃ codanāyāṃ na yujyate ||
svataḥ sarvapramāṇānāṃ prāmāṇyam iti gamyatām | na hi svato 'satī śaktiḥ kartum anyena śakyate ||
ātmalābhe ca bhāvānāṃ kāraṇāpekṣatā bhavet | labdhātmanāṃ svakāryeṣu pravṛttiḥ svayam eva tu ||
jāte 'pi yadi vijñāne tāvan nārtho 'vadhāryate | yāvatkāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ na pramāṇāntarād bhavet ||
tatra jñānāntarotpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt | yāvad dhi na paricchinnā śuddhis tāvad asatsamā ||
tasyāpi kāraṇe śuddhe tajjñāne syāt pramāṇatā | tasyāpy evam itīcchaś ca na kva cid vyavatiṣṭhate ||
yadā svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ tadānyan naiva gṛhyate | nivarttatte hi mithyātvaṃ doṣājñānād ayatnataḥ ||
tasmād bodhātmakatvena prāptā buddheḥ pramāṇatā | arthānyathātvahetūtthadoṣajñānād apodyate ||
aprāmāṇyaṃ tridhā bhinnaṃ mithyātvājñānasaṃśayaiḥ | vastutvād dvividhasyātra sambhavo duṣṭakāraṇāt ||
avijñāne tu doṣāṇāṃ vyāpāro naiva kalpyate | kāraṇābhāvatas tv eva tatsiddhaṃ nastvaduktivat ||
doṣataś cāpramāṇatve svataḥprāmāṇyavādinām | guṇajñānānavasthāvan na doṣeṣu prasajyate ||
sākṣād viparyayajñānāl laghvyeva tv apramāṇatā | pūrvābādhena notpattir uttarasya hi sidhyati ||
duṣṭakāraṇabodhe tu siddhe 'pi viṣayāntare | arthāt tulyārthatāṃ prāpya bādho godohanādivat ||
tatra doṣāntarajñānaṃ bādhadhīr vā parā na cet | tadudbhūtau dvitīyasya mithyātvād ādyamānatā ||
svata eva hi tatrāpi doṣājñānāt pramāṇatā | doṣajñāne tv anutpanne na śaṅkyā niṣpramāṇatā ||
evaṃ tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥ | prārthyate tāvataivaikaṃ svataḥ prāmāṇyam aśnute ||
śabde doṣodbhavas tāvad vaktradhīna iti sthitiḥ | tadabhāvaḥ kva cit tāvad guṇavadvaktṛkatvataḥ ||
tadguṇair apakṛṣṭānāṃ śabde saṃkrāntyasambhavāt | yadā vaktur abhāvena na syur doṣā nirāśrayāḥ ||
pauruṣeye dvayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ doṣābhāvo guṇās tathā | prāmāṇyaṃ tatra guṇato naiva syād ity udāhṛtam ||
tasmād guṇebhyo doṣāṇām abhāvas tadabhāvataḥ | aprāmāṇyadvayāsattvaṃ tenotsargo 'napoditaḥ ||
pratyayotpattihetutvāt prāmāṇyaṃ nāpanīyate | doṣābhāvo guṇebhyaś cen nanu saivāsthitir bhavet ||
tadā tu vyāpriyante hi jñāyamānatayā guṇāḥ | doṣābhāve tu vijñeye sattāmātropakāriṇaḥ ||
tatrāpavādanirmuktir vaktrabhāvāl laghīyasī | vede tenāpramāṇatvaṃ nāśaṅkām api gacchati ||
ato vaktranadhīnatvāt prāmāṇye tadupāsanam | na yuktam, apramāṇatve kalpye tatprārthanā bhavet ||
tataś cāptāpraṇītatvaṃ na doṣāyātra jāyate | prayogāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ pratisādhanam ||
pauruṣeye tu vacane pramāṇāntaramūlatā | tadabhāve hi tad duṣyeditaran na kadā cana ||
tenetaraiḥ pramāṇair yā codanānām asaṅgatiḥ | tayaiva syāt pramāṇatvam anuvādatvam anyathā ||
anyasyāpi pramāṇatve saṅgatir naiva kāraṇam | tulyārthānāṃ vikalpyatvād ekaṃ tatra hi bodhakam ||
yatrāpi syāt paricchedaḥ pramāṇair uttaraiḥ punaḥ | nūnaṃ tatrāpi pūrveṇa so 'rtho nāvadhṛtas tathā ||
saṅgatyā yadi ceṣyeta pūrvapūrvapramāṇatā | pramāṇāntaram icchanto na vyavasthāṃ labhemahi ||
kasya cit tu yadīṣyeta svata eva pramāṇatā | prathamasya tathābhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ ||
śrotradhīś cāpramāṇaṃ syād itarābhir asaṅgateḥ | syāc cet tajjanitenaiva jñānenānyena saṅgatiḥ ||
vede 'pi śatakṛtvaḥ syād buddhir uccāraṇānugā | sādhanāntarajanyā tu buddhir nāsti dvayor api ||
yathā tv ekendriyādhīnajñānāntaranibandhanā | saṅgatiḥ kāraṇaṃ prāptā tathā vede 'pi kalpyatām ||
tasmād dṛḍhaṃ yadutpannaṃ nāpi saṃvādamṛcchati | jñānāntareṇa vijñānaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ pratīyatām ||
na cānumānataḥ sādhyā śabdādīnāṃ pramāṇatā | sarvasyaiva hi mā prāpat pramāṇāntarasādhyatā ||
nanu pramāṇam ityevaṃ pratyakṣādi na gṛhyate | na cetthamagṛhītena vyavahāro 'vakalpate ||
prāmāṇyaṃ grahaṇāt pūrvaṃ svarūpeṇaiva saṃsthitam | nirapekṣaṃ svakāryeṣu gṛhyate pratyayāntaraiḥ ||
tenāsya jñāyamānatvaṃ prāmāṇye nopayujyate | viṣayānubhavo hy atra pūrvasmād eva labhyate ||
apramāṇaṃ punaḥ svārthagrāhakaṃ syāt svarūpataḥ | nivṛttis tasya mithyātve nāgṛhīte parair bhavet ||
na hy arthasyātathābhāvaḥ pūrveṇārthas tathātvavat | tatrāpy arthānyathābhāve dhīr yad vā duṣṭakāraṇe ||
tāvataiva ca mithyātvaṃ gṛhyate nānyahetukam | utpattyavasthaṃ caivedaṃ pramāṇam iti mīyate ||
ato yatrāpi mithyātvaṃ parebhyaḥ pratipādyate | tatrāpy etad dvayaṃ vācyaṃ na tu sādharmyamātrakam ||
codanārthānyathābhāvaṃ kurvataś cānumānataḥ | tajjñānenaiva yo bādhaḥ sa kathaṃ vinivāryate ||
tanmithyātvād abādhaś cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam | nānumānād ato 'nyad dhi bādhakaṃ kiñ cid asti te ||
na cānyair agrahe 'rthasya syād abhāvo rasādivat | teṣāṃ jihvādibhir yasmān niyamo grahaṇe 'sti hi ||
taddhiyaivārthabodhaś cet, tādṛgdharme bhaviṣyati | mamāsiddham idaṃ kin tu vedāj jāte 'vabodhane ||
vaktuṃ na dveṣamātreṇa yujyate satyavādinā | dveṣād asammatatvād vā na ca syād apramāṇatā ||
na cātmecchābhyanujñābhyāṃ prāmāṇyam avakalpate | agnidāhādiduḥkhasya na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||
na cābhilāpikaṃ jñānaṃ prāmāṇyenāvadhāryate | tasmād ālokavad vede sarvasādhāraṇe sati ||
naivaṃ vipratipattavyam, bauddhāder vakṣyate 'ntaram | puruṣāśaktitas tatra sāpavādatvasambhavaḥ ||
vedasyāpauruṣeyatve siddhā tv evaṃ pramāṇatā | kartṛmattve tu vedasya samyaṅmithyātvavādibhiḥ ||
kartā guṇāś ca doṣāś ca mahājanaparigrahaḥ | evamādi vinā yuktyā kalpyam, mīmāṃsakaiḥ punaḥ ||
idānīm iva sarvatra dṛṣṭān nādhikam iṣyate | evambhūtasya vedasya jñānotpattiṃ prakurvataḥ ||
svarūpaviparītatvasaṃśayau bhāṣyavāritau | nivārayiṣyate cāpi duṣṭakāraṇakalpanā ||
puruṣābhāvatas tena taddvāreṇāpy aśaṅkitau | tathā satyatathābhāvo buddhyanutpattim āśritaḥ ||
tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ bravītītyevamādinā | yathādṛṣṭārthavāditvaṃ tac cet pratyayitāditi ||
indriyeti tu mūlaṃ ced asyāstītyevam abravīt | draṣṭṛtvasatyavāditve tac cet pratyayitāditi ||
dṛśyamānārthavāditve syād anāptoktisatyatā | evaṃ tv ekāṅgavaikalyāt pratyudāharaṇasthitiḥ ||
ekaikābhāvamātre syād āptatvaindriyakatvayoḥ | apratyayitapakṣe syād aindriyasyāpy asatyatā ||
anindriyatvapakṣe vā satpratyayitabhāṣitam | vyāhatagranthataivaṃ syāt, tasmāt pūrveṇa satyatā ||
pareṇa mūlasadbhāva indriyeṇa tu darśitaḥ | aprāmāṇyanivṛttyarthaṃ doṣābhāvopavarṇanam ||
guṇāt prāmāṇyam ityevaṃ tatpūrvaṃ sunirākṛtam | pūrvatra pratiṣiddhatvān naitat prāmāṇyakāraṇam ||
samuccayārtho vāśabdaḥ pūrvasmin, uttaratra ca | vikalpenobhayor āha pratyudāharaṇe pṛthak ||
śakye 'py asatye mithyātvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satye 'py aśaktike | nānena vacaneneha sarvajñatvanirākriyā ||
vacanād ṛta ityevam apavādo hi saṃśritaḥ | yadi ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ syāt sarvajñaḥ kena vāryate ||
ekena tu pramāṇena sarvajño yena kalpyate | nūnaṃ sa cakṣuṣā sarvān rasādīn pratipadyate ||
yajjātīyaiḥ pramāṇais tu yajjātīyārthadarśanam | bhaved idānīṃ lokasya tathā kālāntare 'py abhūt ||
yatrāpy atiśayo dṛṣṭaḥ sa svārthānatilaṅghanāt | dūrasūkṣmādidṛṣṭau syān na rūpe śrotravṛttitā ||
bhaviṣyati na dṛṣṭaṃ ca pratyakṣasya manāgapi | sāmarthyam, nānumānāder liṅgādirahite kva cit ||
sarvajñakalpanānyais tu vede cāpauruṣeyatā | tulyatā kalpitā yena tenedaṃ sampradhāryatām ||
sarvajño dṛśyate tāvan nedānīm asmadādibhiḥ | nirākaraṇavacchakyā na cāsīd iti kalpanā ||
na cāgamena sarvajñaḥ, tadīye 'nyonyasaṃśrayāt | narāntarapraṇītasya prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
na cāpy evamparo nityaḥ śakyo labdhum ihāgamaḥ | nityaś ced arthavādatvaṃ tatpare syād anityatā ||
āgamasya ca nityatve siddhe tatkalpanā vṛthā | yatas taṃ pratipadyante dharmam eva tato narāḥ ||
yo 'pīndriyārthasambandhaviṣaye satyavāditām | dṛṣṭvā tadvacanatvena śraddheye 'rthe 'pi kalpayet ||
tenāpi pāratantryeṇa bādhitā syāt pramāṇatā | prāmāṇyaṃ cet svayaṃ tasya kāpekṣānyendriyādiṣu ||
yathaivātrendriyādibhyaḥ paricchedāt pramāṇatā | śraddheye 'pi tathaiva syān na svātantryeṇa labhyate ||
yathā ca teṣāṃ satyatvaṃ sidhyaty etena hetunā | tathānyānavabuddhārthaprāmāṇyābhāvasādhanam ||
aśraddheyārthasatyatvaṃ śraddheye cāpy asatyatā | pūrvajñānānuvāditvaṃ dṛṣṭāntavad iheṣyatām ||
api cālaukikārthatve sati puṃvākyahetukam | mithyātvaṃ bauddhavākyānāṃ syād anyonyaṃ sapakṣataḥ ||
dharmādharmātiriktārthe prāmāṇyaṃ ca prasajyate | sāṃkhyādiṣu ca jīvatsu dṛṣṭānto durlabho 'sya ca ||
alaukikārthavācitvaṃ nṛvākyatve satīti ca | parasparam apekṣyaiva bauddhādeḥ syān mṛṣārthatā ||
vaded evaṃ ca yo nāma vādī prathamasaṅgataḥ | tasyāpi hetuḥ syād eṣa bhavantaṃ pratyasaṃśayam ||
buddhādīnām asarvajñam iti satyaṃ vaco mama | maduktatvād yathaivāgnir uṣṇo bhāsvara ity api ||
pratyakṣaṃ ca maduktatvaṃ tvayā sādhyā taduktatā | tena hetur madīyaḥ syāt sandigdhāsiddhatā tava ||
pratyakṣādyavisaṃvādi prameyatvādi yasya ca | sadbhāvavāraṇe śaktaṃ ko nu taṃ kalpayiṣyati ||
na cāpi smṛtyavicchedāt sarvajñaḥ parikalpyate | vigānāt, chinnamūlatvāt, kaiś cid eva parigrahāt ||
sarvajño 'sāv iti hy eva tatkāle tu bubhutsubhiḥ | tajjñānajñeyavijñānarahitair gamyate katham ||
kalpanīyāś ca sarvajñā bhaveyur bahavas tava | ya eva syād asarvajñaḥ sa sarvajñaṃ na budhyate ||
sarvajño 'navabuddhaś ca yenaiva syān na taṃ prati | tadvākyānāṃ pramāṇatvaṃ mūlājñāne 'nyavākyavat ||
rāgādirahite cāsmin nirvyāpāre vyavasthite | deśanānyapraṇītaiva syād ṛte pratyavekṣaṇāt ||
sānnidhyamātratas tasya puṃsaścintāmaṇer iva | niḥsaranti yathākāmaṃ kuḍyādibhyo 'pi deśanāḥ ||
evamādyucyamānaṃ tu śraddadhānasya śobhate | kuḍyādiniḥsṛtatvāc ca nāśvāso deśanāsu naḥ ||
kin nu buddhapraṇītāḥ syuḥ kimu kaiś cid durātmabhiḥ | adṛśyair vipralambhārthaṃ piśācādibhir īritāḥ ||
evaṃ yaiḥ kevalaṃ jñānam indriyādyanapekṣiṇaḥ | sūkṣmātītādiviṣayaṃ jīvasya parikalpitam ||
narte tadāgamāt sidhyen na ca tenāgamo vinā | dṛṣṭānto 'pi na tasyānyo nṛṣu kaś cit pravartate ||
nityāgamāvabodho 'pi pratyākhyeyo 'nayā diśā | na hi tatrāpi visrambho dṛṣṭo 'nena kṛto 'tha vā ||
sarvadā cāpi puruṣāḥ prāyeṇānṛtavādinaḥ | yathādyatve na visrambhas tathātītārthakīrtane ||
svapnādijñānavac cāpi pratyayo 'syāgamārthayoḥ | bhaved iti saśaṅkānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
puruṣātiśayaś ceṣṭaḥ saiva cāgamanityatā | kalpitaṃ smaraṇaṃ cāsya janmāntaranibandhanam ||
grāhyatve cāgamasyaivaṃ dveṣo 'rthagrahaṇe vṛthā | yo hy anuccāritaṃ śabdaṃ gahṇātyarthe 'sya kā kathā ||
pumāṃs tāvat svatantraḥ syād arthagrahaṇavādinām | āgamapratibhāne tu pāratantryaṃ dvayor api ||
anekapuruṣasthatvād ekatraiva ca janmani | grahaṇasmaraṇād vede na svātantryaṃ vihanyate ||
anyathākaraṇe cāsya bahubhyaḥ syān nivāraṇam | ekasya pratibhānaṃ tu kṛtakān na viśiṣyate ||
ataś ca sampradāye ca naikaḥ puruṣa iṣyate | bahavaḥ paratantrāḥ syuḥ sarve hy adyatvavannarāḥ ||
evaṃ ca kalpayantyanye yāvadāgamasiddhaye | tāvan na kalpayaty etat samatvaṃ jaimineḥ paraiḥ ||
na hi dṛṣṭādhikaṃ kiñ cit prāmāṇye tena kalpyate | aprāmāṇyanimitteṣu parasyādṛṣṭakalpanā ||
dṛṣṭaprāmāṇyabādhaś ca nāstikasya prasajyate | utpanne sati vijñāne balād bādhaprakalpanā ||
sādhite puruṣābhāve nirdoṣajñānajanmanaḥ | pratyakṣān nāstikair vācyo viśeṣaś codanādhiyaḥ ||
upadeśo 'nyathā na syād atīndriyanidandhanaḥ | tasya kartrā na ced dṛṣṭaḥ so 'rtha ity arthakalpanā ||
yad vānumānam evedam upadeśitvam ucyate | dṛṣṭārthapūrvatāvyāptam, vyatireko 'sya nanv iti ||
anyathāpy upapannatvaṃ vyāmohād iti kathyate | liṅgasya vyabhicāro vā bālavākyanidarśanāt ||
vedāj jñātvopadiṣṭaṃ ced ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam | vedād apītyanenoktam, manvādeś caitad iṣyate ||
anyathā saṃvidāno 'pi vivakṣaty anyathā yataḥ | tasmād ekāntato nāsti puṃvākyāt taddhiyāṃ gatiḥ ||
bhrāntasyānyavivakṣāyām anyad vākyaṃ ca dṛśyate | yathāvivakṣam apy etat tasmān naiva pravartate ||
vaktṛdhīr āptavākyeṣu gamyate, nyatra viplutiḥ | tenotsargāpavādābhyāṃ vacasaḥ śaktir ucyate ||
padārtharacanāyatto vākyārthapratyayodbhavaḥ | vivakṣāpūrvavijñānavaśāc ca racanākṛtiḥ ||
vivakṣāntarayuktā hi kurvāṇā racanāntaram | āvāpodvāpabhedena dṛśyante 'rtheṣu mānavāḥ ||
tenārthapratyayotpāde śroturjāte 'pi vākyataḥ | jñāto nūnam aneneti vakturjñāne matir bhavet ||
āptoktikāraṇaṃ kañ cid anuyuṅkte naraṃ yadā | tadā ca nirdiśatyāptaṃ sa jānātyetad ityasau ||
tajjñānāntaritatvāc ca śabdās tāvad udāsate | prāmāṇyasthāpanaṃ tu syād vaktṛdhīhetusambhavāt ||
arthe pūrvapratīte 'pi niścayo hi tadāśrayaḥ | tenārthajñānagamyāpi prāmāṇye saiva pūrvabhāk ||
ato 'tra puṃnimittatvād upapannā mṛṣārthatā | na tu syāt tatsvabhāvatvaṃ vede vakturabhāvataḥ ||
tadbuddhyantarayor nāstīty artho 'rthaiś ca pratīyate | ato na jñānapūrvatvam apekṣyaṃ nāyathārthatā ||
apramāṇatvasiddhau vā dṛṣṭānto ya udāhṛtaḥ | buddhādivacanaṃ tasya sādhyenāsaṅgatocyate ||
teṣām api hi yat kāryaṃ pūrvatra pratipāditam | tatra samyaktvam arthe tu vyāpāro naiva vidyate ||
svavyāpārātirikte 'rthe vedasyāpi mṛṣārthatā | pūrvapakṣārthavattvena prasaktā siddhasādhyatā ||
ajñātvaivamabhiprāyaṃ kṛtakākṛtakatvayoḥ | satyamithyātvahetūktimātrajñānāt paro 'bravīt ||
nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭam, nānyatvād ityadūṣaṇam | anyatvād eva dṛṣṭānto na hi pakṣe sapakṣatā ||
tasmād ayam abhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya varṇyate | abhyupetyārthaviṣayaṃ vākyavyāpāram ucyate ||
yadi syād vyavadhāne 'pi vākyārthāpekṣayānṛtam | dṛṣṭānto nṛvaco 'trāpi hetuḥ sādhāraṇo bhavet ||
satyeṣv api hi dṛṣṭaiva pauruṣeyeṣu vākyatā | atīndriye 'pi kiñ cid dhi satyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yadṛcchayā ||
nānyatvād iti cānena paroktād anyatocyate | anyo hy eṣa tadābhāsaḥ, vipakṣaṃ vānyam abravīt ||
yad vānyasmād visaṃvādān mithyātvaṃ tatra na tv iha | viṣayasyāpi cānyatvāt sādhanāsaṅgataiva sā ||
na hy anyasyeti naikasmin mṛṣārthe 'nyamṛṣārthatā | vivakṣāyā mṛṣārthatve na ca vākye mṛṣārthatā ||
śyāmatve puṃstvavac caitat sādhāraṇye nidarśanam | parokter vāpi duṣṭatvād vikalpasamam ucyate ||
yad vā pramāṇam evedaṃ samyaktve 'nyatvam ucyate | dhiruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ ||
codanājanitā buddhiḥ pramāṇaṃ doṣavarjitaiḥ | kāraṇair janyamānatvāl liṅgāptoktyakṣabuddhivat ||
tathānāptāpraṇītoktijanyatvād bādhavarjanāt | deśakālādibhedādau cāptoktipratyayo yathā ||
akartṛkatvasiddhyā ca hetutvaṃ sādhayiṣyate | evamādyavabudhyāyaṃ nānyatvād ity avocata ||
pratyakṣas tv iti dārḍhyaṃ vā prāthamyaṃ vāpi lakṣayet | svarūpataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ mithyātvaṃ pararūpataḥ ||
jñānābhāvaś ca mithyātvaṃ dvayasyāsambhavād yadi | pratyakṣaṃ tatpareṣāṃ ca siddham asyānumānataḥ ||
yathā ca tava mithyātvaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhayed idam | tathā ca bādhakādhīnaṃ mithyātvam api sādhayet ||
dharma ity upasaṃhārye yacchreyaskarabhāṣaṇam | taddharmapadavācyārthanirūpaṇavivakṣayā ||
śreyo hi puruṣaprītiḥ sā dravyaguṇakarmabhiḥ | codanālakṣaṇaiḥ sādhyā tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatā ||
anyat sādhyam adṛṣṭvaiva yāgādīnanuniṣṭhataḥ | dhārmikatvasamākhyānaṃ tadyogād iti gamyate ||
paśvādīni ca dharmasya phalānīti vyavasthitam | citrāgodohanādīnāṃ tāny uktāni phalāni ca ||
tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatvam, dharmāṇīti ca darśanāt | liṅgasaṃkhyāvinirmukto dharmaśabdo nidarśanam ||
antaḥkaraṇavṛttau vā vāsanāyāṃ ca cetasaḥ | pudgaleṣu ca puṇyeṣu nṛguṇe 'pūrvajanmani ||
prayogo dharmaśabdasya na dṛṣṭaḥ, na ca sādhanam | puruṣārthasya te jñātuṃ śakyante codanādibhiḥ ||
na ca vastvantaraṃ śakyam apūrvaṃ svargayāgayoḥ | jñātuṃ sādhanabhūtaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā nāpy ato 'nyathā ||
śrutasādhanasādhyatvatyāgenāśrutakalpanā | prasajyetāsya tādrūpye vyatireke tv arūpatā ||
tasmāt phale pravṛttasya yāgādeḥ śaktimātrakam | utpattau vāpi paśvāder apūrvaṃ na tataḥ pṛthak ||
śaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāvaśabdair viśeṣataḥ | nopākhyāyanta ityevaṃ nāpūrvaṃ dharmaśabdatā ||
purastāc codanāśabdo vidhāv eva vyavasthitaḥ | na ca tallakṣaṇā hiṃsā pratyudāharaṇaṃ katham ||
codanālakṣaṇo yaś ca śyenādir hi gamyate | niṣedhābhāvatas tasya kathaṃ brūyād anarthatā ||
yady api syād vidhispṛṣṭe niṣedho naiva tādṛśaḥ | vijñāyate hy anarthatvaṃ ṣoḍaśigrahaṇādivat ||
codanālakṣaṇaṃ coktvā niṣiddhatvād virudhyate | śyenādāv upadiṣṭe ca hiṃsā hīti na yujyate ||
hiṃsā hi phalam eteṣāṃ bhinnā tebhyaḥ svarūpataḥ | sā hi prāṇaviyogātmā śyenas tatrāsivatpṛthak ||
upadeśābhidhānaṃ ca nāvidheye 'vakalpate | śyenāder avidhāne ca kasyānyasya vidheyatā ||
sarvatrāvasthito nyāyo bhāvanāṃśadvaye vidhiḥ | sa bādhyeta, iha ye cāmī jyotiṣṭomādayo matāḥ ||
dharmatvena na te 'pi syur hiṃsāsādhanakā hi te | na cāvidhīyamānasya phalatatsādhanāṅgatā ||
sādhanatvena vihitaṃ na cāvihitam ucyate | sādhyatvena vidhānaṃ tu naiveṣṭaṃ lokavedayoḥ ||
tenaivamarthaśabdasya prayojanam ihocyate | pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yā śabdaśravaṇena dhīḥ ||
sā codaneti sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hṛdaye sthitam | pravartakagṛhītis tu syād udāharaṇārthatā ||
tātparye hy arthaśabdasya neyaṃ vyākhyopapadyate | arthagrahaṇalabhyaṃ vā tatpravartakabhāṣaṇam ||
dharme pramāṇabhūtāyās tad vā lakṣaṇam uktavān | evaṃ sati vidhibhyaḥ syād vidheyārthāvadhāraṇam ||
niṣedhebhyo niṣedhyānām anarthatvena nirṇayaḥ | tenārthagrahaṇenoktā vidheyasyeha dharmatā ||
niṣedhyānām anarthatvam arthasiddhaṃ na sūtritam | tasmād ubhayam ityatra vidheyapratiṣedhyayoḥ ||
yāgādibrahmahatyādivargayoḥ syān nidarśanam | śyenādīnāṃ vidheyatvādiṣṭasyāpi ca sādhanāt ||
upacārād anarthatvaṃ phaladvāreṇa varṇyate | pratiṣiddhā hi setyatra sphuṭam etat kariṣyate ||
hiṃsā hīti ca yac cāpi brūte nābhicared iti | śyenādīnāṃ svarūpe tu nottaragranthasaṅgatiḥ ||
vihitatvān niṣedhasya pravṛttis teṣu durlabhā | yadā tu codanāśabdo vidhāveva vyavasthitaḥ ||
tadobhayādiko granthaḥ sadhyasādhanasaṃśritaḥ | sādhyasādhanasambandhe vidhinā pratipādite ||
lakṣyamāṇatvam ubhayoḥ, dvividhaṃ ca phalaṃ kratoḥ | svargādi prāpyate tatra pratiṣedhānatikramāt ||
atikrameṇa hiṃsādi, śāstrāntaranirīkṣayā | phalāṃśe bhāvanāyāś ca pratyayo na vidhāyakaḥ ||
vakṣyate, jaiminiś cāha tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇā | tena sāmānyataḥ prāpto vidhinā na nivāritaḥ ||
phalāṃśopanipātinyā hiṃsāyāḥ pratiṣedhakaḥ | anarthaprāptihetutvaṃ bodhyate tatra yady api ||
śyenasvarūpaṃ nānarthas tatphalasya tv anarthatā | parastūbhayam ityādeḥ phalasyāpi vidheyatām ||
bhāvanāntargatatvād vā matvānarthatvam ākṣipat | naivetyetāvatā cāsya vidheyatvanirākriyā ||
kiṃ vidheyam idānīṃ syād āha śyenādayas tv iti | praśnāpākaraṇe cātra tavyo vidhivivakṣayā ||
prayukto na tu sādhye 'rthe, dvaye 'py anupayogataḥ | anarthasyāpi sādhyatvam avidheyasya hīṣyate ||
sādhyatvarahite ceṣṭā vidheye nityam arthatā | śatuś ca lakṣaṇārthatvaṃ teṣāṃ cāpy upadeśanam ||
bruvan sphuṭīkarotīṣṭam upadeśo hi nānyathā | vidhitvamādiśabdāt syād itikartavyatāsv api ||
tasmāt phalāṃśe yā hiṃsā vaidikī sā niṣidhyate | aṃśadvaye tu yā nāma tanniṣedhābhidhāyinām ||
aviśeṣeṇa yacchāstraṃ śirovad iti cottaram | niṣedhenānavaṣṭabdhe viṣaye na hy anarthatā ||
pratyakṣāder aśakyatvāt kalpyate niṣpramāṇikā | na hi hiṃsādyanuṣṭhāne tadānīṃ doṣadarśanam ||
bāhye 'pi vicikitsā tu śāstrādevopajāyate | hiṃsyamānasya duḥkhitvaṃ dṛśyate yan na tāvatā ||
karturduḥkhānumānaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ tadviparyayaḥ | viṣaye 'syāḥ phalaṃ yādṛk pretya kartus tathāvidham ||
hiṃsā kriyāviśeṣatvāt sūte śāstroktadānavat | ya evamāha, tasyāpi gurustrīgamanādibhiḥ ||
surāpānādibhiś cāpi vipakṣair vyabhicāritā | viruddhatā ca, yādṛgdhi dānais tādṛk phalaṃ bhavet ||
vidhigamyaphalāvāptiḥ, aduḥkhātmakatā tathā | na ca yā sampradānasya prītis tādṛk phalaṃ śrutam ||
dātus tena hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyahīnaḥ pratīyate | sampradānaṃ ca dāne te viṣayaḥ karma hiṃsane ||
vaiṣamyam, sampradāne tu pakṣe tv etadviruddhatā | prīyate sampradānaṃ hi devateti mataṃ tava ||
dṛṣṭānte karma dānaṃ cet, tasya kīdṛk phalaṃ bhavet | japahomādidṛṣṭāntāt parapīḍādivarjanāt ||
coditatvasya hetutvād viruddhāvyabhicāritā | vihitapratiṣiddhatve muktvānyan na ca kāraṇam ||
dharmādharmāvabodhasya tenāyuktānumānagīḥ | anugrahāc ca dharmatvaṃ pīḍātaś cāpy adharmatām ||
vadato japasīdhvādipānādau nobhayaṃ bhavet | krośatā hṛdayenāpi gurudārābhigāminām ||
bhūyān dharmaḥ prasajyeta bhūyasī hy upakāritā | anumānapradhānasya pratiṣedhānapekṣiṇaḥ ||
hṛdayakrośanaṃ kasmād dṛṣṭāṃ pīḍām apaśyataḥ | poḍātaś cāpy adharmatvaṃ tathā pīḍām adharmataḥ ||
anyonyāśrayam āpnoti vinā śāstreṇa sādhayan | evamādāv aśāstrajñomleccho nodvijate kva cit ||
tasya nādharmayogaḥ syāt pūrvoktā yadi kalpanā | tasmād anugrahaṃ pīḍāṃ tadabhāvam apāsya ca ||
dharmādharmārthibhir nityaṃ mṛgyau vidhiniṣedhakau | kva cid asyā niṣiddhatvāc chaktiḥ śāstreṇa bodhitā ||
pratyavāyanimittatve vidhinā nāpagacchati | śāstreṇa na hi śaktīnām āvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
vidyamānā hi kathyante śaktayo dravyakarmaṇām | tad eva cedaṃ karmeti śāstram evānudhāvatā ||
hiṃsādīnām adharmatvaṃ kathyate nānumānataḥ | evaṃ ye nipuṇaṃ prāhus tair apy etat parīkṣyatām ||
surāpānādibhiḥ śūdraḥ kiṃ yāti narakaṃ kṛtaiḥ | vaiśyastomena vā kiṃ syād viprarājanyayoḥ phalam ||
pañcamyām iṣṭikaraṇānmadhyāhne cāgnihotrataḥ | tasmād yady ādṛśaṃ karma yatphalotpattiśaktikam ||
śāstreṇa gamyate tasya tādṛśasyaiva tat phalam | hiṃsā cāṃśadvayādanyā yā tasyāḥ pratiṣedhajam ||
pratyavāyārthatājñānam, vidhinānyatra vāryate | jñānam eva ca śaktīnāṃ nāvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
jñāyante śāstratas tāstu kriyābhedavyavasthitāḥ | vyavasthāḥ śaktibhedānāṃ dṛṣṭārtheṣv api karmasu ||
abhinnatve 'pi dṛśyante bhujeḥ svasthātur eṣv api | rūpābhede 'pi hiṃsāder bhedo 'ṅgānaṅgakāritaḥ ||
tathāpy ekaphalatvaṃ cet kriyātvāt sarvasaṅkaraḥ | yajitvādyaviśeṣāc ca citrādiphalatulyatā ||
bhedāt tatra vyavasthā ced ihāpyevaṃ bhaviṣyati | vidhīnāṃ vāpi sarveṣāṃ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ tena nānartho 'taḥ pratīyate | na caiṣu śrūyate 'narthaḥ, niṣedhān na ca kalpyate ||
na ca prakaraṇasthatvāt puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ bhavet | karmopakāraḥ kalpyas tu dṛṣṭo 'dṛṣṭo 'tha vā punaḥ ||
kalpanāvasaras tatra nānarthasyānapekṣaṇāt | kratvarthaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ paśor nārādupakriyā ||
dṛṣṭaiva tv avadānānāṃ niṣpattiḥ kratvapekṣitā | abhicāre 'py upāyasthā hiṃsā nādharma ucyate ||
tasmād anaṅgabhūtāyāṃ hiṃsāyām etad ucyate | uddeśāc ca phalatvena śyenādau na vidhīyate ||
bhāvanāvidhir apy eva phalāṃśād vinivartate | ataḥ svato na dharmatvaṃ śyenāder nāpy adharmatā ||
phalānarthānubandhitvāt taddvāreṇopacaryate | nirākāṅkṣasya caikena śyenasya na phaladvayam ||
tasmāt kriyāntarād eva hiṃsāto 'nartha ucyate | phalato 'pi ca yatkarma nānarthenānubadhyate ||
kevalaprītihetutvāt taddharmatvena hīṣyate | nanu ceṣṭābhyupāyatvāt śyenāder dharmatā bhavet ||
phalaṃ tāvad adharmo 'sya śyenādeḥ sampradhāryate | yadi yeneṣṭasiddhiḥ syād anuṣṭhānānubandhinī ||
tasya dharmatvam ucyeta tataḥ śyenādivarjanam | yadā tu codanāgamyaḥ kāryākāryānapekṣayā ||
dharmaḥ prītinimittaṃ syāt tadā śyene 'pi dharmatā | yadi tv aprītihetur yaḥ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
so 'dharmaś codanārthaḥ syāt tadā śyene 'py adharmatā | yas tu hiṃsātvasādharmyād bāhyavaccodanāsv api ||
vaded anarthahetutvaṃ tasyāpy āgamabādhanam | tam anādṛtya yo brūyād yāgāder apy asau vadet ||
svargādisādhanāśaktiṃ kriyātvād bhojanādivat | gītāmantrārthavādair yā kalpyate 'narthahetutā ||
pratyakṣaśrutibādhyatvāt sānyārthatvena nīyate | śiṣyān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt sūtravaidikavākyayoḥ ||
aśakteś cobhayoḥ sāmyān na sūtreṣv ity anuttaram | prāguktaparisaṃkhyāyāḥ phalam etat prakāśyate ||
sūtreṣu hy anayā yuktyā gatir eṣāpi yujyate | tasmād āvartate sūtram, tantraṃ vā śaktibhedataḥ ||
ekadeśānumānād vā dve sūtre parikalpite | itaretarasāmīpyād etāv eva parasparam ||
kalpyete vākyaśeṣāya nānyāvayavakalpanā | viśiṣṭārthānuvāditvād atha vety api bhāṣite ||
vākyabhedaḥ sa eveti saṃjñātantratvam uttaram | arthaṃ vā pratyupādānāt saṃjñālakṣaṇaśabdayoḥ ||
tantraṃ lakṣaṇaśabdo vā vācyo dharmārthaśabdayoḥ | dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ kathyate yadā ||
vṛttam eva tadārthatvaṃ kimarthaṃ punarucyate | codanālakṣaṇatvasya dharmaṃ prati vidheyatā ||
labhyate 'rthānuvādena saṃśayo hy anyathā bhavet | tathā ca ye 'py anarthasya sādhanatvena kalpitāḥ ||
niṣedhais te 'pi dharmāḥ syuś codanālakṣaṇatvataḥ | tasmād arthāparityāgād ekārthagrahaṇaṃ yathā ||
labhyate vacanavyaktyā sā syād arthānuvādataḥ | viśeṣaṇād vinā caitadarthasāmarthyakāritam ||
kathyate bhāṣyakāreṇa phalaṃ hiṃsādivarjanam ||

§ 3 nimittasūtra NMS

pratijñāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa yady api | vakṣyamāṇā svapakṣasya yuktiḥ pūrvaṃ nidarśitā ||
pratijñāmātram ityetajjaiminer matam ucyate | vṛttikāro 'dhikaṃ vāpi bhūtādi dvāram abravīt ||

§ 4 pratyakṣasūtra PAS

varṇyate sūtrabhedena yena pratyakṣalakṣaṇam | tena sūtrasya sambandho vācyaḥ pūrvapratijñayā ||
lakṣaṇasyābhidhānaṃ tu kenāṃśenopayujyate | kimarthaṃ cānumānāder lakṣaṇaṃ nātra kathyate ||
na tāvad apramāṇatvaṃ teṣāṃ nāpy akṣabuddhiṣu | śakyate 'ntargatir vaktuṃ na ca lakṣaṇatulyatā ||
na cāpi siddhir eṣāṃ syād arthāt pratyakṣalakṣaṇāt | na hi tatpūrvakaṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇam iti niścitam ||
pratyakṣalakṣaṇoktiś ca nānumānādilakṣaṇāt | vinā na sidhyatītyevamarthākṣepo na yujyate ||
tadetatpūrvakatve dhīr na ca tallakṣaṇād bhavet | tadukter vānumānādi kiṃ na syāt tadapūrvakam ||
na ca lakṣaṇabhedasya svarūpe yat tayor api | pratyakṣalakṣaṇād eṣāṃ kathañ cid avadhāraṇā ||
prasiddhatvād avācyatvaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi prasajyate | tenānyaparisaṃkhyārthaṃ sūtraṃ mūḍhena vocyate ||
na tv ekaṃ lakṣayed eṣu buddhipūrvaṃ kathañ cana | sambhavaty ekavākyatve vākyabhedaś ca neṣyate ||
na cāpy etena sūtreṇa pratyakṣaṃ lakṣyate sphuṭam | tadābhāse 'pi tulyatvāt, svapnajñānaikavarjanāt ||
taddhīndriyārthasambandhavyāpāreṇa vinā bhavet | kena cit samprayoge tu bhrāntyādi syān niyogataḥ ||
grāhyeṇānyena vety etat kṛtaṃ naiva viśeṣaṇam | samprayogasya yena syād viśeṣo vakṣyamāṇavat ||
asāmarthya ca matvāsya vṛttikāreṇa lakṣaṇe | tatsamprayoga ityevaṃ pāṭhāntaramṛdāhṛtam ||
tenānyenāpi saṃyoge cakṣurāder yadutthitam | viṣayāntaravijñānaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ prasajyate ||
satsamprayoganirdeśo vyarthaś ced, etad eva hi | pratipādyaṃ parasyāpi lakṣaṇāsiddhir eva ca ||
svapnādīnāṃ nivṛttir vā phalaṃ tasya bhaviṣyati | tasmād vidhyanuvāditvaṃ nānukte lakṣaṇe bhavet ||
tena naiṣā vacovyaktir yatsatīndriyasaṅgame | vijñānaṃ jāyate tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ pratīyatām ||
pratyakṣaṃ yajjane siddhaṃ tasyaivandharmakatvataḥ | vidyamānopalambhatvaṃ tena dharme nimittatā ||
evaṃlakṣaṇatvaṃ ca na svarūpavivakṣayā | evaṃliṅgakam ityetad bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
yato 'sti tatra dharmo 'yaṃ vidyamānopalambhanam | tasmāt tena prasiddhena gamyatām animittatā ||
pratyakṣatvamado hetuḥ śeṣaṃ hetuprasiddhaye | asmād ādau prasiddhatvād yogyartham abhidhīyate ||
prakṛtena ca sambandhaḥ śeṣāprāmāṇyadarśanāt | tadaprāmāṇyasiddhiś ca sambandhāder anīkṣaṇāt ||
śakyam anyāpramāṇatvam iti sūtrair na paṭhyate | na ca paryanuyogo 'tra lakṣaṇānupayogataḥ ||
na ca nyūnātirekādiprasaṅgo lakṣaṇaṃ prati | sarvathā lokasiddhatvād dharmo 'yaṃ tāvad iṣyate ||
tataś ca mṛgatṛṣṇādi na pratyakṣaṃ prasajyate | animittaprasaṅgas tu tasyāpi na nivāryate ||
atītānāgate 'py arthe sūkṣme vyavahite 'pi ca | pratyakṣaṃ yoginām iṣṭaṃ kaiś cin muktātmanām api ||
vidyamānopalambhatvam asiddhaṃ tatra tān prati | bhaviṣyattvasya vā hetor tadgrāhyair vyabhicāritā ||
mā bhūtāmiti tenāha lokasiddhaṃ sad ity ayam | na lokavyatiriktaṃ hi pratyakṣaṃ yoginām api ||
pratyakṣatvena tasyāpi vidyamānopalambhanam | satsamprayogajatvaṃ vāpy asmatpratyakṣavad bhavet ||
teṣām avartamāne 'rthe vā nāmotpadyate matiḥ | pratyakṣaṃ sā tatas tv eva nābhilāṣasmṛtādivat ||
loke cāpy aprasiddhatvāt pratyakṣatvapramāṇataḥ | pratibhāvad dvayāsattvaṃ sad ity etena kathyate ||
laukikī pratibhā yadvat pratyakṣādyanapekṣiṇī | na niścayāya paryāptā tathā syād yoginām api ||
avidyamānasaṃyogāt syāc cet pratyakṣadhīḥ kva cit | bhaviṣyaty api dharme syāc chaktety āha sad ity ayam ||
pratyakṣaḥ prāganuṣṭhānān na dharmo 'nuṣṭhito 'pi vā | phalasādhanarūpeṇa tadānīṃ yena nāsty asau ||
asmatpratyakṣavac cāpi vidyamānopalambhanam | pratyakṣaṃ dhyāyināṃ dharme pratyakṣatvāc ca neṣyate ||
avidyamānasaṃyogāt pratyakṣatvanirākṛtiḥ | yogināṃ kena labhyeta neṣṭaṃ sadgrahaṇaṃ yadi ||
saptamyāpi tu labhyeta sadarthaḥ, kalpanā punaḥ | pareṣāṃ vāraṇīyeti yatno jaimininā kṛtaḥ ||
samyagarthe ca saṃśabdo duṣprayoganivāraṇaḥ | prayoga indriyāṇāṃ ca vyāpāro 'rtheṣu kathyate ||
duṣṭatvāc chuktikāyogo vāryate, rajatekṣaṇāt | evaṃ saty anuvādatvaṃ lakṣaṇasyāpi sambhavet ||
tataś cāprāpyakāritvād yad bauddhaiḥ śrotracakṣuṣoḥ | lakṣaṇāvyāptisiddhyarthaṃ saṃyogo neti kīrtyate ||
prāpyagrahaṇapakṣe hi sāntarāgrahaṇaṃ kila | adhiṣṭānādhikaś cārtho na gṛhyeta tvagādivat ||
vyāpāramātravācitvād aviruddhaṃ tad atra naḥ | yadi vārthārjavasthānaṃ samprayogo 'tra varṇyate ||
yogyatālakṣaṇo vācyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kāryalakṣitaḥ | sāṃkhyādīn vā vinirjitya prāptipakṣo 'tra dūṣyatām ||
tayoś ca prāpyakāritvam indriyatvāt tvagādivat | ke cit tayoḥ śarīrāc ca bahirvṛttiṃ pracakṣate ||
cikitsādiprayogaś ca yo 'dhiṣṭhāne prayujyate | so 'pi tasyaiva saṃskāra ādheyasyopakārakaḥ ||
taddeśaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ sarvavyāptyartha ucyate | cakṣurādyupakāraś ca pādādāv api dṛśyate ||
tasmān naikāntataḥ śakyaṃ saṃskārāt tatra vartanam | bahirvṛttis tayoś ceṣṭā pṛthvagrā santatāpi ca ||
adhiṣṭhānādhikaṃ tena gṛhyate yatra yādṛśam | pṛthutvaṃ vṛttibhāge syād, dūre 'pi grahaṇaṃ tathā ||
dīpaprabhā yathā tasmin vinaśyati vinaśyati | tathā bahirgatāpy eṣā mūlacchedād vinaśyati ||
adhiṣṭhānapidhāne tu saty apy ucchinnayatnayā | tayārtho 'nupanītatvād ātmanā nānubhūyate ||
vicchinna iti buddhiḥ syād adhiṣṭhānam apekṣya ca | śabde tv ādhikyavicchedau bhrāntyaivoktāv asambhavāt ||
puruṣendriyaśabdau ca vyavadhānena kalpitau | puruṣo laukiko vā syād yo vāsmin sādhayiṣyate ||
vikriyā jñānarūpāsya na nityatve virotsyate | buddhijanmeti cāpy āha jāyamānapramāṇatām ||
vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇāṃ hi dṛṣṭo janmātirekataḥ | pramāṇe 'pi tathā mā bhūd iti janma vivakṣyate ||
na hi tat kṣaṇam apy āste, jāyate vāpramātmakam | yenārthagrahaṇe paścād vyāpriyetendriyādivat ||
tena janmaiva viṣaye buddher vyāpāra iṣyate | tad eva ca pramārūpaṃ tadvatī karaṇaṃ ca dhīḥ ||
janma cāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam | tac ca bhūtabhaviṣyattvāt kṛtaṃ buddher viśeṣaṇam ||
yadāpy aulūkyasiddhāntāt samavāyasya janmatā | buddhis tatrendriyādhīnā tena pratyakṣamaśnute ||
pramāṇaphalabhāvaś ca yayeṣṭaṃ parikalpyatām | sarvathāpy animittatvaṃ vidyamānopalambhanāt ||
yadvendriyaṃ pramāṇaṃ syāt tasya vārthena saṅgatiḥ | manaso vendriyair yoga ātmanā sarva eva vā ||
tadā jñānaṃ phalam, tatra vyāpārāc ca pramāṇatā | vyāpāro na yadā teṣāṃ tadā notpadyate phalam ||
na ca sarvātmanākṣeṇa sambandho 'rthasya vidyate | yena sarvārthabodhaḥ syāt tatpramāṇābhidhāyinām ||
prāptimātraṃ hi sambandho nendriyasyābhyupeyate | mā bhūt kāraṇamātreṇa tvacā rūpāvadhāraṇam ||
yathā pramāṇaniṣpattau yogyatvād indriyārthayoḥ | niyatā saṅgatir hetuḥ phale 'py evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
yogasya dvyāśrayatve 'pi bhavatyanyatarāśrayaḥ | vyapadeśaḥ, atha vāpy akṣaṃ tatrāsādhāraṇaṃ bhavet ||
saṃyoge tv ātmamanasoḥ syāc ced viṣayabhinnatā | pramāṇaphalayoḥ, nāsau, arthe hi vyāpṛtaṃ dvayam ||
athāpy āśraya iṣṭas te na yogād viṣayāntaram | ātmasthatvena vijñānaṃ na bhinnaviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||
prakṛṣṭasādhanatvāc ca pratyāsatteḥ sa eva naḥ | karaṇaṃ tena nānyatra kārake syāt pramāṇatā ||
pramāṇe sarvasaṃyoge doṣo naiko 'pi vidyate | pramāṇaṃ tv indriyaṃ yasya tasyaiko viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
pramāṇaphalate buddhyor viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | yadā tadāpi pūrvoktā bhinnārthatvanirākriyā ||
viśeṣaṇe tu boddhavye yadālocanamātrakam | prasūte niścayaṃ paścāt tasya prāmāṇyakalpanā ||
niścayas tu phalaṃ tatra, nāsāv ālocite tadā | tadā naiva pramāṇatvaṃ syād arthānavadhāraṇāt ||
hānādibuddhiphalatā pramāṇaṃ ced viśeṣyadhīḥ | upakārādisaṃsmṛtyā vyavāyaś cet, iyaṃ phalam ||
viṣayaikatvam icchaṃs tu yaḥ pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ vadet | sādhyasādhanayor bhedo laukikas tena bādhitaḥ ||
chedane khadiraprāpte palāśe na cchidā yathā | tathaiva paraśor loke cchidayā saha naikatā ||
bhavate bhedahānena rucitā viṣayaikatā | tattyāgena parebhyas tu bhedo rucim upāgataḥ ||
karaṇatvopacāras tu phale cet kalpyate tvayā | kathañ cid viṣayaikatvaṃ parair vā kiṃ na kalpyate ||
paricchedaphalatvena vṛttasyānantarasya naḥ | pramāṇatvaṃ bhavej jñāne pramāṇe tu paraṃ phalam ||
svasaṃvittiphalatvaṃ tu tanniṣedhān na yujyate | pramāṇe viṣayākāre bhinnārthatvān na yujyate ||
svākāraś ca svasaṃvittiṃ muktvā nānyaḥ pratīyate | prāmāṇyaṃ yasya kalpyeta svasaṃvittiphalaṃ prati ||
svākārasya paricchedo na cākārāntarād vinā | tasyāpy evaṃ tathā ca syān nākārāntaḥ kadā cana ||
na cāsañcetitaḥ sattāṃ svākāraḥ pratipadyate | grāhye ca viṣayākāre grāhako 'nyo na labhyate ||
manasas tv indriyatvena pratyakṣā dhīḥ sukhādiṣu | manasā samprayukto hi tāny ātmā pratipadyate ||
sambaddhaṃ vartamānaṃ ca grahyate cakṣurādinā | sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣo vā grāhyaṃ nāto 'tra kalpyate ||
lakṣaṇaṃ yac ca yair uktaṃ pratyakṣe laukike sati | vidyamānopalambhitvāt sarvasyaivānimittatā ||
nirvikalpakapakṣe tu sutarām animittatā | sādhyasādhanasambandho nāvikalpya hi gṛhyate ||
kathaṃ pratyakṣapūrvatvam anumānādi no bhavet | yadā smṛtyasamarthatvān nirvikalpendriyasya dhīḥ ||
na cāvikalpya liṅgasya liṅgisambandhayos tathā | gṛhītiḥ, upamāne 'pi sādṛśyagrahaṇāt smṛteḥ ||
arthāpattiḥ punaḥ prāyo nānyadṛṣṭe 'rtha iṣyate | pravartate ca yaṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'py arthaḥ savikalpakaḥ ||
yatra cānumitaṃ liṅgaṃ sūryagatyādi liṅgi ca | tatra pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ katham adhyavasīyate ||
pratyakṣāvagate cārthe kutas teṣāṃ pramāṇatā | tair yadā sa pratīyeta tadā nākṣasya gocaraḥ ||
atha kasya cid arthasya jñānāt tatpūrvatā bhavet | tadārthasya bhaviṣyattvaṃ na syād ajñānakāraṇam ||
vartamāne hi kasmiṃś cid vijñāte 'rthe 'kṣabuddhibhiḥ | liṅgād avidyamāno 'pi dharmo gamyeta tais tadā ||
pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca varṇān vede 'pi gṛhyate | prameyam iti so 'pi syāt tatpūrvatvād akāraṇam ||
ke cit tatpūrvakatvaṃ tu hetur naiveti manvate | tatpūrvakatvād yat tāvat prāmāṇyaṃ tadasambhavaḥ ||
pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca, liṅgādyanyatamaṃ dhruvam | pravṛttir anumānāder na ca dharme 'sti tādṛśam ||
anumānānumānāder na cāpy astīha sambhavaḥ | sambandhaliṅgiliṅgānāṃ pūrvasiddher asambhavāt ||
sattā ca nānumānena kasya cit pratipadyate | dharmeṇānyad viśeṣyaṃ cet, pakṣo 'siddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
tasmād adṛṣṭapūrvatvāt kena cid vastunā saha | dharmasya nānumeyatvam asādhāraṇavastuvat ||
adṛṣṭasadṛśatvāc ca svayaṃ cānupalambhanāt | dharmasya nopameyatvam asādhāraṇavad bhavet ||
nanv arthāpattir evaṃ syāj jagadvaicitryadarśanāt | sukhiduḥkhādibhedo hi nādṛṣṭāt kāraṇād ṛte ||
dṛṣṭasya vyabhicāritvāt tadabhāve 'pi sambhavāt | sevāvyayanatulyatve dṛṣṭā ca phalabhinnatā ||
syād evaṃ yadi śakyeta svābhāvikanivāraṇā | karmaśakteś ca vaicitrye hetur anyo bhaved yadi ||
yathā ca phalavaicitrye karmaṇāṃ śaktatā svataḥ | tathā ca citratā loke svabhāvād upapatsyate ||
adharme dharmarūpe vā hy avibhakte phalaṃ prati | kim apy astīti vijñānaṃ narāṇāṃ kvopayujyate ||
kiṃ nu yāgād ito duḥkhaṃ hiṃsādeḥ kiṃ sukhodbhavaḥ | svargaputrādibhedaś ca kīdṛśāt karmabhedataḥ ||
iti yāvad avijñānaṃ tāvan naiva pravartate | pravṛttyaṅgaṃ ca yajjñānaṃ tasya mūlaṃ pratīkṣyate ||
tasmāt siddhe 'pi sāmānye viśeṣo nāgamād ṛte | viśeṣasya tu jijñāsā sūtrakāreṇa sūtritā ||
gamyamāne viśeṣe ca tadantarbhāvakāritaḥ | sāmānyapratyayo 'pi syāc chāstrād evety akāraṇam ||
yathārthāpattir evaṃ ca nānumānopameṣyate | śāstraṃ cet tadapekṣeta tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||
pratyakṣāgrahaṇaṃ yat tu liṅgāder avikalpanāt | tan na, iṣṭatvād vikalpasyāpy artharūpopakāriṇaḥ ||
asti hy ālocanā jñānaṃ prathamaṃ nirvikapakam | bālamūkādivijñānasadṛśaṃ śuddhavastujam ||
na viśeṣo na sāmānyaṃ tadānīmanubhūyate | tayor ādhārabhūtā tu, vyaktir evāvasīyate ||
mahāsāmānyam anyais tu dravyaṃ sad iti cocyate | sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca pratyakṣasyaivam āśritam ||
viśeṣās tu pratīyante savikalpakabuddhibhiḥ | te ca ke cit pratidravyaṃ ke cid bahuṣu saṃśritāḥ ||
tān akalpayad utpannaṃ vyāvṛttānugatātmanā | gavyaśve copajātaṃ tu pratyakṣaṃ na viśiṣyate ||
tad ayuktam, pratidravyaṃ bhinnarūpopalambhanāt | na hy ākhyātum aśakyatvād bhedo nāstīti gamyate ||
nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi dvyātmakasyāpi vastunaḥ | grahaṇam, lakṣaṇākhyeyaṃ jñātrā śuddhaṃ tu gṛhyate ||
na cāsādhāraṇatvena paravyāvṛttyakalpanāt | viśeṣānugamākḷpteḥ sāmānyam iti nāpi tat ||
tataḥ paraṃ punarvastudharmair jātyādibhir yayā | buddhyāvasīyate sāpi pratyakṣatvena sammatā ||
karaṇaṃ cendriyaṃ buddher na tatra jñānam āhitam | tataḥ smṛtyasamarthatvād vikalpo 'to na vāryate ||
ātmany eva sthitaṃ jñānam, sa hi boddhātra gamyate | smaraṇe cāsya sāmarthyaṃ sandhānādau ca vidyate ||
tenendriyārthasambandhe vicyamāne smarann api | vikalpayan svadharmeṇa vastu pratyakṣavān naraḥ ||
tac caitadindriyādhīnam iti tair vyapadiśyate | tadasambandhajātaṃ tu naiva pratyakṣam iṣyate ||
punaḥ punarvikalpe 'pi satī jātiḥ pratīyate | tatsambandhānusāreṇa sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iṣyate ||
na hi praviṣṭamātrāṇām uṣṇād garbhagṛhādiṣu | arthā na pratibhāntīti gṛhyante nendriyaiḥ punaḥ ||
yathā tv ābhāsamātreṇa pūrvaṃ jñātvā svarūpataḥ | paścāt tatrāvabudhyante tathā jātyādidharmataḥ ||
yadi tv ālocya saṃmīlya netre kaś cid vikalpayet | na syāt pratyakṣatā tasya sambandhānanusārataḥ ||
asambaddhavikalpe 'pi tulyam ātmādi kāraṇam | tenāsādhāraṇatvaṃ syād atrākṣasyaiva kalpane ||
nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi nākṣaṃ kevalakāraṇam | tatpāramparyajāte vā rūḍhiḥ syāt paṅkajādivat ||
animittaiva vā rūḍhiḥ sutarāṃ savikalpakam | pratyakṣaṃ sammataṃ loke na tathā nirvikalpakam ||
vṛddhaprayogagamyāś ca śabdārthāḥ sarva eva naḥ | tena yatra prayukto 'yaṃ na tasmād apanīyate ||
siddhānugamamātraṃ hi kartuṃ yuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ | na sarvalokasiddhasya lakṣaṇena nivartanam ||
kalpanāyāḥ svasaṃvittāv indriyādhīnatā katham | manas tatrendriyaṃ cet syād gotvādāv api tatsamam ||
svasaṃvittau tad iṣṭaṃ cet, loko na hy evam icchati | tasmād rūḍhatvam eṣṭavyaṃ pāribhāṣikatāpi vā ||
manasas tv indriyatvena sudhaduḥkhādibuddhiṣu | yathā pratyakṣataivaṃ nas tadadhīnā bhaviṣyati ||
tadadhīnatvasāmye 'pi kalpanāpoḍhaśabdanāt | pratyakṣaṃ kiñ cid eveṣṭaṃ yathā tatra tathaiva naḥ ||
liṅgādyabhāvataś cāpi nānumānādidhīr iyam | bādhakapratyayāsattvān nāprāmāṇyaṃ ca yujyate ||
na ca parvamadṛṣṭatvāt smṛtitvam upapadyate | tasmāt pratyakṣam evedam, vyavahāras tathaiva ca ||
jātyādyarthāntaraṃ yasmād atadrūpe 'pi vastuni | bhavaty adhyasya dhīs tasmān mṛgatṛṣṇādibhiḥ samā ||
naitadaśvādibuddhīnām adhyāropādyasambhavāt | sthitaṃ naiva hi jātyādeḥ paratvaṃ vyaktito hi naḥ ||
yadi hy ekāntato bhinnaṃ viśeṣyāt syād viśeṣaṇam | svānurūpāṃ sadā buddhiṃ viśeṣye janayet katham ||
sphaṭikādau tu lākṣādisvarūpā yā matir bhavet | avyutpannasya sā mithyā vyutpannānāṃ hi bhedadhīḥ ||
na tu jātyādinirmuktaṃ vastu dṛṣṭaṃ kadā cana | tadvimokena vā tāni lākṣādisphaṭikādivat ||
tatrāpi cen na dṛśyeta bhedaḥ kaiś cit kadā cana | raktādibuddhisamyaktvaṃ vinivāryeta kena vā ||
na cāpy ayutasiddhānāṃ sambandhitvena kalpanā | nāniṣpannasya sambandhaḥ, niṣpattau yutasiddhatā ||
tathā ca sati sambandhe hetuḥ kaś cin na vidyate | tasmāc cāpi na sambandhaḥ padārthānāṃ pratīyate ||
samavāyaviyogāc ca viśleṣaḥ syāt parasparam | tatkḷptāvavyavasthā syāt tasya tasyānyasaṅgateḥ ||
atha tasyātmarūpatvān nānyasambandhakalpanā | abhedāt samavāyo 'stu svarūpaṃ dharmadharmiṇoḥ ||
na hi sa vyatiriktaḥ san sambandhaṃ pratipadyate | tasmiṃs tābhyām abhinne tu na nānātvaṃ tayor bhavet ||
nanu dharmātirekeṇa dharmiṇo 'nupalambhanāt | tatsaṅghamātra evāyaṃ gavādiḥ syād vanādivat ||
āvirbhāvatirobhāvadharmakeṣv anuyāyi yat | taddharmi yatra vā jñānaṃ prāgdharmagrahaṇād bhavet ||
ato jātyādirūpeṇa dharmi yad gṛhyate naraiḥ | pārarūpyaṃ na tasyāstīty aprāmāṇyaṃ na yujyate ||
yasyāpi vyatirekaḥ syād dharmebhyo dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭaḥ | nityaṃ tasyāpi tādrūpyān na mithyātvaṃ prasajyate ||
yo hy asadrūpasaṃvedyaḥ saṃvedyetān yathā punaḥ | sa mithyā na tu tenaiva yo nityam avagamyate ||
na cānekendriyagrāhyaṃ bhinnatāṃ pratipadyate | mā bhūd bhinnaśarīrasthagrāhyatvād bhinnarūpatā ||
jātyabhedād abhedaś cet, indriyatvena tatsamam | tulyabuddher ato bhinnā na sattendriyabhedataḥ ||
buddhibhedāc ca naikatvaṃ rūpādīnāṃ prasajyate | ekānekatvam iṣṭaṃ vā sattārūpādirūpataḥ ||
kva cic ca saṅkarān nākṣam ekam ity avasīyate | dārḍhyadaurbalyabhedena vyavasthāpi yataḥ kva cit ||
yathā hi manasaḥ sārdhaṃ rūpādau cakṣurādinā | pravṛttiḥ sukhaduḥkhādau kevalasyaiva dṛśyate ||
na kva cit saṅkarābhāvāt sarvatraiva nivartate | kva cic ca saṅkaraṃ dṛṣṭvā saṅkaro 'nyatra kalpyate ||
śrotrāder upaghāte 'pi śabdādismṛtidarśanāt | vartamānasya cājñānād vyavasthā sampratīyate ||
ekaṃ yadi bhaved akṣaṃ sarvair gṛhyeta vā na vā | kalpyate śaktibhedaś cet, śaktir evendriyaṃ bhavet ||
śṛṇuyād badhiraḥ śabdaṃ saṅkare cakṣurādinā | manaso vā svatantratve vartamānārthabuddhiṣu ||
na smared badhiraḥ śabdaṃ śrotraṃ cet smṛtikāraṇam | smṛtivad vā bhaved asya vartamānārthadhīr api ||
smṛtiś ca na bhavet paścād gṛhṇīyāt tan na cen manaḥ | śrotragrahaṇavelāyām, na cāsarvā smṛtir bhavet ||
bodhātmakatayā puṃsaḥ sarvatra grahaṇaṃ bhavet | yugapadviṣaye 'py asya karaṇāpekṣitā na cet ||
tasmāj jñānānusāreṇa vyavasthāsaṅkarau kva cit | grāhyagrāhakaśaktibhyaḥ kāryadvāreṇa kalpitau ||
cakṣūrūpādibhedas tu pañcadhaiva vyavasthitaḥ | tena nīlādibhede 'pi nendriyānantyakalpanā ||
tasmāt pañcabhir apy akṣair bodhaḥ sattāguṇatvayoḥ | dravyamūrtau punardvābhyāṃ rūpādāv ekaśaḥ sthitaḥ ||
nanu jātyādirūpe 'pi śabdābhedopacārataḥ | pravartamānā mithya syād buddhī rūpeṣu buddhivat ||
na śabdābhedarūpeṇa buddhir artheṣu jāyate | prāk śabdād yādṛśī buddhiḥ śabdād api hi tādṛśī ||
nanu gotvādirūpeṇa gavākārādibuddhayaḥ | na prāk śabdārthasambandhajñānāt santi kadā cana ||
jātyādes tatsvarūpaṃ ced aśabdajño 'pi lakṣayet | anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śabdarūpatvaniścayaḥ ||
yathā rūpādayo bhinnāḥ prāk śabdāt svātmanaiva tu | gamyante tadvad evaitat saṃjñitvaṃ kevalaṃ param ||
na cāvikalpitaḥ śabdād iti vācyo na gṛhyate | tenāgṛhītaśabdo 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate ||
śrutisaṃsparśabodhe 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate | vivekād arthaśabdānāṃ cakṣuḥ śrotradhiyā kṛtāt ||
anantadharmake dharmiṇy ekadharmāvadhāraṇe | śabdo 'bhyupāyamātraṃ syān nātmādhyāropakāraṇam ||
na copeye 'bhyupāyasya rūpādhyāsaḥ prasajyate | na hi dīpendriyādīnāṃ rūpādhyāropa iṣyate ||
nityaṃ yadi ca gotvādi śabdarūpeṇa gṛhyate | rūpāntaraṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ ced bhedādhyāsau kuto nvimau ||
yady abhedo na mithyātvam, bhedaś cet syāt svarūpataḥ | nādhyāropaprasaṅgaḥ syād bhrāntyā tv adhyāsakalpanā ||
śabdenaiva ca nirdeśo gṛhīte 'rthe 'vakalpate | gaur ity eva ca nirdeśo vācyatadbuddhivādinām ||
nirdeśatulyatāyāṃ ca śrotrā vaktṛsvarūpatā | śabdajñānaprameyeṣu vijñānasyāvasīyate ||
bhrāntihetusamānatve 'py upāyatvānmatiśrutī | manyate 'rthe samadhyaste nārthādhyāsaṃ tayoḥ punaḥ ||
gotve sāsnādimadrūpāṅgādirūpābhidhāyake | nirākārobhayajñāne saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ ||
yadi cābhedarūpeṇa śabdenārthaḥ pratīyate | ekarūpatvam akṣādau devanādeḥ prasajyate ||
syād anakṣanivṛtyā cet, na prāk śabdāt pratīyate | gavādiṣv api tulyaṃ cet, nekarūpasya darśanāt ||
traye bibhītakādīnāṃ naikadharmānvayo 'sti hi | śabdaḥ sādhāraṇas teṣāṃ jātiśabdād vilakṣaṇaḥ ||
parasparavibhinnaṃ tu jñāyate 'trākṛtitrayam | tadadhyāse na yujyeta tadrūpasyāvibhāgataḥ ||
bhinnāḥ syur akṣaśabdāś cet, nārthe saṃśayadarśanāt | na sāmānyād ṛte sa syād, rūpābhedaś ca gamyate ||
bhavatyādau ca bhinne 'pi nāmākhyātatvasaṃjñayā | rūpaikatvena cādhyāse tulyārthatvaṃ prasajyate ||
śabdaniṣpattyabhedāc ca tiṅantārthasya sādhyatā | katham, kathaṃ ca mūrtārtho vācake mūrtivarjite ||
gavāśvaśuklaśabdāder vācyarūpānapekṣaṇe | vācakatvavyavasthānaṃ kathaṃ jātiguṇādiṣu ||
vṛkṣaplakṣādiśabdānāṃ tulye bhede ghaṭādibhiḥ | viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ katham arthānapekṣayā ||
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na syad vācakabuddhivat | ekatra copasaṃhāro na buddhyor nirvikalpake ||
vastumātre sa ced evaṃ sarveṣām ekavācyatā | bhaved gavādiśabdānāṃ sarvair vastu hi gamyate ||
na cāsādhāraṇe bhede nīlotpalam itīṣyate | na hi śabdapravṛttiḥ syād anyatrānyatra ceṣyate ||
na ca nīlotpalaṃ nāma vastvekaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate | śabdārthayor yato bhedo gamyate 'vayavānugaḥ ||
śabdadvayasya cādhyāsaḥ paryāyeṣv api dṛśyate | ekādhikaraṇās tena syus te nīlotpalādivat ||
na cānavagate pūrvaṃ padam arthe prayujyate | tatra sambandhavelāyāṃ kīdṛśo 'rthaḥ pratīyate ||
tadānīṃ nārtharūpe hi śabdarūpasya sambhavaḥ | na cāsādhāraṇāṃśena sambandhānugamaḥ kva cit ||
tatra pūrvānapekṣatve yadyātmādhyāsaśaktatā | śabdasya prathame 'pi syāc chravaṇe 'dhyastarūpatā ||
mama vācyānabhijñatvān na bhavet smaraṇaṃ tataḥ | bhavatas tv artharūpasya vācakeṣv api darśanāt ||
yathā tv ajñātaśabdānāṃ vācye taddhīr na jāyate | tathaivājñātavācyānām upalabdhe 'pi vācake ||
tasmān nātīva vācyānāṃ vācakādhīnatā bhavet | smārakatvāc ca teṣv eva pāratantryaṃ pratīyate ||
tena sambandhavelāyām arthātmā yo 'vasīyate | śabdād api sa eveti nārtharūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yāṃ śabdaḥ kurute matim | tādātmyaṃ tasya śabdasya na kathañ cit pratīyate ||
karahastādiśabdebhyaḥ śabdarūpasya bhedataḥ | bhinno 'rthaḥ sampratīyeta tadadhyāropakalpane ||
ātmādhyāsas tu sādṛśyād uparāgāc ca dṛśyate | na tāvad arthasādṛśyaṃ śabdasyeha pratīyate ||
na cānurāgaḥ śabdena bhinnadeśasya yujyate | dūrasthapratibimbaṃ ca nārūpasya pratīyate ||
śabdasarvagatatvena yadyarthaprāptir ucyate | sarvārthānāṃ bhavec chabdaiḥ sarvair evānurañjanam ||
na ca bhinnendriyagrāhyaṃ kiñ cid asty anurāgakṛt | na hi lākṣānurakte 'pi sphaṭike dhīs tvagādibhiḥ ||
anumānāgamau mithyā syātāmadhyāsakalpane | nirūpaṇasya mithyātvāt sarvābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
tathās tv iti yadi brūyāt, mithyā svavacane sati | katham evaṃ vaded artho nānṛtād dhi pratīyate ||
śūnyavādottarāccāpi yathārthaṃ buddhiśabdayoḥ | pravṛttir na tu tat tantram artharūpaṃ kadā cana ||
tasmāt prāg api ye śabdād bhirnnaikatvādibuddhibhiḥ | gṛhyante sarvadā teṣāṃ paramārthastitā bhavet ||
śabdābhyupāyake 'py arthe tadabhāve ca yady api | arthabuddhir na jāyeta nārthe rūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
cakṣurāder abhāve hi rūpādyātmā na gṛhyate | svarūpanāśo rūpādes tāvanmātreṇa neṣyate ||
sambandhasya ca nityatvān nārthasya syād arūpatā | yugapanna hi sarveṣām anyākārārthavedanam ||
tadākāre 'pi tadvac ced, dvaye sati parīkṣyatām | kiṃ nv arthasyātathābhāvo grahītuḥ kiṃ nv aśaktatā ||
sadasadbhāvayor arthe virodhitvād asambhavaḥ | grahītṛbhedāc chaktatvam aśaktatvaṃ ca yujyate ||
yathāndhānandhayoḥ pārśve rūpasyety abhidhāsyate | tenārthe dhvanyupāyasya tadhīrnānyasya jāyate ||
devadattādiśabde tu sambandhādyatvadarśanāt | arthasyānityatāyāṃ ca tādrūpyasyāpy anityatā ||
tatrāpy autpattikī śaktis tadrūpapratyayaṃ prati | grāhyagrāhakayor iṣṭā niyogasya tv anityatā ||
tatra sarvair atādrūpyaṃ prāṅniyogāt pratīyate | teneṣṭam eva mithyātvaṃ kaiś cid adhyāsakalpane ||
yadā tu yādṛśaḥ piṇḍaḥ pūrvaṃ śabdāt pratīyate | tādṛśasmaraṇe hetuḥ śabdas tatra yathārthatā ||
niyogāt parato vāpi śabdena vyajyatām iyam | tadgrāhyaśaktir arthasya, pārarūpyaṃ na tāvatā ||
sarvākāraparicchedyaśakte 'rthe vācake 'pi vā | sarvākārārthavijñānasamarthe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ||
tatra śabdārthasambandhaṃ pramātuḥ smarato 'pi yā | buddhiḥ pūrvagṛhītārthasandhānād upajāyate ||
cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣṭe 'rthe nāpratyakṣam asau bhavet | viviktā eva te 'py arthāḥ smṛtipratyakṣagocarāḥ ||
smaryete śabdasambandhau mā bhūt pratyakṣatā tayoḥ | tadapratyakṣabhāvena na tv arthasyāpi vāryate ||
gṛhītam api gotvādi smṛtispṛṣṭaṃ ca yady api | tathāpi vyatirekeṇa pūrvabodhāt pratīyate ||
vyaktikālādibhedena tatrāsty avasaro miteḥ | yaḥ pūrvāvagato 'ṃśo 'tra sa na nāma pramīyate ||
idānīn tanam astitvaṃ na hi pūrvadhiyā gatam | na hi smaraṇato yatprāk tat pratyakṣam itīdṛśam ||
vacanaṃ rājakīyaṃ vā vaidikaṃ vāpi vidyate | na cāpi smaraṇāt paścād indriyasya pravartanam ||
vāryate kena cin nātastat tadānīṃ praduṣyati | tenendriyārthasambandhāt prāgūrdhvaṃ vāpi yatsmṛteḥ ||
vijñānaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iti gamyatām | vimanaskā yadā ke cit sambaddham api cendriyaiḥ ||
na budhyante tathā cānye sādṛśyādivimohitāḥ | tatra yo 'rthaṃ vivekena kauśalāt sadṛśeṣv api ||
sūkṣmaṃ vāpi prapadyeta tasya bhrāntirna tāvatā | yathā ṣaḍjādibhedena gāne laukikavaidike ||
vivekenāvagacchanti yeṣāṃ tatsaṃskṛtā matiḥ | gānamātraṃ vijānanti tatrānadhikṛtās tu ye ||
tadajñānān na mithyātvaṃ vaktuṃ śakyaṃ vivekinām | te hi ṣaḍjādiśabdebhyo vināpy eṣaṃ viviktatām ||
yathāvadadhigacchanti, tadvad gotvādivas tv api | saṅkīrṇam arthamātraṃ tu budhyante 'bhyāsavarjitāḥ ||
vivekaṃ pratipadyante ye śabdasmṛtisaṃskṛtāḥ | yathā rūpādimatyarthe yasyaivāsti yadindriyam ||
sa tanmātraṃ gṛhītvānyan na gṛhṇātyanumānataḥ | tathā vivekahetūnāṃ yadā yaṃ pratipadyate ||
tadupeye tadā jñānaṃ vartate tadanugrahāt | tena yāvat pramātāṇāṃ vivekopāyadarśanam ||
na syāt tāvad bhavet teṣāṃ vijñānaṃ nirvikalpakam | tasmād yatra prakalpyeta vastu vastvantarātmanā ||
pramāṇābhāsatā tatra na svadharmavikalpane | pratyakṣatvam ataḥ siddhaṃ sāmānyasya tathaiva ca ||
sambandhasyeti tat pūrvam anumānādi jāyate | sarvaṃ cāpy anumānādi pratyakṣe nirvikalpake ||
na pravartata ity etadanumāne 'bhidhāsyate | nanv evaṃ sati yāpy agner dūrād apy auṣṇyakalpanā ||
sāpi pratyakṣam eva syād yathā gotvādibuddhayaḥ | pratyāsannataraṃ gotvaṃ pratyakṣatvena sammatam ||
vijñānaṃ nānyad astīti pratyakṣam idam eva naḥ | tatrāpy akṣair asambandhaṃ manvānasyopajāyate ||
yadā buddhiḥ, tadā naiva pratyakṣatvena kalpyate | sparśanena tu sambandhe pratyakṣatvena jāyate ||
tasmād yadindriyaṃ yasya grāhakatvena kalpitam | tenaiva sati sambandhe pratyakṣaṃ nānyathā bhavet ||
evaṃ samāne 'pi vikalpamārge yatrākṣasambandhaphalānusāraḥ | pratyakṣatā tasya tathā ca loke vināpyado lakṣaṇataḥ prasiddham ||

§ 5,1 vṛttikāragrantha VKG

pratyakṣādau niṣiddhe 'pi nanu lokaprasiddhitaḥ | dharmādharmau pramāsyete brāhmaṇādivivekavat ||
dhārmikādhārmikatvābhyāṃ pīḍānugrahakāriṇau | prasiddhau hi, tathā cāha pārāśaryo 'tra vastuni ||
idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ pāpam ity etasmin padadvaye | ācaṇḍālaṃ manuṣyāṇām alpaṃ śāstraprayojanam ||
nirmūlāsambhavād atra pramāṇaiḥ saiva mṛgyate | kutaḥ punaḥ pravṛtteti, pratyakṣādi tu vāritam ||
na caitāni parityajya pṛthag loke pramāṇatā | saṃsāramocakādeś ca hiṃsā puṇyatvasammatā ||
na paścāt puṇyam icchanti ke cid evaṃ vigānataḥ | mlecchāryāṇāṃ prasiddhatvaṃ na dharmasyopapadyate ||
na cāryāṇāṃ viśeṣo 'sti yāvacchāstram anāśritam | tanmūlārthaprasiddhis tu tatprāmāṇye sthite bhavet ||
tasmād abhāvaktrasthau dharmādarmau na śaknuyāt | codanā cet samuddhartuṃ grastau tenaiva paśyatām ||
upadeśo hi bhavati jñānaṃ tasyeti yojyate | jñāyate yena tajjñānam ekādhikaraṇatvataḥ ||
autpattikagirā doṣaḥ kāraṇasya nivāryate | abādho 'nyatirekeṇa, svatas tena pramāṇatā ||
sarvasyānupalabdhe 'rthe prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtir anyathā | codanā copadeśaś ca vidhiś caikārthavācinaḥ ||
vākyāntare samarthe 'pi kimarthaṃ vidhir āśritaḥ | sādhyasādhanasambandhaḥ sarvākhyāteṣu vidyate ||
sarvavākyeṣu cākhyātaṃ tenākāṅkṣānivartanāt | pravṛttisiddhir icchātaḥ, pratiṣedhāt tu varjanam ||
vidhāvanāśrite sādhyaḥ puruṣārtho na labhyate | śrutasvargādibādhena dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatāṃ vrajet ||
vidhau tu tam atikramya svargādeḥ sādhyateṣyate | tatsādhanasya dharmatvam evaṃ sati ca labhyate ||
svapratyayāntarāpekṣā syād anāptanaroktiṣu | āptoktiṣu narāpekṣā nobhayaṃ codanāsu naḥ ||

§ 5.2

ādiśabdo makārāntaḥ, luki kleśena saṅgatiḥ | nañadhyāhriyate sūtre, saṅkarāt paricodanā ||
pramāṇalakṣaṇājñānād vyabhicārāt parīkṣaṇam | naitat pratyakṣam ityevamaparīkṣopasaṃhṛtā ||
tatrānyasyāyathārthatvaṃ pratyakṣe tu yathārthatā | yadābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ tatsaṃyoge tad iṣyate ||
sampūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hy etat, tatsator vyatyayaḥ kṛtaḥ | śobhanārthas tu sacchabdaḥ, yad vākhyāhārakalpanā ||
arthāpattyetareṣāṃ ca pratyakṣābhāsalakṣaṇam | bādhakajñānalābho hi pūrvābādhe na sambhavet ||
sa cāstīti, avabodhatve sati nānyonyasaṃśrayam | na cānāgatabādhe ca pūrveṇātmā hi labhyate ||
nimittadoṣabodhena paścād yatrāpy abādhanam | bhavaty eva hi tatrāpi narāntaraviparyayaḥ ||
sarveṣāṃ sarvadā yatra dhīḥ syāt tatra na bādhanam | na hi kāraṇaduṣṭatvabuddhis tatra balīyasī ||
jātyādiṣu yadā jātā buddhiḥ paścād asambhavāt | nāśyate yuktibhis tatra vyaktam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||
svataḥ prāmāṇyataś cātra nirṇayo 'stitvabodhanāt | tadrūpapratyayotpattes tadasadvādinām api ||

§ 5,3 nirālambanavāda NAV

pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve puṇyapāpādi tatphalam | vidhyarthavādamantrārthanāmadheyādikalpanā ||
sarveṣu lakṣaṇeṣv evaṃ svapramāṇagaṇaiḥ sthitiḥ | vacanavyaktibhedena pūrvasiddhāntapakṣatā ||
karmabhyaḥ phalasambandhaḥ pāralaukyaihalaukike | sarvam ityādy ayuktaṃ syād arthaśūnyāsu buddhiṣu ||
tasmād dharmārthibhiḥ pūrvaṃ pramāṇair lokasammataiḥ | arthasya sadasadbhāve yatnaḥ kāryaḥ kriyāṃ prati ||
yadā saṃvṛtisatyena sarvam etat prakalpyate | jñānamātre 'pi kasmād vo vṛthāgraho 'rthakalpane ||
saṃvṛter na tu satyatvaṃ satyabhedaḥ kuto 'nvayam | satyā cet saṃvṛtiḥ keyaṃ mṛṣā cet satyatā katham ||
satyatvaṃ na ca sāmānyaṃ mṛṣārthaparamārthayoḥ | virodhāt, na hi vṛkṣatvaṃ sāmānyaṃ vṛkṣasiṃhayoḥ ||
tulyārthatve 'pi tenaiṣāṃ mithyāsaṃvṛtiśabdayoḥ | vañcanārtha upanyāso lālāvaktrāsavādivat ||
nāstikyaparihārārthaṃ saṃvṛtiḥ, kalpaneti ca | kalpanāpi tv abhinnasya naiva nirvastuke bhavet ||
tasmād yan nāsti nāsty eva, yat tv asti paramārthataḥ | tat satyam anyanmithyeti, na satyadvayakalpanā ||
svapnādibhogavac cāpi yopabhogatvakalpanā | tannivṛttyartham eveha paramārthe pravartate ||
na hi svapnasukhādyarthaṃ dharme kaś cit pravartate | yādṛcchikatvāt svapnasya tūṣṇīmāsyeta paṇḍitaiḥ ||
paramārthaphalāvāptim icchadbhis tena yatnataḥ | pratipattir vidhātavyā yuktibhir bāhyavastuṣu ||
tatrārthaśūnyaṃ vijñānaṃ yogācārāḥ samāśritāḥ | tasyāpy abhāvam icchanti ye mādhyamikavādinaḥ ||
tatra bāhyārthaśūnyatvaṃ tulyaṃ tāvad dvayor api | nivṛttyāsya tato jñāne tadvat saṃvṛtikalpanā ||
tasmāt sādhāraṇatvena tanmūlatvena cāpy ayam | bāhyārthasadasadbhāve yatno bhāṣyakṛtā kṛtāḥ ||
bāhyārthāpahnave 'dvaitam ekārthasya parīkṣaṇāt | pramāṇam āśritaś caikas tatrāstāṃ yaḥ prameyataḥ ||
pramāṇasthas tu mūlatvād ihedānīṃ parīkṣyate | prastutaḥ sa dvidhā cātra prathamaṃ tv anumānataḥ ||
pratyakṣabādhane cokte paścāt tacchaktyavekṣaṇāt | tatrānumānamāhedaṃ nanv iti, asya ca saṅgatiḥ ||
tatsamprayogajaṃ nāma pratyakṣam iti bhāṣitam | tatrendriyārthasambandhabhedo na paramārthataḥ ||
kalpitaḥ samprayogas tu svapnādāv api vidyate | tadatadyogajanyasya vibhāgas tena durlabhaḥ ||
mithyātvaṃ yad dvidhaivoktaṃ nāyathety atra cocyate | sarvasyaiva ca mithyātve kiṃ viśiṣyābhidhīyate ||
stambhādipratyayo mithyā pratyayatvāt tathā hi yaḥ | pratyayaḥ sa mṛṣā dṛṣṭaḥ svapnādipratyayo yathā ||
siddhasādhanabhāvo 'ṃśe dṛṣṭāntābhāva eva ca | mā bhūtām evaśabdaś ca vyartho 'śeṣaprasādhane ||
sarva eveti tenātra jāgradbuddhiparigrahaḥ | svāṃśābhyupagamāc cāpi bāhyagrāhyanivāraṇam ||
pratyayasyeti sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanam | hetuś copanayenātra jāgrato 'pīti darśataḥ ||
vipakṣābhāvataś cātra vyatireko na kathyate | sāmānyasya ca hetutvāt kasmāt pakṣaikadeśatā ||
jāgrajjñāne viśeṣo 'yaṃ yataḥ supariniścayaḥ | bāhyālambanasambandho na prasiddhaḥ paraṃ prati ||
tasmād yad bhāṣyakāreṇa dattam uttaram atra tu | vikalpasamatā vā syād vaidharmyasamatāpi vā ||
dṛṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣasya jātyuktiḥ kaiś cid āśritā | pratijñādoṣam evāhuḥ ke cit pratyakṣabādhanam ||
śakṣyāmo yadi vispaṣṭaṃ svāṃśagrāhyanivāraṇam | tadā te śuddha eva syāt pakṣo grāhyanivāraṇaḥ ||
pratyakṣādeś ca viṣayo bāhya evāvatiṣṭhate | tanniṣedhakṛtas tasya tair bhavet pakṣabādhanam ||
suniścayena caiteṣāṃ bādhakapratyayād ṛte | pramāṇābhāsatā nāstīty etasmāt katyate balam ||
duṣṭajñānagṛhītārthapratiṣedho hi yujyate | gṛhītamātrabādhe tu svapakṣo 'pi na sidhyati ||
agrāhyatvāc ca bhedena viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | aprasiddhobhayatvaṃ vā vācyam anyatarasya vā ||
vaktṛśrotroś ca yajjñānaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | tannirālambanatvena svavāgbādho dvayor api ||
sambhavo na ca bhedasya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | tasmān nirūpaṇaṃ nāsti pratijñārthasya śobhanam ||
nirālambanatā nāma na kiñ cid vastu gamyate | tena yadvyatirekādau praśno naivopapadyate ||
yady avastu kathaṃ tv asmāṃs tvaṃ bodhayitum icchasi | budhyase vā svabuddhyā tvam, kalpitā tv atha sādhyate ||
asataḥ kalpanā kīdṛk, kḷptau vastu prasajyate | katham iṣṭam abhāve ced, vastu so 'pīti vakṣyate ||
tathā pratyaya ity eṣa karma bhāvādi vā bhavet | bhāvādiṣu virodhaḥ syāt karma cet siddhasādhanam ||
pratyāyyasya hi rūpāder nirālambanateṣyate | avijñānātmakatvena kiñ cin nālambate hy asau ||
kartṛtve karaṇatve vā pakṣatvaṃ śabdayor api | tannirālambanatvena pakṣābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
pratyāyyena ca bhinnena vinā kartrādyasambhavaḥ | pratyaye tannimitte vā bādhaḥ svavacanena te ||
athāpi rūḍhirūpeṇa pratyayaḥ syāt tathāpi tu | grāhakaṃ vastu siddhaṃ naḥ pratyayo 'nyasya vastunaḥ ||
tam abhyupetya pakṣaś ced abhyupetaṃ virudhyate | viśeṣyasyāprasiddhaś ca tava, asmākam atādṛśe ||
ātmadharmasvatantratvakalpane 'pi tathā bhavet | na ca pratyayamātratvaṃ kiñ cid asty anirūpaṇāt ||
śabdārthamātrarūpeṇa yathānyeṣāṃ nirūpaṇam | tathā ca bhavato na syād vācyabhedamanicchataḥ ||
nirālambanatā cāpi sarvathā yadi sādhyate | viśeṣaṇāprasiddhiś ca dṛṣṭāntaś ca na vidyate ||
kena cic cet prakāreṇa nirālambanatocyate | rasajñānasya rūpādiśūnyatvāt siddhasādhanam ||
atha buddhir yadākārā tadālambanavāraṇam | svākārasyābhyupetatvāt tadabhāvo virudhyate ||
bāhyānālambanatve 'pi bāhya ity agraho yadi | stambhādau naiva tadbuddhir ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam ||
atha stambhādirūpeṇa nirālambanatocyate | saṃvedanasya dṛṣṭatvāt tadvirodhaḥ prasajyate ||
dvicandrādiṣu tulyaś cet, nendriyāprāptito hi naḥ | tatrānālambanoktiḥ syān nārthasaṃvittyabhāvataḥ ||
sarvatrārthendriyāṇāṃ naḥ saṃyogasadasattayā | saṃvittau vidyamānāyāṃ sadasadgrāhikā sthitiḥ ||
bhavatas tv indriyādīnām abhāvād grahaṇād ṛte | nālambanasya hetuḥ syān niṣedho 'to na yujyate ||
bahirbhāvāprasiddhatvāt tenānālambanā matiḥ | kathañ cit sādhyate naiṣa pakṣo hi jñāyate tadā ||
yathānyabodhanāśakter nāprasiddhe viśeṣaṇe | pakṣasiddhis tathaiva syād viśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇe ||
nāprasiddhe padārthe hi vākyārthaḥ sampratīyate | tatpūrvakatvāt pakṣaś ca vākyārthaḥ sthāpayiṣyate ||
paryudāse niṣedhe vā vyatiriktasya vastunaḥ | prameyatvādyabhedena jagataḥ siddhasādhanam ||
yadi cātyantabhedena nirālambanatocyate | kathañ cic ced virudhyeta prākpakṣaḥ kalpitena ||
vastvādyākārataś cāpi dhīr nirālambaneṣyate | grāhakāc ced abhinnatvaṃ śaktibhedo virudhyate ||
nirālambanabuddheś ca yady utpattiḥ prasādhyate | dṛṣṭatvāt seṣyate 'smābhir bāhyagrāhyavivarjitā ||
samyaktvaṃ punar etasyās tvaṃ necchasi kathañ cana | ātmāṃśe 'vasitā hy eṣā mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat ||
caitrādipratyayānāṃ ca nirālambanatā yadi | dharmabhūtā na gṛhyeta sādhanotthitayā dhiyā ||
tato viṣayanānātvāt pratiyogyanirākṛtā | rūpāt sālambanaprāptiḥ satī kena nivāryate ||
yadi pratyayaśabdo 'pi pratyayatvena gṛhyate | saṃvittyālambanatvaṃ ca vāryate, siddhasādhanam ||
buddhyutpādanaśaktiś ced vāryā, sādhyaṃ na sidhyati | sādhanasya prayogo 'tra bodhakatvād vinā na te ||
na cābhidhāstyasambandhād ṛte bhedāc ca nāsty asau | na cāsau tadgataṃ bhedaṃ bodhayantya dhiyā vinā ||
prāśnikair agṛhīte ca vākyasyāvayave pṛthak | pakṣe hetau ca dṛṣṭānte vādini prativādini ||
sādhanasyāprayogaḥ syād abhyupetyocyate yadi | pūrvābhyupagamenaiva pratijñā bādhyate tataḥ ||
dharmādharmādibhede ca nāsiddhe paramārthataḥ | śiṣyātmanoś ca dharmāder upadeśo 'vakalpate ||
tadanuṣṭhānato buddher iṣṭo bhedaḥ, sphuṭaṃ ca taiḥ | sūtrāntare 'bhyupetatvād bhaved āgamabādhanam ||
sarvalokaprasiddhyā ca pakṣabādho 'tra te dhruvam | kṛtsnasādhanabuddhiś ca yadi mithyeṣyate tataḥ ||
sarvābhāvo yatheṣṭaṃ vā nyūnatā vābhidhīyate | teṣāṃ sālambanatve vā tair anaikāntiko bhavet ||
tadanyasya pratijñā cet, tadanyapratyayo mṛṣā | tanmithyātvaprasaṅge ca sarvaṃ pūrva na sidhyati ||
stambhādisādhanajñānabhedo na hi tathā bhavet | yāvad yāvat pratijñeyaṃ tadaṅgasya pratīyate ||
tāvat tāvat pareṣāṃ syān mithyātvād anyabādhanam | viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ ||
itthaṃ sarveṣu pakṣeṣu vaktavyaṃ pratisādhanam | bāhyārthālambanā buddhir iti samyak ca dhīr iyam ||
bādhakāpetabuddhitvād yathā svapnādibādhadhīḥ | sāpi mithyeti ced brūyāt, svapnādīnām abādhanāt ||
tasmāt sādharmyadṛṣṭānto bhavataḥ sādhane na hi | vijñānāstitvabhinnatvakṣaṇikatvādidhīs tathā ||
samyak ced abhyupeyeta tadānaikāntiko bhavet | tanmithyābhyupapattau ca pakṣabādhaḥ prasajyate ||
tathā ca baddham uktādivyavasthā na prakalpate | tataś ca mokṣayatnasya vaiphalyaṃ vaḥ prasajyate ||
vikalpotpadyamānā ca jñānāstitvādidhīr yadi | mṛṣeṣṭā, na ca dṛṣṭātra pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
pramāṇābhāvatas tena jñānāstitvādi durlabham | sarvaṃ cāpy asmadādīnāṃ mithyā jñānaṃ vikalpanāt ||
sānnidhyaviprakṛṣṭatve sattvāsattve ca durlabhe | mithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pi sāṃkhyādiparivarjanāt ||
bauddhadarśana ekasmin pakṣapāto na yujyate | mṛṣātvaṃ yadi buddheḥ syād bādhaḥ kiṃ nopalabhyate ||
bādhād vināpi tac cet syād vyavasthā na prakalpate | pratiyogini dṛṣṭe ca jāgrajjñāne mṛṣā bhavet ||
svapnādibuddhir asmākaṃ tava bhedo 'pi kiṅkṛtaḥ | na cānyat pratiyogyasti jāgrajjñānasya śobhanam ||
yaddarśanena mithyātvaṃ stambhādipratyayo vrajet | svapnādipratiyogitvaṃ sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
tadīyadharmavaidharmyād bādhakapratyayo yathā | yogināṃ jāyate buddhir bādhikā pratiyoginī ||
jāgratstambhādibuddhīnāṃ tataḥ svapnāditulyatā | prāptānāṃ tām avasthāṃ ca sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api ||
bādho 'yaṃ bhavitā tena siddhā sapratiyogitā | iha janmani keṣāñ cin na tāvad upalabhyate ||
yogyavasthāgatānāṃ tu na vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati | yogināṃ cāsmadīyānāṃ tvaduktapratiyoginī ||
tvaduktiviparītā vā bādhabuddhir bhaviṣyati | īdṛktve yogibuddhīnāṃ dṛṣṭānto na tavāsti ca ||
dṛṣṭāntas tv asmadādīnāṃ yo gṛhītaḥ sa vidyate | atha stambhādibuddhīnāṃ vadet sapratiyogitām ||
bādhyatvaṃ cāpi buddhitvān mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat | iṣṭaṃ sapratiyogitvaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhibhiḥ ||
tadātmanā ca bādhyatvaṃ grāhyāntaratayāpi ca | bādhakaiś cāpy anekāntaḥ, tadanyatve ca pūrvavat ||
mithyādhīpratiyogitvaṃ svapnādāv iva te bhavet | rāgādikṣayayogitvanimittādhigatis tathā ||
yāvān viśeṣa iṣṭaś cet sarvābhāvād viruddhatā | mahājanasya vā bādhādivānīmbādhabuddhivat ||
vācyo 'numānabādho vā yadi vā pratisādhanam | pūrvasādhanadoṣāś ca sandheyāḥ, tasya cādhunā ||
sādhyābhedād avācyatvād hetor nobhayasiddhatā | pratyayatvaṃ ca, sāmānyaṃ bhinnābhinnaṃ na vidyate ||
bhavato 'tyantabhinnaṃ ca matpakṣe 'pi kathañ cana | sārūpyānyanivṛttī ca netyetat sādhayiṣyate ||
tasmād dhetur na sāmānyam asti siddhaṃ dvayor api | viśeṣayoś ca hetutvaṃ pakṣatattulyasaṃsthayoḥ ||
na syād anvayahīnatvād ataddharmatayāpi ca | na cārthahīnā tadbuddhir hetutvena bhaviṣyati ||
āśrayāsiddhitā coktā viśeṣyasyāprasiddhitaḥ | tathā hetor viruddhatvaṃ dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
viśeṣaṇāprasiddhatvavikalpenaiva bodhite | svapnādipratyaye bāhyaṃ sarvathā na hi neṣyate ||
sarvatrālambanaṃ bāhyaṃ deśakālānyathātmakam | janmany ekatra bhinne vā tathā kālāntare 'pi vā ||
taddeśo vānyadeśo vā svapnajñānasya gocaraḥ | alātacakre 'lātaṃ syāc chīghrabhramaṇasaṃskṛtam ||
gandharvanagare 'bhrāṇi pūrvadṛṣṭaṃ gṛhādi ca | pūrvānubhūtatoyaṃ ca raśmitaptoṣaraṃ tathā ||
mṛgatoyasya vijñāne kāraṇatvena kalpyate | dravyāntare viṣāṇaṃ ca śaśasyātmā ca kāraṇam ||
śaśaśṛṅgadhiyaḥ, mauṇḍyaṃ niṣedhe śiraso 'sya ca | vastvantarair asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ śūnyatādhiyaḥ ||
kāraṇatvaṃ padārthānām asadvākyārthakalpane | atyantānanubhūto 'pi baddhyā yo 'rthaḥ prakalpyate ||
tasyotpattau kathañ cit syuḥ pṛthivyādīni kāraṇam | eṣa pratyakṣadharmaś ca vartamānārthataiva yā ||
sannikṛṣṭārthavṛttiś ca na tu jñānāntareṣv iyam | katham utpādayej jñānaṃ tatrāsaṃścet, kuto nviyam ||
arthasyāvidyamānasya vijñānotpattyaśaktatā | bāhyālambanatāyāṃ nau vivādo 'rthasya saṃnidhiḥ ||
yadi nāsti, kim evaṃ syād asmatpakṣanivartanam | tasmād yadanyathāsantam anyathā pratipadyate ||
tannirālambanaṃ jñānam, abhāvālambanaṃ ca tat | bhāvāntaram abhāvo 'nyo na kaś cid anirūpaṇāt ||
bhavatā dvayamatyetad durnirūpaṃ sahetukam | pratijñādoṣavac cāpi yojyā hetor viruddhatā ||
samastavyastadharmādisvarūpādiviparyayāt | dṛṣṭāntadoṣāḥ sarve ca yojyāḥ, na hy ekavastuni ||
tava sādhyāṃśahetvaṃśavyāptadharmādisambhavaḥ | ke cid vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto nāstīty apy anuyuñjate ||
tadabhāvād avṛtteś ca nāsty atrāvasaras tava | vidhirūpapratijñāyām etad vaktuṃ hi śakyate ||
tatrāvastuvipakṣe 'pi prayogasya hi sambhavaḥ | yasminn anityatā nāsti kāryatāpi na vidyate ||
tasmin, yathā khapuṣpādāv iti śakyaṃ hi bhāṣitum | atra tv avastusādhyatvaṃ vastunaś ca vipakṣatā ||
tena syād vyatireko 'sya vācyaḥ, yaś cāpi darśayet | pratiṣedhadvayāt tena vidhir eva pradarśitaḥ ||
