na ca śakyo vidhir vaktuṃ vastuny asati kena cit | evaṃ sthite ca sarvajñaniṣedhādāv iyaṃ gatiḥ ||
pratyakṣāder asāmarthyaṃ tadīyasyāsmadādivat | vaidharmyāsambhave 'py etadanye tv āhur adūṣaṇam ||
vinaiva tatprayogeṇa hetur aikāntiko yataḥ | sarvathā sadupāyānāṃ vādamārgaḥ pravartate ||
adhikāro 'nupāyatvān na vāde śūnyavādinaḥ | nanu sarvaṃ bhavatsiddhaṃ mayedaṃ sādhanaṃ kṛtam ||
kimarthaṃ tadasiddhyā tvaṃ vikalpyātrātthadūṣaṇam | vipralipsur ivāhaivaṃ kimarthaṃ nyāyavid bhavān ||
nāśrauṣīḥ sādhanatvaṃ kiṃ prasiddhasya dvayor api | yo 'pi tāvat parāsiddhaḥ svayaṃ siddho 'bhidhīyate ||
bhavet tatra pratīkāraḥ svato 'siddhe tu kā kriyā | taṃ sādhayan virundhyād dhi pūrvābhyupagataṃ naraḥ ||
asādhite tu sādhyo 'rtho na tena pratipadyate | parāsiddho na paryāptaḥ pareṣāṃ pratipattaye ||
tenāsādhanatā yuktā, svato 'siddhe tu kiṅkṛtā | dvayoḥ siddhasya hetutvaṃ nādṛṣṭāyopadiśyate ||
pratyeṣyanti svasiddhena sādhanena svayaṃ yataḥ | vadet katham asiddhaṃ cet, ityanenāpi kiṃ tava ||
gṛhītam agṛhītaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā sādhanāpi vā | mayocyate cet tv asiddhaṃ kiṃ tvaṃ na pratipadyase ||
yatra syāt puruṣādhīnā buddhis tatredam ucyate | kuto 'sya pūrvavijñānam ityatretanna yujyate ||
yadi caivaṃ bhaved atra pratijñāmātra eva hi | maddoṣājñānamātreṇa pratipattir bhavet tava ||
yatas tu sādhanāpekṣā tenāsyaiva pramāṇatā | tatsmṛtyutpattimātre tu vākyavyāpāra iṣyate ||
tasmād yathaiva sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanāt | sādhyaṃ gṛhṇan na vaktāram apekṣeta tathā bhavān ||
yac cāpi bhavato jñānaṃ pratyakādiḥ kim atra te | matprasiddhāsti yuktir vā sādhyaṃ vātra yathecchasi ||
tasmān na viduṣām etaduttaraṃ yujyate yataḥ | tava hetur asiddho 'yaṃ mama tena na sādhanam ||
satyaṃ yadi mamaivātra pratipattiḥ phalaṃ bhavet | tadā tvadaprasiddhe 'pi hetau māṃ prati hetutā ||
yadā tu jñānamātratvapratipattau bhavān mayā | pṛṣṭaḥ ko hetur atreti tadaivaṃ nopapadyate ||
svayaṃ na hy agṛhītena matprasiddhena vā bhavān | hetunā sādhyam etat tu pratipannaḥ kathañ cana ||
na ca vyāpriyate 'nyatra vacanaṃ prāśnikān prati | svaniścayāya yo hetus tasyaiva pratipādanāt ||
matprasiddhatvam etasya kutaś cāvagataṃ tvayā | kathaṃ cetthaṃ vivakṣā te svayam artham ajānataḥ ||
mayi jijñāsamāne 'pi buddhipūrvābhidhāyinaḥ | iti jñātvā ca vo vṛddhair bhāṣitobhayasiddhatā ||
tena yadvanmamaitena tvamadhitsasi hetunā | sādhyajñānam, tathaivāham ajñānaṃ tava dūṣaṇaiḥ ||
yathaiva ca bhavānīdṛk sādhyam uktvāsya sādhanam | sādhyānurūpam ajñātvā vihataḥ pratipādanāt ||
tathaiva pratipādyo 'pi tādṛksādhyabubhutsayā | manvānaḥ sādhanaṃ duṣṭaṃ tataḥ sādhyaṃ na budhyate ||
saṃvittyā sādhanaṃ matvā tatsadbhāve dṛḍhe sthite | sādhyasyāsambhavād eva tvaduktaṃ nāvabudhyate ||
tenāśeyaṃ na kartavyā mohād api mayerite | sādhane sādhanaṃ jñātvā para evāvabhotsyate ||
vispaṣṭaś cākṣapādokto virodho hetusādhyayoḥ | yamadṛṣṭvā parair uktam adūṣaṇam idaṃ kila ||
nanu lokaprasiddhena pūrvam etena hetunā | sādhyasiddhir mamāpy āsīt paramārtho 'sya nāstitā ||
yo 'dhunā paramārthena nāstītyevaṃ prakāśate | kathaṃ pūrvam asāv āsīd asaṃścet sādhanaṃ katham ||
sādhanaṃ ced avaśyaṃ ca paramārthāstitā bhavet | siddhir nāparamārthena paramārthasya yujyate ||
na dṛṣṭā śaśaśṛṅgādeḥ samyagjñānādihetutā | bāṣpādināpy adhūmena mithyā vahnyādibodhanam ||
tasmād asatyahetor yā paramārthe matis tava | sāpy asatyā na satyaṃ hi satyābhāsena gamyate ||
ye 'pi rekhādayo dṛṣṭā varṇānāṃ pratipādakāḥ | na te svenāpi rūpeṇa paramārthatvavarjitāḥ ||
varṇātmanā na satyāś cet, sarvabhāveṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ | padārthāntararūpeṇa na satyaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate ||
svarūpe vidyamāne tu yad apy evaṃ prakāśate | svarūpābhāvakḷptau tu na satyaṃ nāpy asatyatā ||
hetvādīnāṃ tu bhavataḥ svarūpeṇāpy asatyatā | tena bāṣpādivat teṣām upāyatvam, na lekhyavat ||
upāyānāṃ svarūpaṃ hi saṃvṛttyātmakam eva naḥ | tathā ca satyateṣṭaiva svarūpāsatyatā katham ||
saṃvṛtyā yat svarūpaṃ hi tadvāṅmātranibandhanam | hetutvaṃ paramārthasya pratipattuṃ na śaknuyāt ||
paramāthāc ca lokasya na bhede hetur asti te | laukikopāyagamyasya kena syāt paramārthatā ||
nanv asaty api bāhye 'rthe buddhyārūḍhena sidhyati | vāsanāśabdabhedotthavikalpapravibhāgataḥ ||
nyāyavidbhir idaṃ coktaṃ dharmādau buddhim āśrite | vyavahāro 'numānādeḥ kalpyate na bahiḥsthite ||
astīdaṃ vacanaṃ teṣām idaṃ tatra parīkṣyatām | bhedo 'sataḥ kathaṃ hi syād buddhiśabdaprakalpanāt ||
nirvastuke kathañ cin nu prasavo buddhiśabdayoḥ | śabdabhedo 'pi bhavatas tadabhāvān na sidhyati ||
yadi vā vidyamāno 'pi bhedo buddhiprakalpitaḥ | sādhyasādhanadharmāder vyavahārāya kalpyate ||
tato bhavatprayukte 'smin sādhane yāvad ucyate | sarvatrotpadyate buddhir iti dūṣaṇatā bhavet ||
yaś ca mantras tv ayokto 'yaṃ dharmyādau buddhim āśrite | na bāhyāpekṣayā sa syād asiddhyādau mayerite ||
buddhiprakḷptisiddhiś ca bhavatāṃ vyavahāriṇām | maduktaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ siddhaṃ tvaduktaṃ tu na sādhanam ||
bāhyārthavyavahāritvāj jñānotpāde sthite 'pi naḥ | kathañ cin na hi kalpyeta vyavahāro 'rthavarjitaḥ ||
nanu yadvanmayā hetur neṣyate dūṣaṇaṃ tathā | tena me dūṣaṇābhāvād aduṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ bhavet ||
nedānīṃ dūṣaṇaiḥ kāryam, sādhanābhāvato yadi | tvayaivāsmadabhipretā svapakṣāsiddhir āśritā ||
na cāsti vāsanābhedo nimittāsambhavāt tava | jñānabhedo nimittaṃ cet, tasya bhedaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ ||
vāsanābhedataś cet syāt, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam | svacchasya jñānarūpasya na hi bhedaḥ svato 'sti te ||
pramāṇaṃ vāsanāstitve bhede vāpi na vidyate | kuryād grāhakabhedaṃ sā grāhyabhedas tu kiṅkutaḥ ||
saṃvittyā jāyamānā hi smṛtimātraṃ karoty asau | kṣaṇikeṣu ca cit teṣu vināśe ca niranvaye ||
vāsyavāsakayoś caivam asāhityān na vāsanā | pūrvakṣaṇair anutpanno vāsyate nottaraḥ kṣaṇaḥ ||
uttareṇa vinaṣṭatvān na ca pūrvasya vāsanā | sāhitye 'pi tayor naiva sambandho 'stīty avāsanā ||
kṣaṇikatvād dvayasyāpi vyāpāro na parasparam | vinaśyac ca kathaṃ vastu vāsyate 'nyena naśyatā ||
avasthitā hi vāsyante bhāvābhāvair avasthitaiḥ | avasthito hi pūrvasmād bhidyate nottaro yadi ||
pūrvavad vāsanā tatra na syād evāviśeṣataḥ | bhaṅgure pūrvasādṛśyād bhinnatvāc cāsti vāsanā ||
naitad asty anurūpaṃ tu kṣaṇikatve dhiyāṃ tava | pūrvajñānaṃ tv anutpannaṃ kāryaṃ nārabhate kvacit ||
na vinaṣṭaṃ, na tasyāsti niṣpannasya kṣaṇaṃ sthitiḥ | tenotpannavinaṣṭatvān nāsty ārambhakṣaṇo 'pi hi ||
niranvayavinaṣṭatvād ānurūpyaṃ kutaḥ punaḥ | na tadīyosti kaś cic ca dharma uttarabuddhiṣu ||
samānadharmatāṃ muktvā nānurūpyaṃ ca vidyate | yadi syād ānurūpyāc ca vāsanā godhiyo yadā ||
hastibuddhir bhavet tatra vailakṣaṇyān na vāsanā | tataḥ paraṃ ca gojñānaṃ nirmūlatvān na sambhavet ||
sarvaṃ vilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ na syād eva vilakṣaṇāt | bāhyārthānugrahābhāvāt pārārthyenāvaśīkṛtāḥ ||
niranvayavināśinyaḥ kuryuḥ kāryaṃ kathaṃ kramāt | vināśe kāraṇasyeṣṭaḥ kāryārambhaś ca nānyathā ||
tataiva jñānanāśena vinaṣṭāḥ sarvavāsanāḥ | tena sarvābhya etābhyaḥ sarvākāraṃ yadutthitam ||
jñānam ekakṣaṇenaiva vināśaṃ gantum arhati | yady āśrayavināśe 'pi śaktyanāśo 'bhyupeyate ||
kṣaṇikatvaṃ ca hīyeta na cārambho 'nyathā bhavet | vāsanānāṃ pravāho 'pi yadi jñānapravāhavat ||
vāsanātas tato jñānaṃ na syāt tasmāc ca vāsanā | kuryātāṃ tulyam evaite nānyonyaṃ tu kadā cana ||
nānyo vilakṣaṇo hetur yenānyādṛk phalaṃ bhavet | tasmāt saṃvṛtisatyaiṣā kalpitā nāsti tattvataḥ ||
na cedṛśena bhāvena kāryam utpadyate kva cit | yasya tv avasthito jñātā jñānābhyāsena yujyate ||
sa tasya vāsanādhāro vāsanāpi sa eva vā | kusume bījapūrāder yallākṣādyupasicyate | tadrūpasyaiva saṃkrāntiḥ phale tasya, ity avāsanā ||
yuktyānupetām asatīṃ prakalpya yadvāsanām arthanirākriyeyam | āsthānivṛttyarthamavādi bauddhair grāhaṃ gatās tatra kathañ cid anye ||

§ 5,4 śunyavāda SNV

evam ukte 'numānasya jñānam āśritya dūṣaṇe | jñānapravṛttyaśaktyā tu paraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ||
yat tāvanmanyamānena pratyakṣaṃ bhavatocyate | dūṣaṇaṃ tadvirodhādi tadidānīṃ parīkṣyatām ||
pravartituṃ hi kiṃ śaktaṃ stambhādyarthe bahiḥ sthite | atha vātmāṃśa evaitat grāhye kṣīṇaṃ na vastuni ||
tad yady etena bāhyo 'rtho gṛhyate dūṣaṇaṃ tataḥ | tvaduktaṃ sarvam ātmāṃśe grāhye tannopapadyate ||
tatra tāvad idaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api | grāhyataṃ nīlapītādidīrghādyākāravastunaḥ ||
na cāpy ākārabhedena jñānajñeyāvadhāraṇā | na cānyataradharmatvaṃ vispaṣṭaṃ tatra gṛhyate ||
gṛhyamāṇasya cāstitvaṃ nāgrāhyasyāpramāṇakam | tasmād ākāravad vastu grāhyatvād vidyate dhruvam ||
ataḥ parīkṣamāṇānāṃ jñānam ākāravad yadi | tanmātre ca pramā kṣīṇā tato nāsty arthakalpanā ||
yadi vākāravattā syād bāhyasyaiveha vastunaḥ | tad asti gṛhyamāṇatvāt tatsiddhaivāsti dhīr api ||
kiṃ tāvad atra yuktaṃ syāj jñānam ākāravat, kutaḥ | ekam ākāravad vastu grāhyam ity adhyagīṣmahi ||
tad yady ākāravānartho bāhyaḥ kalpyeta tasya ca | grāhyatvam anyathā na syād iti grāhakakalpanā ||
tenākāravataḥ kḷptād grāhyād ākāravarjitam | vastvantaraṃ prakalpyaṃ syād grāhakaṃ niṣpramāṇakam ||
tasyākalpanam icchaṃś ced arthe grāhakatāṃ vadeḥ | saṃjñāmātre visaṃvādaḥ siddhā tv ekārthakalpanā ||
grāhyagrāhakayor aikyaṃ sarvathā pratipādyate | bāhyābhyantararūpaś ca parikalpyo mṛṣeṣyate ||
matpakṣe yady api svaccho jñānātmā paramārthataḥ | tathāpy anādau saṃsāre pūrvajñānaprasūtibhiḥ ||
citrābhiś citrahetutvād vāsanābhir upaplavāt | svānurūpyeṇa nīlādi grāhyagrāhakarūṣitam ||
pravibhaktam ivotpannaṃ nānyam artham apekṣate | anyonyahetutā caiva jñānaśaktyor anādikā ||
anekakalpanāyāś ca jyāyasī hy ekakalpanā | śaktimātrasya bhedaś ca vastubhedād viśiṣyate ||
tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāj jñānasyākārakalpanā | jyāyasī, bhavatas tv arthaṃ kalpayitvā bhaved iyam ||
tadasiddhāvaśaktatvāt, tenaivaṃ viprakṛṣṭatā | pratyāsannaṃ ca, sambaddhaṃ grāhyaṃ mama bhaviṣyati ||
itaś cākāravajjñānam, yasmāt tadvat prakāśakam | svayamprakāśahīnasya bāhyasyopāsanaṃ matam ||
na cāgṛhīte jñānākhye prakāśyo 'rtho 'vadhāryate | tadadhīnaprakāśatvād dīpābhāse yathā ghaṭaḥ ||
utpanneṣv api cārtheṣu prakāśābhāvataḥ kva cit | pratibandhakayogād vā saṃvittir nopajāyate ||
jñānasyotpadyamānasya pratibandho na kaś cana | na cāprakāśarūpatvaṃ yenāsyāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
prāk cārthagrahaṇādiṣṭā tasyotpattis tadaiva ca | saṃvedanaṃ bhaved asya, na cet kālāntare 'pi na ||
kiṃ hi tasya bhaved ūrdhvaṃ prāk ca nāsīn na yena tat | pūrvaṃ gṛhītaṃ paścāt ca gṛhītam iti bhāṣyate ||
jñānāntarasya cotpattiṃ prakāśo na pratīkṣate | tasya tasyāpi cānyena saṃvittāvasthitir bhavet ||
jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvam arthābhāve 'pi dṛśyate | parāmarśo 'rtharūpasya sa kathaṃ vopapadyate ||
tadrūpamārthamālikhya yadi dhīrnopajāyate | bhūtakāle ca yadyarthas tatpūrvaṃ nopalakṣitaḥ ||
vaktāraś cāpi dṛśyante varttamānārthabuddhiṣu | nīlo 'rtho 'yaṃ yato me 'tra tadrūpā jāyate matiḥ ||
tasmāt pūrvagṛhītāsu buddhiṣv arthopalambhanam | na copalabdhir astīhi nirākārāsu buddhiṣu ||
vivekabuddhyabhāvāc ca, sākārasya ca darśanāt | ākāravattayā bodho jñānasyaiva prasajyate ||
na hy evaṃ kalpanā śakyā nirākārād ito matiḥ | gṛhyate 'rthas tataḥ paścāt sākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
ākāravattvabhedo hi jñātvā śakyeta bhāṣitum | prāgbuddhigrahaṇād arthe saṃvittir neti sādhitam ||
na cārthākāra evāyaṃ jñānārūḍhaḥ pratīyate | na hi so 'ntaḥpraveśāya paryāpto nārthahānaye ||
itthambhāve pramāṇaṃ ca tasya vaktuṃ na śakyate | tadīyapratibimbatvam etasmād eva neṣyate ||
niścandre bimbarūpaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ yena divā jalam | sa rātrau khe ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā jānāti pratibimbatām ||
vijñāne na kadā cit tu prāṅ nirākāradarśanam | bāhye vākāravattādhīr yenaivaṃ kalpanā bhavet ||
śabdagandharasānāṃ ca kīdṛśī pratibimbatā | jñāne ca gṛhyamāṇasya kathaṃ syād arthadharmatā ||
bāhyābhyantaradeśatvān na cārthajñānayor mithaḥ | samparko 'sti yato mohādavivekamatir bhavet ||
asammūḍhasya cādṛṣṭe na sammohaprakalpanā | kalpyamāne 'tha vāpy evaṃ tad dvayor avatiṣṭhate ||
saṃsargadhama ākāras tasmād eva na yujyate | deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, mūrāmūrtatayā tathā ||
tailokyena prasaṅgāc ca saṃsargo naikakālatā | na cāpy ārjavataḥ sthānaṃ jñāne nārthasya vidyate ||
sarvathā kalpanāyāṃ ca cakṣuṣāpi rasādayaḥ | gṛhyeran sarvabhāvānāmaṇvākārāś ca tadgatāḥ ||
na cāpi viṣayatvena sthāne saṃsargakalpanā | viṣayatvaṃ hi kīdṛk syāt prāgākāropalambhanāt ||
na hy asañcetito bhāvo viṣayatvena kalpyate | viṣayatvāt tadākāra ākārād viṣayaś ca saḥ ||
dvayor ākāranirmuktaṃ sattvaṃ saṃsṛṣṭatā tathā | svarūpataḥ paricchidya vaktum ityādi yujyate ||
na cāpy asyeha sadbhāvaḥ prāg gṛhīto na copari | na hy ākāravinirmuktaṃ grāhyam astīti bhāṣitam ||
tasmād arthena saṃsargo niṣpramāṇaka eva te | jñānavaicitryasiddhyarthaṃ na cāstyarthasya kalpanā ||
tadadhīnaṃ hi vaicitryaṃ kva dṛṣṭaṃ yena kalpyate | nirākāreṇa cotpattir vaicitryākārayoḥ katham ||
nirākārāc ca viṣayād buddhyākāro 'tivismayaḥ | smṛtisvapnādibodhe ca syād anākāratā tava ||
na hi tatrārthasaṃsargaḥ kevalā vāsanaiva tu | hetutvenopapanneti saiva jāgraddhiyām api ||
anvayavyatirekābhyām evaṃ jñānasya gamyate | ākāraḥ, na hi bāhyasya jñānāpeto nidarśyate ||
bāhyāpeto mayā yadvat, tasmāt saṃsargavāgiyam | nirākāre 'pi vijñāne vāsanāsv eva yujyate ||
dvayor apy eka ākāra ityetasyāpramāṇatā | deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, dvayoś cānavadhāraṇāt ||
evam evārthabuddhyoḥ syāt sādṛśyān nāvibhaktatā | bhede jñāte hi sādṛśyaṃ nājñāte syāt khapuṣpavat ||
tathā dvicandramāyādāv anyathārthe vyavasthite | yā syād ākārasaṃvittir nāsāv arthanibandhanā ||
nakṣatraṃ tārakā tiṣyo dārā ityevamādiṣu | naikatrārthe viruddhatvāl liṅgānekatvasambhavaḥ ||
parivrāṭkāmukaśunāṃ kuṇapādimatis tathā | dīrghahrasvatvabuddhiś ca hy ekasminn apy apekṣayā ||
ghaṭatvāt pārthavadravyaprameyādimatis tathā | yugapadgrāhakāṇāṃ ca na syād aikātmyavattayā ||
nārthe hy ekatra yugapad viruddhākārasambhavaḥ | pratyayānāṃ tu bhinnatvād bhavec chaktyanusārataḥ ||
nirapekṣaṃ svarūpeṇa tasmāj jñānaṃ yadākṛti | tathārtho na yathārthaṃ tu jñānam utpadyate kva cit ||
itthaṃ vijñānatantratve ko nv arthaṃ kalpayiṣyati | dhīranāropitākārā svātmany evopayokṣyate ||
naitad asti, tvayaikaṃ hi grāhyaṃ grāhakam iṣyate | na caikasyaivam ātmatve dṛṣṭāntaḥ kaścid asti te ||
agnyādayo ghaṭādīnāṃ prasiddhā ye prakāśakāḥ | na te prakāśyarūpā hi prakāśasya, anapekṣaṇāt ||
grāhyatvaṃ tu yadā teṣāṃ tadākṣaṃ grāhakaṃ matam | akṣagrahaṇakāle tu grāhikā dhīr bhaviṣyati ||
tasyāṃ tu gṛhyamāṇāyām anyā dhīr grāhikeṣyate | nanv ātmā grāhako grāhyo bhavatābhyupagamyate ||
kathañcid dharmarūpeṇa bhinnatvāt pratyayasya tat | grāhakatvaṃ bhavet tatra grāhyaṃ dravyādi cātmanaḥ ||
yas tu nātyantabhedo 'tra kva vāsāv iṣyate mayā | pratyāsattinimittā tu pratyagātmapravarttitā ||
asmatprayogasambhinnā jñānasyaiva tu kartari | bhavantī tatra saṃvittir yujyetāpy ātmakartṛkā ||
na cātra karaṇajñānagrāhakākāravedanam | grāhyatvaṃ yena buddheḥ syād abhinnatve 'pi pūrvavat ||
anyarūpāpi saṃvittir yady anyaviṣayeṣyate | jñānākārāpi saṃvittiḥ kasmān nārthasya kalpyate ||
abhinnatvaṃ yadā ceṣṭaṃ grāhyagrāhakavastunoḥ | tadānyatarasaṃvittau dvyākāraṃ grahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
yadā tu grāhyam ākāraṃ nīlādi pratipadyate | na tadā grāhakākārā saṃvittir dṛśyate kva cit ||
tasmād abhinnatā cet syāt tasyāpy anubhavo bhavet | grāhyo vā nānubhūyeta grāhakānanubhūtivat ||
grāhakagrahaṇe 'py evaṃ grāhyasaṃvedanaṃ bhavet | śuddham eva nirākāraṃ grāhakaṃ saṃvidasti hi ||
grāhyād abhinnatāyā ca sā saṃvittir na yujyate | grāhako vā na gṛhyeta tadgrāhyānanubhūtivat ||
yathāvad grāhyasaṃvittau grāhakagrahaṇe 'pi vā | grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittir nāsty eva syād dvayor api ||
sa bahirdeśasambaddhaḥ ity anena nirūpyate | grāhyākārasya saṃvittir grāhakānubhavād ṛte ||
paraṃ prati hi sādhyatvad arthasyākārasiddhaye | bahirdeśena sambandho na hetutvāya kalpate ||
tasmād bahir itīhedaṃ niṣkṛṣṭaṃ grāhakāṃśataḥ | saṃvedyaṃ nīlapītādi pratyakṣāder udāhṛtam ||
na pūrvaṃ jñāyate buddhir ityatraitad vadiṣyate | grāhakasyaiva saṃvittir lakṣyate grahaṇe kva cit ||
na smarāmi mayā ko 'pi gṛhīto 'rthas tadeti hi | smaranti grāhakotpādagrāhyarūpavivarjitam ||
tasmād abhinnatāyāṃ ca grāhye 'pi smaraṇaṃ bhavet | grāhakasmṛtinirbhāsāt tatrāpy eṣaiva gṛhyate ||
tadatyantāvinābhāvān naikākāraṃ hi jāyate | anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ siddhaivaṃ bhinnatā tayoḥ ||
grāhyāṃśo grāhakāṃśena gṛhyate, grāhakaḥ punaḥ | gṛhyeteti na vaktavyam, grāhakāntaravarjanāt ||
grāhyāṃśenāpy aśaktatvān na tasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet | grāhakatvena caitasya hīyetaiva dvirūpatā ||
grāhake gṛhyamāṇe ca grāhyamātraprasañjanam | na syād ākāra ekaś ced itarasyāpi nāstitā ||
udbhavābhibhavābhyāṃ ca grāhyāgrāhyatvadarśanam | yathā dīpaprabhādīnāṃ rūpamātropalambhanam ||
divā cāgneḥ samīpasthaiḥ sparśa evopalabhyate | gandhavad dravyavṛttau ca gandhasyaivopalambhanam ||
na guṇāntarasaṃvittir yathātrābhibhavāt, tathā | nākārāntarasaṃvittir grāhyagrāhakabuddhiṣu ||
grāhyād ananyabhūto 'pi kaś cin naivopalabhyate | nityānityādayo dharmāḥ śabdādigrahaṇe yathā ||
abhedaṃ vābhyupetyāyaṃ prasaṅgo yadi gīyate | ekasmin gṛhyamāṇe 'śe na gṛhyetāparaḥ katham ||
tasmād yat syād yadā yogyaṃ tasyaiva grahaṇaṃ tadā | dvayaṃ ca tvadupanyastaṃ śaktyabhāvān na gṛhyate ||
kuto 'yam ekavastutve yogyāyogyatvasambhavaḥ | udbhavābhibhavātmatvaṃ kathaṃ caikasya kalpitam ||
ekāṃśābhibhave ca syād itarābhibhavo 'pi te | tathā tasyābhibhūtatvād grāhyatvaṃ na ca yujyate ||
ayogyatā vikalpyaivam, dṛṣṭāntā ye 'tra kīrtitāḥ | rūpādibhedāt tatra syād udbhavābhibhavādyapi ||
yadāpy ekāntato bhedo rūpāder na parasparam | tadāpi dravyarūpasya pariṇāmas tathā tathā ||
abhinnatve 'pi na grāhyam iti yac cābravīd bhavān | kṛtakatvādidharmāṇāṃ dhībhede 'nanyatā katham ||
na hy anyatpratyayād asti bhinnād grāhyasya bhedakam | na ceyattaiva bhedasya deśato mūrtito 'pi vā ||
kāraṇānāṃ hi sambandhaḥ kāryaiḥ kṛtakatocyate | vibhāgo 'vayavānāṃ ca bhavet kva cid anityatā ||
buddhyāder ātmarūpādisthānaṃ nāśitvam ucyate | nityatvaṃ sarvadā sattā, vastutvaṃ saiva kīrtyate ||
pramāṇajñānasambandhaḥ prameyajñeyatocyate | sarvatra cātra bhinnatvam asti kena cid ātmanā ||
tasmād yathaiva rūpāder deśabhedādibhir vinā | buddhibhedena bhedo 'sti tathaivātra pratīyatām ||
atyantabhinnatāsmābhir naiva kasya cid iṣyate | sarvaṃ hi vasturūpeṇa bhidyate na parasparam ||
sarvaṃ ca kṛtakatvādi kriyāhetvādyapekṣayā | gṛhyate tadasaṃvittāvabhede 'pi na gṛhyate ||
jñāne naivaṃvidho bhedo nāpekṣānyatra vidyate | paraspareṇa cāpekṣā syāc cet, sannihitaś ca saḥ ||
nanu grāhakam ityevaṃ grāhyam ity api vā matiḥ | nīlādigrahaṇe nāstīty apekṣā katham ucyate ||
mā bhūd evaṃ tathāpy atra dvyākāre grahaṇaṃ bhavet | evaṃ cāgṛhyamāṇe vā jñāne dvyākāratā katham ||
uttarottaravijñānaviśeṣād yā prakalpyate | grāhakākārasaṃvittiḥ smaraṇāc cānumānikī ||
ekākāraṃ kila jñānaṃ prathamaṃ yadi kalpyate | tatas tadviṣayāpy anyā tadrūpaiva matir bhavet ||
ghaṭavijñānatajjñānaviśeṣo 'to na sidhyati | grāhakākārasaṃvittau tv ākārapracayo bhavet ||
jāyate pūrvavijñānaṃ dvyākāraṃ yatra tat punaḥ | tasyātmīyaś ca pūrvau ca viṣayasthāvupaplutau ||
pareṣv ākāravṛddhyaivaṃ pūrvebhyo bhinnatā, tathā | grāhyavat smaraṇāt paścāt saṃvittau grāhakaḥ purā ||
na tāvad evamākārān paśyāmaḥ pracayānvitān | viṣayavyapadeśāc ca narte jñānanirūpaṇam ||
tasmāj jñānātmanaikatve grāhyabhedanibandhanaḥ | saṃvittibhedaḥ siddho 'tra kimākārāntareṇa naḥ ||
nirākāratasāmye 'pi yathākāravatāṃ dhruvam | bhedaḥ svābhāvikas tadvajjñānānāṃ kiṃ na sidhyati ||
smṛter uttarakālaṃ cetyetanmithyaiva gīyate | tadaiva hy asya saṃvittir arthāpattyopajāyate ||
gṛhītam eva yac coktaṃ tadabhedāt, na tad, yataḥ | nāsmabhir vākyavṛttes tvaṃ nimittam anuyujyase ||
grāhyagrāhakataivāsya kena cin nopalabhyate | pratyakṣajñānapakṣe ca naiṣā syād ānumānikī ||
ekākāre ca vijñāne yady anyo 'py atra kalpyate | sahasrākārataikasya kasmān na parikalpyate ||
grāhyagrāhakayor bhedo nanv asty eva parasparam | siddho naḥ pakṣa evaṃ syāt, na, jñānatvād abhedataḥ ||
bhinnābhinnatvam ekasya kuto 'tra parikalpitam | tvayā sāṃkhyamatenaivam uktvā buddhasya śāsanam ||
ekaṃ ced grāhakaṃ grāhyaṃ kuto bhinnatvavāgiyam | bhinnaṃ cet katham ucyeta tasyaikatvaṃ punas tvayā ||
ekajñānād ananyatvād grāhyagrāhakayor mithaḥ | ekatvena bhavej jñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakam eva vā ||
tatra cānyatarāpāye dvitīyāpāyataḥ punaḥ | jñānasyāṃśadvayāsattvān naiḥsvābhāvyād abhāvatā ||
bhinnābhyāṃ vāpy abhinnatvād bhedo jñānātmano bhavet | tatsvātmanaḥ, tataś caivaṃ siddhaṃ vastudvayaṃ hi naḥ ||
tayoś ca yadi saṃjñeyaṃ jñānam ity astv athāpi vā | jñānaṃ jñāyata ityartho dhīrbhāve karaṇe 'pi vā ||
sarvathā vastubhedo naḥ siddhaḥ śabdo yathāruci | pravartatāṃ na nas tatra kācid vipratipannatā ||
atha saty api bhinnatve grāhyaṃ jñānāntaraṃ bhavet | jñānatve tasya kā yuktiḥ, pūrvoktā yadi seṣyate ||
jñānaṃ jñānam itīdaṃ tu na dvayor anuvartate | vyatiriktaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ tvayā nābhyupagamyate ||
vyatireke tayor jñānān na jñānātmakatā bhavet | tadrūparahitatve ca jñānābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
tābhyāṃ ca tasya sambandhe pratyekaṃ vyatiṣajya ca | bhedasāvayavatvādi doṣo vaiśeṣikādivat ||
yathā hi teṣāṃ jātyādau doṣā hy uktāḥ parair amī | tathaivaiṣāṃ prasajyante bhinnābhinnārthasaṅgatau ||
tābhyām avyatireke vā bhedaḥ pūrvokta eva te | sādṛśyāpohasāmānyakalpanā vārayiṣyate ||
vastvantarasya cābhāvāt tvayāpoho 'pi duṣkaraḥ | nājñānaṃ nāma kiñ cit syād apohyaṃ jñānavādinaḥ ||
apoho na hy abhāvasya kathañ cid upapadyate | vastvantaram abhāvaḥ syād, apohyatvāc ca vastutā ||
tenājñānanivṛttau hi jñāne 'nyārtha prasajyate | kalpitaṃ syād apohyaṃ cet, nātyantāsatyakalpanā ||
buddhir ajñānanirbhāsā tavājñānaṃ prakalpitam | tataś ca jñānam evaikam apohyatvena sammatam ||
na cātmāpoha evāsti kva cit sāmānyakalpane | vṛkṣasya na hy apohyatvaṃ vṛkṣeṇaiva kadā cana ||
apohye caiva vijñāne jñānatvaṃ na bhavet tava | vṛkṣatvaṃ na hy apohyeṣu kalaśādiṣu yujyate ||
tataś cājñānam evārtha ity abhinnārthatā bhavet | ajñānapratyayaś cāyaṃ kimālambana iṣyate ||
na tāvaj jñānanirmuktam ajñānaṃ grāhyam asti te | na ca vastu niṣiddhaṃ tadabhāvaḥ kiṃ na gṛhyate ||
bhāvo na gṛhyate yena tasyābhāveṣu kā kathā | svāṃśaparyavasānaṃ ca tulyam atrāpi kāraṇam ||
tena jñānāntaraṃ vā syād grāhyam ātmāṃśa eva vā | svarūpaviparītaṃ ca kathaṃ grāhyaṃ pratīyate ||
yathoṣṇe 'nuṣṇadhīr nāsti, jñāne 'py ajñānadhīs tathā | tena na jñānamātratve syād apohyaṃ kathañ cana ||
grāhyagrāhakayoś cāto na jñānātmasamānatā | tasmād anyataratredaṃ jñānatvaṃ sampratīyate ||
tatrāpy ubhayasiddhatvād grāhakasyeti gamyate | vastubhede prasiddhe ca vyapadeśo yathāruci ||
jñānam astūbhayaṃ vārtho grāhako vārtha ucyatām | buddhyor ayugapadbhāvān na dvayor mayamānatā ||
kṣaṇikā hītyanenoktam, artho hy ekaḥ prasajyate | anyonyanirapekṣatvād yugapac cāpi janmani ||
mānameyatvanāstitvam, kriyākārakavarjanāt | arthavijñānayor atra yā mitiṃ prati saṅgatiḥ ||
kāryakāraṇabhāvo 'yam, nānyatraivaṃ ca dṛśyate | niyamaś ca na labhyeta savyadakṣiṇaśṛṅgavat ||
idaṃ kāryam ayaṃ hetuḥ, dvayaṃ na, anyonyasaṃśrayāt | tadbhāvabhāvitāmātraṃ hetuḥ kair naiva varṇyate ||
paurvāparyavinirmuktaṃ kāryakāraṇalakṣaṇam | gavāśvasya yathā nāsti paurvāparye 'pi tat tathā ||
yugapajjāyamāne 'pi santatyantaraje kṣaṇe | rūpādiṣu ghaṭe yadvat, tasmāt pūrvam avasthite ||
yo yasmāj jāyate paścāt sa tatkāryam itīṣyate | hetuhetumatāṃ siddhaṃ yaugapadyanidarśanam ||
yat pradīpaprabhādyuktaṃ sūkṣmaḥ kālo 'sti tatra naḥ | durlakṣas tu yathā vedhaḥ padmapattraśate tathā ||
bhāgayor yaugapadyena tathaiva syān nirākriyā | na ca śaktyarpaṇadvāraṃ krameṇālambanaṃ bhavet ||
grāhyaṃ tadā hy atītaṃ syāt, tadrūpyaṃ cāpramāṇakam | atītatvānuviddho hi smṛtyā grāhyo 'nubhūyate ||
tadvad eva bhaved atra, svapne na syāt, viparyayāt | tatra hy avartamāno 'pi gṛhyate vartamānavat ||
bādhajñānād idaṃ bhrāntam, na tv atraivaṃ viparyayaḥ | tasmāt pratyakṣabuddhīnāṃ nātito viṣayo bhavet ||
atītatvād yathaivāsāṃ vṛtto janmāntareṣu yaḥ | tadrūpatvena vā jñānaṃ hetur bhāvivad ucyate ||
atītatve 'pi nārtho 'yaṃ dhīreṣety atra kā pramā | atītaṃ yac ca vijñānaṃ grāhyatvena prakalpitam ||
tasmād grāhakarūpaṃ vā grāhyaṃ vobhayathāpi vā | grāhyākāratvamātre syād arthaḥ śabdāntareṇa te ||
svakāle cāpy asaṃvitter na syāc chaktyarpaṇaṃ tataḥ | yathaivānāgatāj jñānāt santatyantarajād api ||
dṛḍhatvenāpy avijñātāt tathotpannād vinaśyataḥ | kevalagrāhakatve tu viṣayatvaṃ na yujyate ||
kimapekṣya ca tasyedaṃ grāhakatvaṃ prakalpyate | dvyākāratā nirastaiva, saṃvedyeta tadaiva ca ||
tataś cottaravijñānaṃ na pratīkṣeta bodhakam | dvyākārakalpanāyāṃ ca parasyātmāṃśa eva te ||
pramāparyavasānena nātīto viṣayo bhavet | pūrvagrāhyasarūpatve grāhakatvaṃ prahīyate ||
grāhakākāramātre syād viṣayo nāsarūpataḥ | na ca śaktyarpaṇasyātra vyāpāra upalabhyate ||
śaktyarpaṇasya cābhāvo yuṣmatpakṣe prasādhitaḥ | santānāntaravac caiṣāṃ niṣedhyā hetusādhyatā ||
vāsyavāsakabhāvaś ca jñānatvād ekasantatau | tasmād yadbhāsakaṃ rūpaṃ tadgrāhyāt tasya bhinnatā ||
tatsaṃvittāv asaṃvitte rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā | grāhyaṃ tadgrāhakāc caiva tatparāmṛśatā yataḥ ||
na parāmṛśyate 'vaśyaṃ rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā | dvayaṃ paraspareṇaivaṃ bhinnaṃ sādhyaṃ rasādivat ||
aikarūpyeṇa cājñānāt santānāntarabuddhivat | jñānaṃ svāṃśaṃ na gṛhṇāti jñānotpatteḥ svaśaktivat ||
grāhyatvapratiṣedhaś ca dvayahīnā hi vāsate | caitrajñānaṃ tadudbhūtajñānāṃśagrāhyabodhakam ||
jñānatvān na bhaved yadvat tasya dehāntarodbhavam | etayaiva diśā vācyā śaktidvayanirākriyā ||
pramāṇāntarasiddhatvād anyatrānekaśaktitā | na tv atra kāraṇaṃ tādṛk śaktibhedakṛdasti te ||
tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāl lāghavād yaḥ parigrahaḥ | upāyatvāc ca yat tasya pūrvagrahaṇakalpanam ||
cakṣurādīndriyair atra tadanaikāntikaṃ bhavet | yad apy apratibaddhatvād utpattau gṛhyatām iti ||
tatrātmanā na śaktyaṃ tannānyotpattis tadasti vā | tenaitat kāraṇābhāvāt tadānīṃ nānubhūyate ||
nānyathā hy arthasadbhāvo dṛṣṭaḥ sannupapadyate | jñānaṃ cen netyataḥ paścāt pramāṇam upajāyate ||
na cāpy apratibandhena kevalena graho bhavet | viśiṣṭakāraṇābhāve 'py artho naivānubhūyate ||
vyāpṛtaṃ cārthasaṃvittau jñānaṃ nātmānamṛcchati | tena prakāśakatve 'pi bodhāyānyat pratīkṣyate ||
īdṛśaṃ vā prakāśatvaṃ tasyārthānubhavātmakam | na cātmānubhavo 'sty asyetyātmano na prakāśakam ||
sati prakāśakatve ca vyavasthā dṛśyate yathā | rūpādau cakṣurādīnāṃ tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
prakāśakatvaṃ bāhye 'rthe śaktyabhāvāt tu nātmani | anyena vānubhāve 'sāv anavasthā prasajyate ||
tatra tatra smṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvānubhavakalpanā | ekena tv anubhūtatve sarvaṃ tatraiva sambhavet ||
tatrāpi smṛtir ity etan na lokānumataṃ vacaḥ | na hi vijñānasantānaṃ kaś cit smarati laukikaḥ ||
ghaṭādāv agṛhīte 'rthe yadi tāvad anantaram | arthāpattyāv abudhyante vijñānāni punaḥ punaḥ ||
yāvacchramaṃ tataḥ paścāt tāvatyeva smariṣyati | tadā tv akalpite 'py evaṃ smṛtivarndhyāsutādivat ||
smṛtibhrāntaś ca yāpy atra paścāj jñāneṣu jāyate | tadaivārthasmṛter eṣāṃ tajñānādipramāṇatā ||
yāvacchramaṃ ca tadbuddhis tatprabandhe mahaty api | śramād rucyānyasamparkād vicchedo viṣayeṣv iva ||
tatrāpi smṛtir ity eṣāṃ prathame pratyaye yadi | tanmātragrahaṇād evaṃ nānavasthā prasajyate ||
smaraṇaṃ tv atha sarveṣu tatsiddhyai grahaṇaṃ tathā | pramāṇavattvād āyātaḥ pravāhaḥ kena vāryate ||
atha tānyādyavijñānaviṣayāṇīti kalpyate | nottarottarabuddhīnāṃ viśeṣa upapadyate ||
vijñānaviṣayatvaṃ ca yasya sarvāsu buddhiṣu | ghaṭavijñāna tajñānaviśeṣas tena durlabhaḥ ||
smaran yathaiva vijñānaṃ nirākāraṃ smaratyayam | tathā smaran gṛhītārthaṃ nirākāratayā smaret ||
jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvaṃ parāmarśo bhavaty asau | tasyārtheṣv abhyupāyatvān na tu grāhyatvakāritaḥ ||
pratyāsannatvasambandhau grāhyatvāsambhavāc cyutau | viṣayatvena vāpy etau staḥ kiṃ deśāvibhāgataḥ ||
arthākārasya yo 'py ukto mithyājñāneṣv asambhavaḥ | dośakālānyathāmātrasambhavaḥ keṣu cit kṛtaḥ ||
pratyakṣād anyavijñānam atītānāgatair api | janyate 'rthe bhavantīṣu vāsanāsvasatīṣu vā ||
yaḥ punar nānubhūto 'rtho na vāpy anubhaviṣyate | vāsanābhāvatas tatra tavāpy anubhavaḥ katham ||
vināpi vāsanātaś ced buddhir utpadyate tataḥ | vāsanāyā nimittatvam abhyupetaṃ virudhyate ||
vāsanā ced bhavet tatra sā ca saṃvittipūrvikā | tathā sati ca pūrvatra gṛhītaḥ kvāpy asau dhruvam ||
evaṃ ca naiva vaktavyam atyantābhavanaṃ kva cit | anyathānupapatyā hi siddhā janmāntare 'stitā ||
duṣṭatvena ca vijñānam anyathāpi vyavasthitam | pṛthivyādiṣu gṛhṇīyād ākāraṃ tannibandhanam ||
tānyapāsya tu naivārthe kva cid ākārakalpanā | na jñānaṃ hy anavaṣṭambham ātmānaṃ labdhum arhati ||
vijñānasyaiva vā kāryaṃ yady eṣo 'nye ca kalpitāḥ | viśeṣaḥ ko 'tra yenāyam atyantāsannitīṣyate ||
tasmād bhrāntir api tv eṣāṃ kalpayantyartham eva naḥ | kalpayatyanyathā santaṃ na tv ātmānaṃ vyavasyati ||
tataś ca bādhakajñānād vācoyuktir iyaṃ bhavet | arthe 'nyathāpi saty eṣa dhiyākāraḥ pratīyate ||
dvicandrādimatiṣv evam, tārakādimatau tathā | strītvādyanyatra dṛṣṭaṃ syāt, kathañ cid veha sambhavet ||
śabdamātrapratīyā vā, dṛṣṭair vā kaiś cid iṅganāt | saṃstyānaprasavasthānair yathā pātañjale mate ||
tena liṅgatrayasyātra sadbhāvaḥ syāt pramāṇavān | apekṣābhedataś cātra virodho 'pi na vidyate ||
kuṇapādimatau caivaṃ sārvarūpye vyavasthite | vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyo vyavasthākāradarśane ||
svapratyayānukāro hi bahvākāreṣu vastuṣu | nirdhāraṇe bhaved dhetur nāpūrvākārakalpane ||
tathā dīrghaghaṭatvādau bhinnāpekṣānibandhanā | ākārabhedasampattir aviruddhā bhaviṣyati ||
nānekākārasaṃvitter nirākāratvakalpanā | yuktā, pratītibhedāt tu bahvākāratvasambhavaḥ ||
saṃvitteś ca viruddhānām ekasminn api sambhavaḥ | ekākāraṃ bhaved ekam iti neśvarabhāṣitam ||
tathaiva tadupetavyaṃ yad yathaivopalabhyate | na cāpy aikāntikaṃ tasya syād ekatvaṃ ca vastunaḥ ||
tasmād deśādisadbhāvanimittaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pṛthak | vastvākārāḥ pratīyerann udbhavābhibhavātmakāḥ ||
yugapadgrāhakāṇāṃ ca yo yadākāravācinam | śabdaṃ smarati tenāsāv ākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
nityaṃ satsu tathā loke rūpādiṣu ghaṭe pṛthak | cakṣurādyanurodhena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
evam eva ghaṭatvādau sarvān prati bhavaty api | vācakasmṛtibhedena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
tasmād bahiḥ sthito 'py ātmā narāṇāṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ | prāpya vāprāpya vā buddher viṣayatvena kalpyate ||
vadanti laukikā yac ca yādṛg jñānaṃ tathā bahiḥ | te punar jñānasaṃvittyā tathārthaṃ prati jānate ||
grāhakatvena vijñānaṃ yathārthaṃ naḥ samarpayet | tādṛgarthaḥ sa ityevaṃ teṣāṃ vā tadupāyataḥ ||
laiṅgikāsattvam aprāptair etair bāhyārthavādibhiḥ | jñānānubhavam utkramya bāhya eva pratīyate ||
yathā loke ca tadbuddhir vācyam evaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ | na yādṛgantarākāras tādṛg bāhyo 'vakalpate ||
utpadyamānā gṛhyeta dhīrarthagrahaṇe yadi | pūrvapakṣasya kiṃ siddham, kathaṃ cārthāntaraṃ vadet ||
bāhyārthavādinaṃ brūte bhavān kiṃ naivam icchati | pratibandho na tasyāsti gṛhṇātyarthāntaraṃ yadā ||
uttaraṃ grahakābhāvāl liṅgābhāvāc ca nāsti naḥ | tadā grahaṇam ity etat, anyatarkeṣu cocyate ||
teṣu tarkeṣu vijñānam arthakāle 'vagamyate | tathā satyarthanāśaḥ syād ity etadupadiśyate ||
nanv ity etadasambaddhaṃ pareṣṭasyaiva codanāt | paurvāparyavibhāgo 'pi prāguktena virudhyate ||
kṣaṇikatvena yuktaṃ syāj jñātatvam atha cet tadā | bhūtakālāśrayād brūyād, pṛthoktasya punarvacaḥ ||
atrāpi na svasiddhāntamūce vyājāt parasya tu | bhrāntatvād anyathā pakṣaṃ gṛhītveti sma pṛcchati ||
sahotpattyupalabdhā hi jñānasyaikāntataḥ sthitiḥ | prāgūrdhvaṃ vārthasaṃvitter yugapad veti cintyate ||
evaṃ cārthasya saṃvitteḥ paścāj jñānāvabodhanam | bravītu nūnam etasya paścād utpadyate 'pi tat ||
na caitac chaktyate tasmād utpatter apakarṣaṇam | karomi tāvat tatkālā saṃvittir api setsyati ||
prāk ca tadgrahaṇe siddhe bāhyābhyantarayor dhruvam | vivekādarśanam, tasmād idam, pūrvaṃ ca coditam ||
yugapad gṛhyamāṇe 'pi nākāro 'rthasya lakṣyate | tasmād arthasya saṃvittiḥ pūrvaṃ yatnena sādhyate ||
yas tv etasyottaro granthaḥ prāg evāsau nirūpitaḥ | na tv etat sādhanaṃ sākṣāt pūrvaṃ buddher abodhane ||
na parāmṛśyate 'rthātmā jñāto 'py ajñātavad yataḥ | tasān na grahaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ buddheḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam ||
ataḥ pūrvopalabdhyā yo buddhyākāro 'tra vāñchitaḥ | tannirākaraṇenaiva phalatvād granthavarṇanā ||
kāmaṃ buddher iti tv etadarthādhīnatvam ucyate | na cārtharūpād bhedena dhiyām asti nirūpaṇam ||
pararūpanirūpyaṃ ca na meyaṃ mṛgatoyavat | asadgrāhyānusāreṇa jñānasaṃvedyatā tava ||
svacchatvāt tu svarūpasya kalpitā grāhyatā dhiyām | vāsanopaplavāt tena na meyaṃ pāramārthikam ||
nimittaniyatatvaṃ tu samānam ubhayor api | nijaśaktyanusāritvāj jñānabāhyārthavādinoḥ ||
tantvarthair api kasmād vaḥ kriyate kevalaḥ paṭaḥ | nārabhyate ghaṭaḥ kiṃ tair mṛtpiṇḍārthena vā paṭaḥ ||
tantumṛtpiṇḍavijñāne hy anuyojye mate yadi | arthaparyanuyogo 'pi tadvad eva prasajyate ||
arthārambhavyavasthā cet sāmarthyaniyamāśrayā | jñānārambhavyavasthāyāṃ sāmarthyaṃ kena vāryate ||
tasmād yatrobhayor doṣaḥ parihāro 'pi vā samaḥ | naikaḥ paryanuyoktavyas tādṛgarthavicāraṇe ||
deśakālanimittāni vyañjakānyarthavādinaḥ | śaktīnāṃ kāraṇasthānāṃ svakāryaniyamaṃ prati ||
śaktayo 'pi ca bhāvānāṃ kāryārthāpattikalpitāḥ | prasiddhāḥ pāramārthikyaḥ pratikāryaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ||
bhavatas tu na vijñānād bhinnābhinnā nirūpyate | śaktiḥ saṃvṛtisadbhāvam utsṛjya paramārthataḥ ||
vāsanaiva ca yuṣmābhiḥ śaktiśabdena gīyate | nimittaniyatatvaṃ ca vāsanāyā yad ucyate ||
tasyāś cāsambhavenaitad apārārthyāc ca durlabham | deśakālanimittādi na ca te 'sti niyāmakam ||
matvaitad api cety āha bhāṣyakāraḥ paraṃ prati | tasmād aparihāro 'yaṃ tantubhyas te yathā paṭaḥ ||
tathā me tantubuddhibhyaḥ paṭabuddhir itīdṛśaḥ | evamādyapramāṇābhyāṃ na tāvad bāhyaśūnyatā ||
āgamasya tu naiveha vyāpāraḥ, ato 'nyathāpi vā | nopamā sadṛśābhāvāt, nārthāpattir viparyayāt ||
tasmād abhāvagamyatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sthitaṃ hi naḥ | evaṃ pramāṇato 'siddhā yaiḥ prameyāśrayocyate ||
bāhyasyāṇusamūhāder grāhyasyāsambhavekṣaṇāt ||
tairāntarāsambhavato yathoktād jñeyatvam anyasya balād upeyam | grāhyā na ceṣṭāḥ paramāṇavo 'taḥ satyaḥ samūhaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ ||
iti bahirviṣayapratipādanād tadabhāvakṛtā matisaṃvṛtiḥ | ubhayatattvavidāṃ paramārthataḥ, kṣamam idaṃ dhuri dharmavicāraṇe ||

§ 5,5 anumānapariccheda AMP

pratyakṣāvyabhicāritvād evaṃlakṣaṇakaṃ ca yat | prasiddham anumānādi na parīkṣyaṃ tad apy ataḥ ||
pramātā jñātasambandhaḥ, ekadeśyatha vocyate | karmadhārayapakṣo vā sambandhinyekadeśatā ||
dvayaṃ vā jñātasambandham upalabdhaṃ parasparam | tasyaikadeśaśabdābhyām ucyete samudāyinau ||
sambandho vyāptir iṣṭātra liṅgādharmasya liṅginā | vyāpyasya gamakatvaṃ ca vyāpakaṃ gamyam iṣyate ||
yo yasya deśakālābhyāṃ samo nyūno 'pi vā bhavet | sa vyāpyo vyāpakas tasya samo vābhyadhiko 'pi vā ||
tena vyāpye gṛhīte 'rthe vyāpakas tasya gṛhyate | na hy anyathā bhavaty eṣā vyāpyavyāpakatā tayoḥ ||
vyāpakatvagṛhītas tu vyāpyo yady api vastutaḥ | ādhikye 'py aviruddhatvād vyāpyaṃ na pratipādayet ||
vispaṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭam etac ca goviṣāṇitvayor mitau | vyāpyatvād gamikā gāvo vyāpikā na viṣāṇitā ||
tena yatrāpy ubhau dharmau vyāpyavyāpakasammatau | tatrāpi vyāpyataiva syād aṅgaṃ na vyāpitā miteḥ ||
tena dharmyantareṣv eṣā yasya yenaiva yādṛśī | deśe yāvati kāle vā vyāpyatā prāṅ nirūpitā ||
tasya tāvati tādṛk sa dṛṣṭo dharmyantare punaḥ | vyāpyāṃśo vyāpakāṃśasya tathaiva pratipādakaḥ ||
bhūyodarśanagamyā ca vyāptiḥ, sāmānyadharmayoḥ | jñāyate bhedahānena, kva cic cāpi viśeṣayoḥ ||
kṛttikodayamālakṣya rohiṇyāsattikḷptivat | vyāpteś ca dṛśyamānāyāḥ kaś cid dharmaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
asmin saty amunā bhāvyam iti śaktyā nirūpyate | anye paraprayuktānāṃ vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ ||
tair dṛṣṭair api naiveṣṭā vyāpakāṃśāvadhāraṇā | ye tu tān api visrabdhaṃ sādhyasiddhyau prayuñjate ||
sulabhaiḥ pratihetvādidoṣair bhrāmyanti te ciram | teṣv āgamaviruddhatvaṃ svayaṃ ceṣṭavighātitā ||
alaukikavivādāś ca varṇyas te haitukais tataḥ | niṣiddhitvena hiṃsānām adharmatvaṃ prayujyate ||
tadabhāve na tatsiddhir hiṃsātvād aprayojakāt | hetudvayaprayukte ca mithyātve sarvabuddhiṣu ||
jñānatvotpattimattvādisādhako naprayojakaḥ | traivarṇikaprayuktā ca yāgādeḥ svargahetutā ||
na manuṣyatvamātreṇa śūdrasthena prayujyate | kṛtasāvayavatvādiprayuktā ca vināśitā ||
prayatnānantarajñānasadṛśair na prayujyate | jātimattvendriyatvādi vastusanmātrabandhanam ||
śadānityatvasiddhyarthaṃ ko vaded yo na tārkikaḥ | tasmād ya eva yasyārtho dṛṣṭaḥ sādhanaśaktitaḥ ||
sa eva gamakas tasya na prasaṅgānvito 'pi yaḥ | upāttaś caikadeśābhyāṃ dharmy apy atraikadeśatā ||
apārārthye hi dhūmādeḥ svarūpair naikadeśatā | sa eva cobhayātmāyaṃ gamyo gamaka eva vā ||
asiddhenaikadeśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ | ataḥ pṛthagabhinno vāprayoktāṇāṃ vivakṣaya ||
anityaḥ kṛtako yasmād dhūmavān agnimān iti | dharmyabhinnam upādānam, bhedo 'trāgnir itīdṛśe ||
ekadeśaviśiṣṭaś ca dharmyevātrānumīyate | na hi tannirapekṣatve sambhavaty anumeyatā ||
na dharmamātraṃ siddhatvāt, tathā dharmī, tathobhayam | vyastaṃ vāpi samastaṃ vā svātantryeṇānumīyate ||
ekadeśasya liṅgatvaṃ sādhyenānugamo 'sya ca | dvayaṃ ca na syād iṣṭaṃ sat pakṣeṣv eṣu yathākramam ||
anityatvādayo dharmāḥ kṛtakatvādayo na hi | dhvaninānugamo naiṣāṃ nobhayasyobhayena vā ||
sambandho 'py anupādānān nāmnā ṣaṣṭhyāpi vā mitau | na cāpy anugamas tena liṅgasyeha nidarśyate ||
na cākāradvayaṃ tasya sādhyasādhanabhāg bhavet | tasmad arthagṛhītatvānmatubarthasya gamyatā ||
na svāntantryeṇa mantavyā, yathā daṇḍyādiśabdataḥ | viśīṣṭārthapratītau syāt sambandho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvam āpannau dvāv imāv ataḥ | gamyau, aṅgāṅgibhāvas tu kaiś cid iṣṭo vikalpataḥ ||
sarvathā dharmiṇo dharmo dharmeṇa tv avagamyate | viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve na viśeṣo 'vadhāryate ||
tatrotaraṃ vadanty anye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam | hetudharmeṇa sambandhas tasyāprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
pradhānatvād dhi dharmeṇa sambandho vākyato bhavet | tatrāsambhavataḥ paścāt kalpyo 'sau dharminā saha ||
dhvaner ity atha vā vācyam, anvayasya tu darśane | bhedopāttasya dharmasya guṇābhāvo na duṣyati ||
agner deśaviśiṣṭatve na caitat pakṣalakṣaṇam | viśiṣṭatāsya deśena bhaved evamprakārikā ||
yo 'gniḥ so 'sti kva cid deśe yo dṛṣṭo yatra tatra vā | agniḥ pūrvānubhūto vā deśamātreṇa saṅgataḥ ||
yo 'gniḥ so 'nena yukto vā, yo dṛṣṭo 'nena so 'tha vā | yo 'yaṃ sa deśamātreṇa yuktaḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy ayam ||
etaddeśaviśiṣṭo vā yo 'yam agnir iti, iha tu | pūrvayoḥ siddhasādhyatvaṃ pareṣu syād viruddhatā ||
vyāptir etena deśena sarvāgnīnāṃ na yujyate | nāpi pūrvasya, nāpy eṣa vahniḥ sarvair viśiṣyate ||
deśaiḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy asya na deśena viśeṣyatā | etaddeśaviśiṣṭo 'yam ity etat kathyate katham ||
yadā deśānapekṣo 'gnir nāyam ity avadhāryate | agneḥ pūrvataraṃ cātra deśa evāvadhāryate ||
tajjñānakālabuddhaś ca na deśaḥ syād viśeṣaṇam | deśasya parvatādes tu svarūpe pāvakād ṛte ||
gṛhīte 'gniviśiṣṭasya punarjñānaṃ na duṣyati | tasmād dharmaviśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā ||
sā deśasyāgniyuktasya, dhūmasyānyaiś ca kalpitā | nanu śabdavad eva syāl liṅgagamyaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
naivam, na hy atra liṅgasya śaktyanekatvakalpanā | na ca tasyānumeyatvam, viśeṣyaś cāvadhāritaḥ ||
viśiṣṭatvena cājñānāt tanmātrasyānumeyatā | nanu dhūmaviśeṣyatve hetoḥ pakṣaikadeśatā ||
naitad asti, viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānyahetutā | dhūmatajjānasambandhasmṛtiprāmāṇyakalpane ||
phalena viṣayaikatvaṃ tadvyāpārāt puroditam | prameyadhīpramāṇatvaṃ bhāṣyakāras tu manyate ||
pratyakṣāniyamoktaś ca sarvatraivānuṣajyate | anumānagṛhītasya tenaiva pratipādanam ||
parebhyo vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrvapakṣo yathoditaḥ | tatra dharmiṇam uddiśya sādhyadharmo vidhīyate ||
niyamas tadvipakṣāc ca kalpyate nāvirodhinaḥ | asannikṛṣṭavācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam ||
tādrūpyeṇa paricchittis tadviparyayato 'pi ca | pramitasya pramāṇe hi nāpekṣā jāyate punaḥ ||
tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇaṃ niṣphalaṃ param | vaiparītyaparicchinne nāvakāśaḥ parasya tu ||
mūle tasya hy anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayo hṛtaḥ | pratyakṣādeś ca ṣaṭkasya yenaivārtho 'vadhāritaḥ ||
tenaivottarabādhaḥ syād, vikalpāder asambhavāt | agrāhyatā tu śabdādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate ||
teṣām aśrāvaṇatvādi viruddham anumānataḥ | na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇāvagamyate ||
sānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ gamyate badhirādiṣu | tridhā śabdavirodhaḥ syāt pratijñādivibhāgataḥ ||
pratijñāpūrvasañjalpasarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ | yāvajjīvam ahaṃ maunīty uktimātreṇa bādhyate ||
sarvavākyamṛṣātve tu dharmoktyaivātmabādhanam | dharmyuktyāhaṃ yato jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama ||
bauddhasya śabdanityatvaṃ pūrvopetena bādhyate | candraśabdābhidheyatvaṃ śaśino yo niṣedhati ||
sa sarvalokasiddhena candrajñānena bādhyate | jñātagogavayākāraṃ prati yaḥ sādhayed idam ||
na gor gavayasādṛśyaṃ tasya bādhopamānataḥ | gehāvagatanāstitvo jīvaṃś caitro yadā bahiḥ ||
nāstīti sādhyate bādhas tatrārthāpattito bhavet | agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde cānabhidhāyake ||
śrotrādināstitāyāṃ ca śabdānityatvasādhane | śrutārthāpattibādho 'tra yadāptoktinivārite ||
divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātribhojanam | śaśaśṛṅgādisadbhāvavirodho 'nupalabdhitaḥ ||
evaṃ ca dharmasambandhabādhas tāvad udāhṛtaḥ | dharmadharmyubhayeṣāṃ ca svarūpasvaviśeṣayoḥ ||
śrutyarthākṣiptayor vākye vācyaḥ sarvapramāṇakaḥ | tṛṇādivikriyāhetor agnimaddhimasādhane ||
pratyakṣāvagatāc chaityāt tadviśeṣotthabādhanam | adharmo vihito duḥkhaṃ karotyalpam itīha tu ||
vihitatvād adharmasya svarūpasyaiva bādhanam | tathā duḥkhanimittatvaṃ viśeṣas tasya bādhyate ||
ayathārthā dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ ity ukte dvayabādhanam | svarūpasvaviśeṣābhyām, taddhīmithyātvasādhanāt ||
kṣaṇikātyantamithyātve viśeṣau ca dvayor iha | darśanād ekadeśasyety anenaitad vyudasyate ||
yatraikasyobhayor vāpi saṃśayādhīviparyayāḥ | śaityān na dāhako bahniś cākṣuṣatvād anityatā ||
śabdasyetyevamādau tu dvayoḥ siddho viparyayaḥ | kṛtakatvaguṇatvādau parokte yājñikaṃ prati ||
svokte caivamprakāre syād asiddho 'nyatarasya tu | bāṣpādibhāvasandigdho dvayor anyatarasya vā ||
dhūmas tridhāpy asiddhaḥ syāt, evaṃ tāvat svarūpataḥ | eta eva prakārāḥ syur āśrayāsiddhikalpane ||
jñāte 'pi hi svarūpeṇa nātaddharme 'sti hetutā | sarvatra dṛṣṭakāryatvād ātmā sarvagatas tv iti ||
bauddhaṃ pratyāśrayāsiddhaḥ, laukikādes tu saṃśayaḥ | bāṅmātrāsiddhimātreṇa vyavahārāprakalpanāt ||
dvābhyāṃ yo 'sattvato jñātas tadvaco dūṣaṇaṃ matam | itarat sādhanaṃ tu syād vādinā yadi sādhyate ||
nirākaraṇasiddhau vā dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ | sandehaviparītatvahetū cātra nirākṛtau ||
jñātasambandhavacanāt, trayaḥ saṃśayahetavaḥ | san sādhye tadabhāve vā dvābhyāṃ vyāvṛtta eva ca ||
dvau viruddhārthasambaddhau yāv ekatraikadeśini | prameyānityatāmūrtidharmāḥ sādhāraṇā dvayoḥ ||
nityāyatnotthayatnotthānityeṣu dviranityataḥ | nityā bhūrgandhavattvena syād asādhāraṇas tvayam ||
niścayaikāṅgavaikalyād eṣa saṃśayakāraṇam | sādhāraṇo yathā dṛṣṭo buddhidvayanimittakaḥ ||
viruddhaikānavāpteś ca saṃśaye kāraṇaṃ matam | atrāsādhāraṇo nāsti tadabhāvamukhena tu ||
dvayāsattvavirodhāc ca mataḥ saṃśayakāraṇam | sandigdhahetutā caiṣāṃ viṣayāpekṣayocyate ||
nirṇayasyāpi hetutvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sādhyāntare yataḥ | vyavacchedānvayau labdhvā, niṣkriyādāv amūrtivat ||
kṣityekadeśasiddhatve gandhavattvasya hetutā | yatrāpratyakṣatā vāyor arūpatvena sādhyate ||
sparśāt pratyakṣatā vāsau viruddhāvyabhicāritā | ke cij jātyantaraṃ caināṃ varṇayantyapare punaḥ ||
sādhāraṇatvam aṃśena samastaṃ vāpy ananvayam | pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrvoktair yasya sādhanaiḥ ||
tat parājayataḥ kāryo nirṇayo bādhavarjanāt | kva cit saṃśayahetū yau pratyekatvena lakṣitau ||
saṅghāte nirṇayas tābhyāmūrdhvatākākavattvavat | pratyekaṃ saṃhatau vāpi gamakāvavirodhinau ||
tasmād bhinnau viruddhārthau hetū cātra nidarśitau | ṣoḍhā viruddhatām āhuś caturddhā vaikadhāpi vā ||
śrutyarthoktasya bādhāyāṃ pratijñārthasya hetunā | nityatve kṛtakatvasya dharmabādhād viruddhatā ||
bādho dharmaviśeṣasya yadā tv evaṃ prayujyate | arthavacchabdarūpaṃ syāt prāksambandhāvadhāraṇāt ||
vibhaktimattvāt paścādvat svarūpeṇeti cāśrite | asvarūpārthayogas tu paścāc chabdasya dṛśyate ||
tena prāg api sambandhād asvarūpārthatā bhavet | ihapratyayahetutvād dravyāder vyatiricyate ||
samavāyo yathehāyaṃ ghaṭa ityādisaṅgatiḥ | atrāpy asamavāyatvaṃ saṃyogasyeva sidhyati ||
tena dharmisvarūpasya vaiparītyād viruddhatā | yac ca sattāvad ekatvaṃ samavāyasya kalpitam ||
tatra saṃyogavadbhedāt syād viśeṣaviruddhatā | nityam ātmāstitā kaiś cid yadā sautrāntikaṃ prati ||
sādhyate 'vayavābhāvād vyomavad dvayabādhanam | tadobhayaviśeṣasya bādho 'yaṃ sādhyate yadā ||
pārārthyaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ saṅghātāc chayanādivat | śayane saṅghapārārthyaṃ bhautikavyāptahetuke ||
ātmānaṃ prati pārārthyam asiddham iti bādhanam | asaṃhataparārthatve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatāpi ca ||
anahaṅkārikatvaṃ ca cakṣurādeḥ prasajyate | gamakasyaikadeśasya vyāptir gamyeti bhāṣitum ||
sādhyasādharmyavaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate | tatra hetvartham uddiśya sādhyopādānam iṣyate ||
uddeśyo vyāpyate dharmo vyāpakaś cetaro mataḥ | yadvṛttayogaḥ prāthamyam ity ādyuddeśalakṣaṇam ||
tadvṛttam eva kāraś ca syād upādeyalakṣaṇam | vadatyarthaṃ svaśaktyā ca śabdo vaktranapekṣayā ||
sādhyahetutvam arthānāṃ vyāptiśaktyanurodhataḥ | tatrājñānād yadā vakta sahacāravivakṣayā ||
viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāptatvaṃ vivakṣati | vivakṣann api vā śabdaṃ tadyogyaṃ na vaded yadi ||
ghaṭe kṛtakanāśitve nāśivyāptaṃ kṛtena vā | na tadeṣṭasya hetutvam, syād aniṣṭasya caiva tat ||
tasmād vyāpyatvarūpeṇa vācyo hetutvasammataḥ | yadā samyak prayukte 'pi vākye 'rtho na tathā bhavet ||
sādhyahetūbhayavyāptiśūnyatvāt paramārthataḥ | nityo dhvaniramūrttatvāt karmavat paramāṇuvat ||
ghaṭavad vyomavaccāpi, tadasadvādinaṃ prati | dharmyasiddhāv api hy evaṃ dṛṣṭāntābhāsatā bhavet ||
tat sadbhāve 'pi ca vyomni dvayayukte 'pi kīrtite | karmādyālocanād vyāptir hetor nāstīti varjanam ||
vyāptyā sādharmya ukte ca na vaidharmyam apekṣyate | sahabhāvitvadṛṣṭyā tu yadā vyāptiṃ na lakṣayet ||
paraḥ sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt tac ca nāpekṣate yadā | vaktā vā sahabhāvitvaṃ śuddhaṃ tena vaded yadā ||
viparītānvayaṃ vāpi tat samādhitsayā tadā | pūrvajñānopamardena vaidharmyeṇeṣṭasādhanam ||
sāhityamātraṃ pūrvoktaṃ hetos tatropayujyate | vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo hi bhāvayor yādṛg iṣyate ||
tayor abhāvayos tasmād viparītaḥ pratīyate | dhūmabhāve 'gnibhāvena vyāpte 'nagnis tataś cyutaḥ ||
adhūma eva vidyetetyevaṃ vyāpyatvamaśnute | tathānagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmas tatacyutaḥ ||
anyatrānavakāśatvād vyāpyate dhruvam agninā | vyāpakau tu yadocyete bhāvābhāvau tadā tataḥ ||
naiva vyāpyād vipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet | tasmād dhūmena sādhyatvam agneḥ prārthayate yadā ||
tadānagnir adhūmena vyāpto vācyaḥ, na cānyathā | anagnyadhūmasāhitye vyāpter vāpi viparyaye ||
na prastutopakāraḥ syād anyad vāpi prasādhyate | yatrāpy arthasya śūnyatvaṃ dvābhyām ekena vā bhavet ||
yad anityaṃ tu tan mūrtam aṇuvad buddhivat khavat | sādhyena vyāptisiddhyaiva vyatireko 'tra kathyate ||
yasyāyaṃ nāsty asau hetus tena sādhyena nāpyate | tena dṛṣṭe 'pi sāhitye na sarvo gamya iṣyate ||
sahadṛṣṭir na sambandho vyāptir naiva ca tāvatā | mūrtānityatvayukte 'pi tasmād aṅgīkṛte ghaṭe ||
karmādau vyāptyabhāvena na dṛṣṭāntatvam iṣyate | aśeṣāpekṣitatvāc ca saukaryāc cāpy adarśanāt ||
sādhane yadyapīṣṭo 'tra vyatireko 'numāṃ prati | tāvatā na hy anaṅgatvaṃ yuktiḥ śābde hi vakṣyate ||
bodhaprasaṅgo bhedānāṃ na cāvyāpter bhaviṣyati | astisāmānyavastveṣu vyāpitā tatra gamyatām ||
ke cit sādharmyadṛṣṭānte vyāptyāpi kathite punaḥ | vaidharmyoktim apīcchanti, vyāvṛttiniyamecchayā ||
hetau sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt sādhyenaivāvadhārite | vyāvṛttiḥ sarvataḥ prāptā sādhyābhāve niyamyate ||
tat tu mandaphalaṃ yasmāt pakṣe 'py evaṃ nirūpitam | vyāpakābhāvamātraṃ hi vyāpyān nityaṃ nivartate ||
tasmād yathaiva śuklatve paṭasyokte virodhinām | nivṛttir na tu dairdhyādes tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
dvaividhyaṃ nopapannaṃ tu yathaiva hy agnidhūmayoḥ | pratyakṣadṛṣṭaḥ sambandho gatiprāptyos tathaiva hi ||
āditye 'nupalabdhiś cen na deśe 'py adhunātane | kva cit tatropalabdhiś ced devadatte 'pi dṛśyatām ||
yadi dharmyantarāpekṣā tatra sāmānyadṛṣṭatā | syād agnidhūmayoḥ saiva, tasmād evaṃ pracakṣate ||
pratyakṣadṛṣṭasambandhaṃ yayor eva viśeṣayoḥ | gomayendhanatajjanyaviśeṣādimatiḥ kṛtā ||
taddeśasthena tenaiva gatvā kālāntare 'pi tam | yadāgnir budhyate, tasya pūrvabodhāt punaḥ punaḥ ||
sandihyamānasadbhāvavastubodhāt pramāṇatā | viśeṣadṛṣṭam etac ca likhitaṃ vindhyavāsinā ||
ākṛtyor eva caiṣeṣṭā vyavacchedena kena cit | hetusādhyavyavastheti viśeṣo nopadarśitaḥ ||
agnidhūmāntaratve ca vācye sāmānyato mitau | sāmānyadṛṣṭam ekāntād atretyāditya ucyate ||
pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ ca sāmānyasya prasādhitam | vastutvaṃ ca, atra hetur vā dvayasyāpy abhidhīyate ||
dhūmād agnyanumānasya vastvālambanatā bhavet | abhāvānyapramāṇatvāt svārthe śrotrādibuddhivat ||
sāmānyasya ca vastutvaṃ pratyakṣagrāhyatāpi ca | abhāvānyaprameyatvād asādhāraṇavastuvat ||
sāmānyaṃ nānumānena vinā yasya pratīyate | na ca liṅgavinirmuktam anumānaṃ pravartate ||
asāmānyasya liṅgatvaṃ na ca kena cid iṣyate | na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ kiñ cid asti prakāśakam ||
tasya vāpy anumānena syād anyena gatiḥ punaḥ | tadutpattiś ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānyajñānasaṃhitāt ||
tasya cāpy anumānatvāt bhavel liṅgena codbhavaḥ | anumānāntarād eva jñānenaivaṃ ca kalpane ||
liṅgaliṅgyanumānānām ānantyād ekaliṅgini | gatir yugasahasreṣu bahuṣv api na vidyate ||
atha sāmānyabhūte 'pi liṅge 'nyasmād gatir bhavet | pramāṇād apramāṇād vā, tathā liṅgigatir bhavet ||
evam apy anumānasya nityocchedaḥ prasajyate | pramāṇāntaram eva syāt sāmānyasyāvabodhakam ||
apramāṇāvabuddhād vā liṅgāl liṅgini yā matiḥ | sāpi mithyā bhaven nityaṃ bāṣpajātāgnibuddhivat ||
nanv apramāṇabhūtāpi sambandhasmṛtir iṣyate | yathā liṅgigatau hetus tathā liṅgagatir bhavet ||
tatra yat pūrvavijñānaṃ tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate | tadupasthānamātreṇa smṛteḥ syāc caritārthatā ||
na tu liṅgagatau kiñ cit pramāṇam upapadyate | tadabhāvāsmṛtiś cātra na kathañ cit pravartate ||
smārtam etadabhedena vijñānam iti yo vadet | tasya vandhyāsute 'py asti nūnaṃ smaraṇaśaktatā ||
na cāsādhāraṇo 'rthātmā sāmānyajñānakāraṇam | yasmān nāsyāvinābhāvas tena dṛṣṭaḥ kathañ cana ||
syād vā sambandhadṛṣṭyāsau sāmānyaṃ kṛtakatvavat | na hy asādhāraṇaṃ vastu pūrvatreha ca vidyate ||
na cāpy avyapadeśasya vikalparahitasya ca | vinā pūrvānusandhānāl liṅgatvam upapadyate ||
kalpyante ca viśeṣā ye te 'py aliṅgam ananvayāt | etasmād eva hetoḥ syāt tajñānasyāpy aliṅgatā ||
sāmānyarūpatāyāṃ vā tathaivānavadhāraṇam | kva cid vā dṛṣṭasambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyako bhavet ||
sambandhānubhavo 'vaśyam eṣitavyaś ca liṅganaḥ | anumānapravṛttes tu prāg jñānaṃ tatra nāsti te ||
na cāpi vāsanāmātrāl liṅgajñānasya sambhavaḥ | liṅgijñānaṃ ca tadvat syāt trirūpāl liṅgato na tat ||
tatrābhāvasya liṅgatvaṃ na cāsāv ānumānikaḥ | pramāṇāntaragamyatvāt tatra doṣo na jāyate ||
pratyakṣāvagatāl liṅgād yasya liṅgigatir bhavet | tasya nāto 'dhikaṃ kiñ cit prārthanīyaṃ prasajyate ||
yatrāpy anumitāl liṅgāl liṅgini grahaṇaṃ bhavet | tatrāpi maulikaṃ liṅgaṃ pratyakṣād eva gamyate ||
liṅgatvaṃ kṛtakatvādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā | pratyakṣatvaṃ ca tasyeṣṭam iti dūraṃ na gamyate ||
evaṃ śabdopamānādau sāmānyāśrayatā yataḥ | taddaussthityena daussthityaṃ sarvatrātaḥ prasajyate ||
tasmāt pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ pramāṇāntara iṣyate | pratyakṣatvaṃ ca sāmānye nānyathā hi gatir bhavet ||
pratyakṣālambanatvaṃ ca viśeṣasya kathaṃ bhavet | yadā vastvantarāpekṣaḥ sāmānyāṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate ||
rūpādayo hi sāmānyaṃ sarve nīlādyapekṣayā | svaviśeṣānapekṣyātha nīlādīnāṃ samānatā ||
te cāpi tāvat sāmānyaṃ yāvat syuḥ paramāṇavaḥ | dvyaṇukasyāpi yadrūpaṃ tad dhi sādhāraṇaṃ dvayoḥ ||
na cāntyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāro 'sti kasya cit | na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā ||
bhedenāgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedo grāhyatāṃ vrajet | na ca bhinneṣv abhinnatvabuddher grāhyatvasambhavaḥ ||
samudāyo na vāpy asti bhavatāṃ na ca sarvadā | sarveṣām asatārthena pratyayotpattisambhavaḥ ||
na caikajātiyogena vināsti samudāyatā | samudāye 'pi cāṇutvaṃ naiteṣām apagacchati ||
sāmānyam ity adṛśye 'pi tena sāmānya eva naḥ | vyāsaṅginī bhavaty eṣā dhīrvināpy ekakalpanāt ||
vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathendriyaiḥ | grahaṇaṃ tadvad eva syāt prativyaktiniveśinaḥ ||
mīmāṃsakaiś ca nāvaśyam iṣyante paramāṇavaḥ | yadbalenopalabdhasya mithyātvaṃ kalpayed bhavān ||
samūharūpaṃ pratyakṣam adṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ | yo 'pahnute śaśasyāpi so 'bhāvaṃ śṛṅgato vadet ||
samūhaparamārthatve sthite tatsiddhihetukā | yadi nāmāvagamyeta paramāṇvastitā punaḥ ||
tasmād yad gṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā | tat tathaivābhyupetavyaṃ sāmānyam atha vetarat ||
sattādisāmānyam apekṣya sarvaṃ gotvādi sādhāraṇatām upaiti | tasmād asādhāraṇam akṣagamyaṃ vadan na sāmānyam apahnuvīta ||
sāmānyarūpeṇa na gṛhyate cet, kiṃ vāstyasādhāraṇabuddhir atra | yadvastu lokaḥ pratipadyate 'smin dvidhāpi tacchaktyata eva vaktum ||

§ 5,6 śabdapariccheda SBP

pratyakṣādiṣu vaktavyaṃ śabdamātrasya lakṣaṇam | adatitvariteneha kiṃ śāstrād abhidhīyate ||
sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tyaktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇam | na śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktum ito 'py asya na vācyatā ||
yac coktaṃ śabdavijñānād arthe jñānam itīdṛśam | aviśiṣṭaṃ viśiṣṭasya na tacchāstrasya lakṣaṇam ||
pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā nityena kṛtakena vā | puṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tacchāstram abhidhīyate ||
svarūpakathanaṃ yat tu kasya cit tatra dṛśyate | tadaṅgatvena tasyāpi śāstratvam avagamyate ||
bhāvanāyāṃ samastāyāṃ vākyād evopajāyate | pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā tacchāstraṃ na padād yataḥ ||
aparīkṣāmiṣeṇāpi lakṣaṇāni vadannayam | na svatantropayogitvanirapekṣāṇi jalpati ||
tatra yallokavākyasthaṃ kathayecchabdalakṣaṇam | vedaṃ vyākhyātukāmasya tannātīvopayujyate ||
pratyakṣādyupayogaṃ tu varṇamātrāditaḥ puraḥ | śāstrārthajñānavelāyāṃ matvā tallakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam ||
yat tu gāmānayetyādivākyasthaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam | tasya nehopayogo 'sti tasmāc chāstragataṃ kṛtam ||
veśeṣaś ca na sāmānyam antareṇāsti kaś cana | tasmāt tam apy udāhṛtya sāmānyaṃ lakṣayet sukham ||
sāmānyarūpam apy etadadhikārād viśiṣyate | codanā copadeśaś ca śāstram evety udāhṛtam ||
yathā ca codanāśabdo vaidikyām eva vartate | śabdajñānārthavijñānaśabdau śāstre tathā sthitau ||
pratyakṣādyaparīkṣyatve tadantarbhāvahetukam | śāstrasyāpy aparīkṣyatvamanayaiva dhiyoditam ||
tatrānumānam evedaṃ bauddhair vaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam | bhedaḥ sāṃkhyādibhis tv iṣṭo na tūktaṃ bhedakāraṇam ||
pūrvasaṃskārayuktāntyavarṇavākyādikalpanā | vivakṣādi ca dhūmādau nāstīty etena bhinnatā ||
yair uktā tatra vaidharmyavikalpasamajātitā | dhūmānityaviṣāṇyādiviśeṣān na hi bhinnatā ||
tailakṣaṇyaparityāgo yāvan na pratipādyate | tāvad viśeṣamātreṇa vadato jātitā bhavet ||
yatheṣṭaviniyogena pratītir yāpi śabdataḥ | na dhūmāder itīhāpi vyabhicāro 'ṅgavṛttibhiḥ ||
hastasaṃjñādayo ye 'pi yadarthapratipādane | bhaveyuḥ kṛtasaṅketāste na liṅgam iti sthitiḥ ||
puruṣākṣiptatāyāṃ ca tathaiva vyabhicāritā | padavaidikavākyānāṃ na satyavyāpitā bhavet ||
sambandhātubhavaś cāyaṃ so 'nyatrāpi vilakṣaṇaḥ | etasmin puruṣāpekṣā deśāpekṣāgnidhūmayoḥ ||
kālādyapekṣayā cānyaḥ, uktā cānyair abhinnatā | āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyād anumānataḥ ||
na cāpūrvādiśabdānāṃ bhedāt sarvatra bhinnatā | na cehāśvādiśabdebhyo bhedas teṣāṃ pratīyate ||
na cāpy ajñātasambandhaṃ padaṃ kiñ cit prakāśakam | sambandhān anubhūtyāto na syād ananumānatā ||
tulyākāratayāpy atra śabdajñānārthataddhiyām | agnidhūmeṣv adṛṣṭatvān na bhedas tannivāraṇāt ||
pratibimbeṣv anaikānto bimbaṃ yādṛgghi darpaṇe | tādṛṅ mukhādi budhyante, na cātrānanumānatā ||
pratyakṣatā tadāpy atra tadānyair vyabhicāritā | yatra pādādi bambena gatānām anumīyate ||
ekavākyāt sakṛc coktān nāpy anekasya tatkṣaṇam | syād viruddhāviruddhasya bodhād etasya bhinnatā ||
liṅgasyāpi hi tādrūpyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetuviruddhayoḥ | virodhān nānumānaṃ cet, syād anāgamatāpi te ||
yatra caikārthatā vākye tatra syād anumānatā | sakṛduccarite cāsmin vivakṣaikaiva dṛśyate ||
yas tv anirdhāritārthānām anekapratibhodbhavaḥ | sa liṅge 'py asphuṭe dṛṣṭas tasmān naitena bhidyate ||
dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam | prasiddhatvād dhi tatrāpi na dṛṣṭānto 'bhidhīyate ||
anabhyas te tv apekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim | atra pratyukta ity evaṃ budhyante hi cirāt kva cit ||
paroktā hetavaś cātra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ | śabdānumānayor aikyaṃ dhūmād agnyanumānavat ||
anvayavyatirekābhyām ekapratyakṣadarśanāt | sambandhapūrvakatvāc ca pratipattir ito yataḥ ||
pratyakṣānyapramāṇatvāt tadadṛṣṭārthabodhanāt | sāmānyaviṣayatvāc ca traikālyaviṣayāśrayāt ||
kaiś cin mīmāṃsakair ukto bhedo 'tra viṣayāntarāt | pūrvābhyāṃ hy aparicchinne śāstram arthe pravartate ||
tatrāpi nāgamatvaṃ syāt puruṣokte, tathās tu cet | pratyayaḥ kin nimitto 'rthe, vaktṛbuddheḥ, kuto nv asau ||
na śabdārthasya sāliṅgaṃ na śabdo 'syāḥ kathañ cana | viśeṣo gamyate tābhyāṃ na caitasyānumeyatā ||
tena vaktur abhiprāye pratyakṣādyanirūpite | puruṣoktir api śroturāgamatvaṃ prapadyate ||
na cāpy ananumeyatvam āgamārthasya śakyate | liṅgaṃ hi śabda evāsya dhūmo 'gner iva kalpyate ||
na cāpy ananumeyatvāt pramāṇāntaragamyatā | rūpasyāśrāvaṇatvena na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||
evaṃ sati svayūthyā na ke cin nātiprapañcinaḥ | anumānaviśeṣo 'yam īdṛg dharmasya bodhakaḥ ||
bhaviṣyatyartharūpaṃ tu liṅgaṃ dharme nirākṛtam | saṃjñānumānatecchā tu na duṣyedāgame 'pi naḥ ||
lakṣaṇena tv abhinnatvaṃ yadi śabdānumānayoḥ | vedajñānāpramāṇatvaṃ syād atallakṣaṇatvataḥ ||
āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyān nṛvacassu hi | lakṣaṇenānumānatvāt prāmāṇyaṃ siddhimṛcchati ||
vede tv āptanarābhāvāt sambandhānubhavād ṛte | lakṣaṇaṃ nānumānasyety aprāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate ||
nanv ekadeśasatyatve tasya syād anumānatā | vedatvād agnihotrādau vāyukṣepiṣṭhavākyavat ||
nādityayūpe 'naikāntāt, tadvad vā gauṇatā bhavet | nātaḥ pratyanumānānām evaṃ pūrvoktayā viśā ||
tasmāl lakṣaṇabhedena yadi śabdapramāṇatā | samā loke ca vede ca siddhā vedapramāṇatā ||
tena cāptopadeśatvaṃ na syād āgamalakṣaṇam | nāptasya sambhavo vede, loke nāsmāt pramāṇatā ||
purastād varṇitaṃ hy etat, tasmāc chabdena yā matiḥ | tasyāḥ svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ na cet syād doṣadarśanam ||
anumānena caitasya prāmāṇyaṃ kevalaṃ samam | pade tāvat kṛto yatnaḥ parair ity atra varṇyate ||
viṣayo 'nyādṛśas tāvad dṛśyate liṅgaśabdayoḥ | sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca padasya sthāpayiṣyati ||
dharmādharmaviśiṣṭaś ca liṅgīty etac ca sādhitam | na tāvad anumānaṃ hi yāvat tadviṣayaṃ na tat ||
sāmānyād atiriktaṃ tu śābde vākyasya gocaraḥ | sāmarthyād anumeyatvād aśrute 'pi padāntare ||
saṃkhyādimān padārthaś cet, na tāvat so 'vyayādiṣu | yatrāpi te pratīyante tatra vyakter viśeṣaṇam ||
padāntarābhidheyasya tādarthyāc ca kriyātmanaḥ | vākyārthe 'pi padaṃ yatra gomadādi prayujyate ||
saty apy atra viśeṣṭatve siddhatvān naiva pakṣatā | tāvān eva hi tatrārtho yaḥ pūrvam avadhāritaḥ ||
bhedabuddheś ca vaiṣamyaṃ prakṛtipratyayārthayoḥ | viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyārthasvātantryagrahaṇaṃ na ca ||
viśeṣyapūrvikā tatra buddhiś cātra viparyayaḥ | atha śabdo 'rthavattvena pakṣaḥ kasmān na kalpyate ||
pratijñārthaikadeśo hi hetus tatra prasajyate | pakṣe dhūmaviśeṣe ca sāmānyaṃ hetur iṣyate ||
śabdatvaṃ gamakaṃ nātra gośabdatvaṃ niṣetsyate | vyaktir eva viśiṣyāto hetuś caikā prasajyate ||
bhaved vyañjakabhedāc cet, na tv evaṃ pratyayo 'sti naḥ | kathaṃ cāsya viśiṣṭatvaṃ na tāvad deśakālataḥ ||
tatpratītiviśiṣṭaś cet, paraṃ kim anumīyate | na pratyāyanaśaktiś ca viśeṣasyānumīyate ||
viśeṣāṇāṃ na śaktir hi saikadeśe 'gnijātivat | sāmānyasyaiva śaktatvaṃ pakṣo hetus tad eva ca ||
tasmād arthaviśiṣṭasya na śabdasyānumeyatā | kathaṃ ca pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyeha nirūpyate ||
na kriyākartṛsambandhād ṛte sambandhanaṃ kva cit | rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ sa ucyate ||
vṛkṣas tiṣṭhati śākhāsu tā vā tatreti tasya tāḥ | deśe 'gnimati dhūmasya kartṛtvaṃ bhavanaṃ prati ||
kāryakāraṇabhāvādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate | na cānavagatākāraḥ sambandho 'stīti gamyate ||
na cāsty asati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo 'pi vā | tasmān na pakṣadharmo 'yam iti śakyā nirūpaṇā ||
nivṛtte 'nyatra sambandhe ye 'pi tadviṣayātmanā | vadeyuḥ pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyānupalabdhivat ||
tair apy etannirūpyaṃ tu śabdas tadviṣayaḥ katham | na taddeśādisadbhāvo nābhimukhyādi tasya vā ||
tasmād utpādayaty eṣa yato 'rthaviṣayā matim | tena tadviṣayaḥ śabda iti dharmatvakalpanā ||
tatra vācakatāyāṃ ca siddhāyāṃ pakṣadharmatā | na pratītyaṅgatāṃ gacchen na caivam anumānatā ||
gamakatvāc ca dharmatvaṃ dharmatvād gamako yadi | syād anyonyāśrayatvaṃ hi tasmān naiṣāpi kalpanā ||
na cāgṛhītasambandhāḥ svarūpavyatirekataḥ | śabdaṃ jānanti yenātra pakṣadharmamatir bhavet ||
na ca svarūpamātreṇa dhūmādeḥ pakṣadharmatā | na cāpi pūrvasambandham apekṣyaiṣā prasajyate ||
dhūmavān ayam ity evam apūrvasyāpi jāyate | pakṣadharmamatiḥ, tena bhidyetottaralakṣaṇāt ||
na tv atra pūrvasambandhād adhikā pakṣadharmatā | na cārthapratyayāt pūrvam ity anaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
na ca dharmī gṛhīto 'tra yena taddharmatā bhavet | parvatādir yathā deśaḥ prāgdharmatvāvadhāraṇāt ||
yaś cātra kathyate dharmī prameyo 'sya sa eva naḥ | na cānavadhṛte tasmiṃs taddharmatvāvadhāraṇam ||
prāk sa cet pakṣadharmatvād gṛhītaḥ kiṃ tataḥ param | paṣadharmādibhir jñātair yena syād anumānitā ||
anvayo na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate | vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣām anvitatvaṃ pratīyate ||
yatra dhūmo 'sti tatrāgner astitvenānvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ | na tv evaṃ yatra śabdo 'sti tatrārtho 'stīti niścayaḥ ||
na tāvat tatra deśe 'sau tatkāle vāvagamyate | bhaven nityavibhutvāc cet, sarvārtheṣu ca tat samam ||
tena sarvatra dṛṣṭatvād vyatirekasya cāgateḥ | sarvaśabdair aśeṣārthapratipattiḥ prasajyate ||
athaivaṃ deśakālābhyām asatyatvaprakalpane | vācakapratyayaṃ kaś cid brūyād arthadhiyānvitam ||
naivam apy asti dṛṣṭo hi vināpy arthadhiyā kva cit | vācakapratyayo 'smābhir avyutpannanarān prati ||
dvitīyādiprayoge ca bhaved anvayakalpanā | śatakṛtvaḥ prayukte 'pi na ca dṛṣṭārthadhīḥ kva cit ||
nanu ye jñātasambandhās teṣāṃ dṛṣṭo 'nvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ | yady evam anvayāt pūrvaṃ sambandhaḥ ko 'pi kalpitaḥ ||
nāṅgam arthadhiyām eṣā bhaved anvayakalpanā | anvayādhīnajanmatvam anumānasya ca sthitam ||
jñāte pratītisāmarthye tadvaśād eva jāyate | paścād anvaya ity eṣa kāraṇaṃ katham ucyate ||
tasmāt tannirapekṣaiva śabdaśaktiḥ pratīyate | na ca dhūmānvayāt pūrvaṃ śaktatvam avagamyate ||
vyatireko 'py avijñātād arthāc chabdadhiyau yadi | so 'pi paścāt sthitatvena nārthapratyayasādhanam ||
sambandhaṃ yaṃ tu vakṣyāmastasya nirṇayakāraṇam | syād anvayo 'tirekaś ca na tv arthādhigamasya tau ||
tasmād ananumānatvaṃ cābde pratyakṣavad bhavet | trairūpyarahitatvena tādṛgviṣayavarjanāt ||
sati cāsya pramāṇatve bhedābhedanirūpanā | yuktā na tu padajñānāt padārtho 'tra pramīyate ||
padaṃ prayujyamānaṃ hi caturddhārthe prayujyate | pratyakṣe ca parokṣe ca jñāte 'jñāte 'pi vā purā ||
tatra yat pūrvavijñāte pratyakṣe ca prayujyate | pramite ca prayuktatvād anuvādo 'dhikād vinā ||
adṛṣṭapūrve tv ajñānaṃ sambandhapratyayo 'pi vā | sambandho na ca tasyārthaḥ, yo 'rthaḥ sa tv anyagocaraḥ ||
parokṣe 'nanubhūte ca nābhidheye matir bhavet | parokṣaś cānubhūtaś ca yas tatra smṛtir iṣyate ||
pramite ca pravṛttatvāt smṛter nāsti pramāṇatā | paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyam upajāyate ||
tādātvikaparicchedaphalatvena pramāṇatā | pratyabhijñānavat kasmāt smṛter api na kalpyate ||
yāvān pūrvaparicchinnas tāvān evāvadhāryate | smṛtyā tadanusāreṇa tadāsattve 'sya naiva dhīḥ ||
padam abhyadhikābhāvāt smārakān na viśiṣyate | padādhikyaṃ bhavet kiñ cit tatpadasya na gocaraḥ ||
pramāṇam anumānaṃ vā yady api syāt padānmitiḥ | vākyārthasyāgamārthatvād doṣo nāgamavādinām ||
vākyārthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandhānubhavād ṛte | buddhir utpadyate tena bhinnā 'sāvakṣabuddhivat ||
vākyādhikaraṇe cāsya hetoḥ siddhir bhaviṣyati | sarveṣāṃ ca paroktānāṃ vākyabuddhāvasiddhatā ||
vākyeṣv adṛṣṭeṣv api sārthakeṣu padārthavinmātratayā pratītim | dṛṣṭvānumānavyatirekabhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padābhedavicāraṇāyām ||

§ 5,7 upamānapariccheda UMP

kīdṛggavaya ityevaṃ pṛṣṭo nāgarikair yadi | bravītyāraṇyako vākyaṃ yathā gaur gavayas tathā ||
etasminn upamānatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śabare punaḥ | tasyāgamābahirbhāvād anyathaivopavarṇitam ||
puruṣapratyayenaiva tatrārthaḥ sampratīyate | tadīyavacanatvena tasmād āgama eva saḥ ||
sadṛśād upajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśāntare | dhyānādismṛtitulyatvāt sā pramāṇaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ||
deśakālādibhedena yathānyatra viśiṣyate | prameyaṃ naivam asty atra nagarasthānusārataḥ ||
śrutātideśavākyānām āraṇye gavaye matiḥ | yā sopamānaṃ keṣāñ cid gosādṛśyānurañjitā ||
pratyakṣo gavayas tāvat sādṛśyasmṛtir atra tu | nanu sādṛśyayukte 'rthe na smṛtir nendriyād gatiḥ ||
pūrvavākyārthavijñānān nādhikyaṃ gavaye yadi | smaraṇād aviśiṣṭatvāt saṅgater na pramāṇatā ||
atha tv adhikatā kā cit pratyakṣādivaśād bhavet | yāvaddhīndriyasambandhas tat pratyakṣam iti sthitam ||
syaryamāṇasya cāṃśasya vivedenāpramāṇatā | śrutātideśavākyatvaṃ na cātīvopayujyate ||
ye 'pi hy aśrutatadvākyās teṣām api bhavaty ayam | pratyakṣadṛṣṭagotvānāṃ vane gavayadarśinām ||
atha saṃjñānusandhānaṃ teṣāṃ nāstīti varṇyate | na nāma vastu tat tāvat sarvathā taiḥ pratīyate ||
na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ prameyo 'tra tadeṣyate | sādṛśyāvadhṛte vākye vākyād avagato hy asau ||
na cāsya pratyabhijñānaṃ punarutpadyate vane | śaktyor atīndriyatvena smṛtir eva hi seṣyate ||
śabdānuviddhabodhe 'pi pratyakṣam upapāditam | tasmāt sādṛśyayuktārthaḥ prameyo 'pūrva ucyatām ||
vyavasāyātmakatvaṃ tu pratyakṣasya yadeṣyate | jātyādivat tadā tena sādṛśyaṃ kiṃ na mīyate ||
pratyakṣābhāsam etat tu nirvikalpakavādinām | prameyavastvabhāvāc ca nābhipretā pramāṇatā ||
sādṛśyasyāpi vastutvaṃ na śakyam apabādhitum | bhūyo 'vayavasāmānyayogo jātyantarasya tat ||
sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra padmadalākṣivat | tat svāvayavasāmānyabhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati ||
evaṃ jātiguṇadravyakriyāśaktisvadharmataḥ | ekaikadvitrisāmastyabhedād etasya citratā ||
na dharmā eva sādṛśyaṃ bhūyastā vā tadāśrayā | bhūyastvavaddhi jātyādi sadṛśatvena dṛśyate ||
yamayoḥ katham etac ced, dṛṣṭatvāt kim ihocyate | kva cid dhi bhūyasām etat kva cid alpīyasām api ||
naitāvatā viśeṣeṇa vastutvaṃ tasya hīyate | sāmānyāny api caitāni nāśīnyāśrayanāśataḥ ||
anantāśrayayogāc ca na nāśo 'nyatra vidyate | tena sarvaṃ na sāmānyaṃ nityatvena prakalpyate ||
sāmānyānāṃ na vā nāśaḥ kva cid abhyupagamyate | sarvasya hy āśrayaḥ kaś cid asti deśāntarādiṣu ||
teṣāṃ bhūyas tayā cedaṃ sādṛśyam atiricyate | tāni vyastāni santy evaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi kva cit kva cit ||
sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra nāma pratīyate | tad apy avayavānāṃ syāt samānavayavāntaraiḥ ||
evaṃ tāvad yato nāsti parābhedaprakalpanā | tataḥ paraṃ tu sāmānyaṃ bhavet sādṛśyavarjitam ||
pradhānānāṃ tu sāmānyaṃ yatraikaṃ sampratīyate | sa eveti bhavet tatra tadbhede sadṛśatvadhīḥ ||
citrādau yatra sādṛśyaṃ sāmānyaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet | tatrāpi pṛthivīvarṇaviśeṣādisamānatā ||
rūpagandharasānāṃ ca kasya cit tulyatā kva cit | nāvaśyaṃ sarvasāmānyāt sādṛśyam upajāyate ||
pṛthivyādiṣu caiteṣāṃ satām eva svabhāvataḥ | pariṇāmādibhir vyaktir yathādṛṣṭyavadhāryate ||
na hi śaktyātmanā kiñ cid asajjanma prapadyate | dharmāṇāṃ na ca nānātvam, asti cāvāntarasthitiḥ ||
vastutve sati cāsyaivaṃ sambandhasya ca cakṣuṣā | dvayor ekatra vā dṛṣṭeḥ pratyakṣatvaṃ na vāryate ||
sāmānyavac ca sādṛśyam ekaikatra samāpyate | pratiyoginyadṛṣṭe 'pi tasmāt tadupapadyate ||
tatra yady api gāṃ smṛtvā tadbhānam upajāyate | sannidhergavayasthatvād bhaved indriyagocaraḥ ||
tasmād yat smaryate tat syāt sādṛśyena viśeṣitam | prameyam upamānasya sādṛśyaṃ vā tadanvatam ||
pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhe 'pi sādṛśye gavi ca smṛteḥ | viśiṣṭasyānyato 'siddher upamānapramāṇatā ||
pratyakṣe 'pi yathā deśe smaryamāṇe ca pāvake | viśiṣṭaviṣayatvena nānumānāpramāṇatā ||
yatra tv asadṛśād eva kalpayitvopajāyate | sādṛśyapratyayas tatra tadābhāsatvakalpanā ||
bādhakapratyayāc caiṣā sādṛśyābhāsatā matā | yathā palālakūṭasya sādṛśyaṃ kuñjarādinā ||
samīpastho 'pi jānāti sādṛśyaṃ neti tatra hi | na bādhyate samīpādau yat tu sādṛśyam eva tat ||
na caitasyānumānatvaṃ pakṣadharmādyasambhavāt | prāk prameyasya sādṛśyaṃ na dharmatvena gṛhyate ||
gavaye gṛhyamāṇaṃ ca na gavām anumāpakam | pratijñārthaikadeśatvād gogatasya na liṅgatā ||
gavayaś cāpy asambandhān na gor liṅgatvamṛcchati | sādṛśyaṃ na ca sarveṇa pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadanvayi ||
ekasminn api dṛṣṭe 'rthe dvitīyaṃ paśyato vane | sādṛśyena sahaivāsmiṃs tadaivotpadyate matiḥ ||
śṛṅgitvāder athocyeta sambandhāl liṅgatā gavi | na, teṣāṃ gavayajñānavyāpāraṃ pratyupakṣayāt ||
yadi tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ syān niḥsādṛśyaiva sā bhavet | na gauḥ śṛṅgādisadṛśī sadṛśī gavayena tu ||
sadṛśapratyayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śṛṅgādipratyayāt param | gavayapratyayād eva gojñānam upajāyate ||
sadṛśāvayavatve tu teṣām evopamā bhavet | na ca śṛṅgādayo yatra tatra gaur anumīyate ||
itthaṃ cānumimānasya bhrāntajñānaṃ prasajyate | nagarasthe tu gojñānaṃ smaraṇān nātivartate ||
bhinnānumānād upameyam uktam, sauryādivākyair asahāyi dṛṣṭam | sādṛśyato 'gnyādiyutaṃ kathaṃ nu, pratyāyayed ity upayujyate naḥ ||
pratinidhir api caivaṃ vrīhisādṛśyayogād bhavati tadapacāre yatra nīvārajātau | tad api phalam abhīṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇasyopamāyāḥ pratikṛtir api gauṇair bodhyate yatra cānyaiḥ ||
yadi susadṛśamanyal labhyate tatra mithyā bhavati visadṛśatvān mandasādṛśyayuktam | matir api ca tathaiva drāgivotpadyate 'sminn itaraviṣayabodhe 'saty apītthaṃ ca bādhaḥ ||

§ 5,8 arthāpattipariccheda AAP

pramāṇaṣaṭkavijñāto yatrārtho nānyathā bhavet | adṛṣṭaṃ kalpayed anyaṃ sārthāpattir udāhṛtā ||
dṛṣṭaḥ pañcabhir apy asmād bhedenoktā śrutodbhavā | pramāṇagrāhiṇītvena yasmāt pūrvavilakṣaṇā ||
tatra pratyakṣato jñānād dāhād dahanaśaktatā | vahner anumitāt sūrye yānāt tacchaktiyogyatā ||
śrutārthāpattir atraiva parastād abhidhāsyate | gavayopamitā yā gaus tajjñānagrāhyatā matā ||
abhidhānaprasiddhyartham arthāpattyāvabodhitāt | śabde bodhakasāmarthyāt tannityatvaprakalpanam ||
abhidhā nānyathā sidhyed iti vācakaśaktatām | arthāpattyāvagamyaivaṃ tadananyagateḥ punaḥ ||
arthāpattyantareṇaiva śabdanityatvaniścayaḥ | darśanasya parārthatvād ity asminn abhidhāsyate ||
pramāṇābhāvanirṇītacaitrābhāvaviśeṣitāt | gehāc caitrabahirbhāvasiddhir yā tv iha darśitā ||
tām abhāvotthitām anyām arthāpattim udāharet | pakṣadoṣeṣu cānyāsāmudāharaṇavistaraḥ ||
abhāvāvagatāc caitrād bahirbhāvasya sūcanam | pakṣadharmādyanaṅgatvād bhinnaivāpy anumānataḥ ||
bahirdeśaviśiṣṭe 'rthe deśe vā tadviśeṣite | prameye yo gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmas tv asau katham ||
tadabhāvaviśiṣṭaṃ tu gṛhaṃ dharmo na kasyacit | gṛhābhāvaviśiṣṭas tu tadāsau na pratīyate ||
gamyate tu gṛhaṃ tatra na ca caitraḥ pratīyate | na cātrādarśanaṃ hetur yathābhāve 'bhidhāsyate ||
tena veśmanyadṛṣṭatvād iti hetur na kalpyate | adarśanād abhāve ca prameyasyāvadhārite ||
bahirbhāvamatir nāsau tenādarśanahetukā | caitrābhāvasya hetutvaṃ gehe 'bhāvaś ca saṃsthitaḥ ||
pūrvaṃ na cāgṛhītasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā | na cātra bāhyadeśo vā caitro vā gṛhyate purā ||
nadīpūreṇa yā vṛṣṭir upariṣṭāt pratīyate | deśe katham adṛṣṭe tu pakṣadharmatvasambhavaḥ ||
vṛṣṭimatparadeśatvaṃ nadīpuravato 'tra tu | deśasya pratipadyante yadvārthāpattir eva sā ||
jīvataś ca gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmo 'tra kalpyate | tatsaṃvittir bahirbhāvaṃ na cābuddhvopajāyate ||
agnimattānapekṣā tu dhūmavattā pratīyate | na tadgrahaṇavelāyām agnyadhīnaṃ hi kiñcana ||
gehābhāvas tu yaḥ śuddho vidyamānatvavarjitaḥ | sa mṛteṣv api dṛṣṭatvād bahirvṛtter na sādhakaḥ ||
vidyamānatvasaṃsṛṣṭagṛhābhāvadhiyānayā | gehād utkālitaś caitro vidyate bahir eva hi ||
gehābhāvatvamātraṃ tu yat svatantraṃ pratīyate | na tāvatā bahirbhāvaś caitrasyaivāvadhāryate ||
siddhe sadbhāvavijñāne gehābhāvadhiyātra tu | gehād utkālitā sattā bahir evāvatiṣṭhate ||
tenāsya nirapekṣasya vyabhicāro mṛtādinā | yasya tv avyabhicāritvaṃ na tato 'nyat pratīyate ||
tasmāt pratyakṣato gehe caitrābhāve hy abhāvataḥ | jñāte yat sattvavijñānaṃ tad evedaṃ bahiḥ sthitam ||
pakṣadharmātmalābhāya bahirbhāvaḥ praveśitaḥ | tadviśiṣṭo 'numeyaḥ syāt pakṣadharmānvayādibhiḥ ||
pakṣadharmādivijñānaṃ bahiḥ sambodhato yadi | taiś ca tadbodhato 'vaśyam anyonyāśrayatā bhavet ||
anyathānupapattau tu prameyānupraveśitā | tādrūpyeṇaiva vijñānān na doṣaḥ pratibhāti naḥ ||
avinābhāvitā cātra tadaiva parikalpyate | na prāg avadhṛtety evaṃ saty apy eṣā na kāraṇam ||
gṛhābhāvabahirbhāvau na ca dṛṣṭau niyogataḥ | sāhitye 'pi pramāṇaṃ ca tayor anyan na vidyate ||
anyathānupapattyaiva hy ekenānyat pratīyate | tathā na kalpyate tac cet sāhityaṃ na pratīyate ||
tena sambandhavelāyāṃ sambandhyanyataro dhruvam | arthāpattyāvagantavyaḥ paścād asty anumānatā ||
gṛhadvāri sthito yas tu bahirbhāvaṃ prakalpayet | yadaikasminn ayaṃ deśe na tadānyatra vidyate ||
tadāpy avidyamānatvaṃ na sarvatra pratīyate | na caikadeśe nāstitvād vyāptir hetor bhaviṣyati ||
nanv atrāvidyamānatvaṃ gamyate 'nupalabdhitaḥ | sā cāprayatnasādhyatvād ekasthasyaiva sidhyati ||
naitayānupalabdhyātra vastvabhāvaḥ pratīyate | taddeśāgamanāt sā hi dūrastheṣv asti satsv api ||
gatvā gatvā tu tān deśān yady artho nopalabhyate | tato 'nyakāraṇābhāvād asann ity avagamyate ||
nanu cāgnyādyabhāve 'pi dhūmādivyatirekiṇām | taddeśāgamanāt spaṣṭo vyatireko na sidhyati ||
yasya vastvantarābhāvaḥ prameyas tasya duṣyati | mama tv adṛṣṭamātreṇa gamakaḥ sahacāriṇaḥ ||
nanv evam itaratrāpi sambandho 'nupalabdhitaḥ | caitrābhāvasya bhāvena dṛṣṭatvād upapadyate ||
sāhitye mitadeśatvāt prasiddhe cāgnidhūmayoḥ | vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer gamakatvaṃ prakalpyate ||
iha sāhityam evedam ekasya sahabhāvinaḥ | anantadeśavarttitvān na tāvad upapadyate ||
nanu deśāntaraṃ śūnyaṃ caitreṇaivaṃ pratīyate | taddeśavyatiriktatvāt samīpasthitadeśavat ||
viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ tadvad eva hi gamyate | samīpadeśabhinnatvāt caitrādhiṣṭhitadeśavat ||
puruṣasya tu kārtsnyena yad ekatropalambhanam | tasyānyathā na siddhiḥ syād ity anyeṣv asya nāstitā ||
tenārthāpattipūrvatvam atra yatra ca kāraṇe | kāryādarśanataḥ śakter astitvaṃ sampratīyate ||
kāryasya nanu liṅgatvaṃ na sambandhānapekṣaṇāt | dṛṣṭvā sambandhitāṃ caiṣā śaktir gamyeta nānyathā ||
taddarśane tadānīṃ ca pratyakṣāder asambhavāt | arthāpatteḥ pramāṇatvaṃ trailakṣaṇyād vinā bhavet ||
anumānād abhinnatvān noktau jayaparājayau | vadhyaghātakabhāvena yau sarpanakulādiṣu ||
pīno divā na bhuṅkte cety evamādivacaḥ śrutau | rātribhojanavijñānaṃ śrutārthāpattir ucyate ||
tām arthagocarāṃ kecid apare śabdagocarām | kalpayanty āgamāc cainām abhinnāṃ pratijānate ||
prāyaśaś cānayā vede vyavahāro vyavasthitaḥ | so 'vaidikaḥ prasajyeta yady eṣā bhidyate tataḥ ||
vacanasya śrutasyaiva so 'py arthaḥ kaiścid āśritaḥ | tadarthopaplutasyānyair iṣṭo vākyāntarasya tu ||
na tāvac chrūyamāṇasya vacaso 'rtho 'yam iṣyate | na hy anekārthatā yuktā vākye vācakatā tathā ||
padārthānvayarūpeṇa vākyārtho hi pratīyate | na rātryādipadārthaś ca divāvākyena gamyate ||
na divādipadārthānāṃ saṃsargo rātribhojanam | na bhedo yena tadvākyaṃ tasya syāt pratipādakam ||
anyārthavyāpṛtatvāc ca na dvitīyārthakalpanā | tasmād vākyāntareṇāyaṃ buddhisthena pratīyate ||
tasya cāgamikatve 'pi yat tad vākyaṃ pratīyate | pramāṇaṃ tasya vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣādiṣu yad bhavet ||
na hy anuccārite vākye pratyakṣaṃ tāvad iṣyate | nānumānaṃ na cedaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ tena saha kvacit ||
yadi tv anupalabdhe 'pi sambandhe liṅgateṣyate | taduccāraṇamātreṇa sarvavākyamatir bhavet ||
na cārthāpattigamyāni sarvaiḥ sarvavacāṃsi hi | sambaddhāny upalabdhāni yena teṣv anumā bhavet ||
na ca sattānumānena viśeṣo vānumīyate | iha vākyaviśeṣasya sattaiva tv avagamyate ||
pūrvasiddhaḥ svatantro 'rthaḥ svatantreṇa viśeṣitaḥ | dharmādharmaviśiṣṭo 'tra nānumeyaḥ pratīyate ||
atha śrutasya vākyasya mīyate tadviśiṣṭatā | tataḥ pakṣo 'bhyupetaḥ syād aprasiddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
kiñ ca liṅgāntarābhāvād etasya yadi liṅgatā | pratijñārthaikadeśatvaṃ padavat te prasajyate ||
tadvad eva nirākāryā vacaso dharmadharmitā | nāgṛhīte hi taddharmo gṛhīte nānumeyatā ||
kriyākārakasambandhād ṛte nāsti tu dharmatā | avācakatayā caitan na dharmo viṣayātmanā ||
pratīter vācakatvaṃ cet prasaktānekaśaktitā | anumāviṣayotthaṃ tu dharmatvaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet ||
padārthair api tadvākyaṃ nāsambandhāt pratīyate | sāmānyānyanyathāsiddher viśeṣaṃ gamayanti hi ||
na tu vākyāntareṇaiṣāṃ vinā kiñcin na sidhyati | na cāpy anyaḥ prakāro 'sti tena vākyena saṅgatau ||
athaitad vāci kalpyeta vākyam anyat tathaiva ca | prasaṅgāt tatra dūre 'pi nāsambandhāt pramucyate ||
tataś ca prathamād eva varaṃ jñātum asaṅgatāt | anvayavyatirekau ca pratiṣedhyau pade yathā ||
śrutavākyena sādṛśyaṃ nāśrutasyāsti kiñcana | tasmād anupamānatvam arthasyāpy anayā diśā ||
upamānatvaliṅgatve vākyaṃ prati nivārite | arthe 'pi caivam eva syāt, tasmāt pūrveṣv asambhavaḥ ||
ataḥ śrutasya vākyasya yad arthapratipādanam | tadātmalābha eva syād vinā nety etad iṣyate ||
etadarthād vinā nāyam ity arthaḥ kiṃ na kalpyate | vākyārthavac ca kiṃ nāyam āgamārthaḥ pratīyate ||
savikalpakavijñānaiḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaṃ pratīyate | labdhaprayojane vākye paraṃ nāgamikaṃ ca naḥ ||
nanu cāsati sambandhe sati vānavadhārite | gamyajñānam idaṃ vākyaṃ prasajyetāpramāṇakam ||
sambandhasya pramāṇatvaṃ sthitaṃ kiñceśvarājñayā | pratyakṣasya pramāṇatvaṃ kathaṃ vā saṅgater vinā ||
astīndriyārthasambandhas tatra cen nānapekṣaṇāt | na hi pratyakṣavelāyāṃ sarveṇāsau nirūpyate ||
yenāpi tu nirūpyeta paścād anubhavād asau | na syād eva pramāṇāṅgam asatā tulya eva saḥ ||
aprāpyakāriṇī yeṣāṃ cakṣuḥśrotre ca te yathā | tajjñānasya pramāṇatvam icchanty evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
tasmād asattve sattve vā sambandhasya yad eva naḥ | jāyetābhaṅguraṃ jñānaṃ tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||
na cāpy asyāḥ pramāṇatve kaścid vipratipadyate | bhedābhede visaṃvādaḥ kṛtas tatra ca nirṇayaḥ ||
kṛte yatra ca sambandhād buddhir eva na jāyate | tatra ki kriyatāṃ so 'pi prāmāṇye naiva kāraṇam ||
smṛtyā śrutir yā parikalpyate 'smin liṅgādibhir yā viniyojikā ca | phalādibhir yat paripūraṇaṃ ca sambandhadṛk tatra na kācid asti ||
tat sarvam ityādy asamañjasaṃ syān na cediyaṃ syād anumānato 'nyā | evaṃsvabhāvāpy anumānaśabdaṃ labheta ced asti yathepsitaṃ naḥ ||

§ 5,9 abhāvapariccheda ABH

pramāṇapañcakaṃ yatra vasturūpe na jāyate | vastusattāvabodhārthaṃ tatrābhāvapramāṇatā ||
vastvasaṅkarasiddhiś ca tatprāmāṇyasamāśrayā | kṣīre dadhyādi yan nāsti prāgabhāvaḥ sa ucyate ||
nāstitā payaso dadhni pradhvaṃsābhāva iṣyate | gavi yo 'śvādyabhāvas tu so 'nyonyābhāva ucyate ||
śiraso 'vayavā nimnā vṛddhikāṭhinyavarjitāḥ | śaśaśṛṅgādirūpeṇa so 'tyantābhāva ucyate ||
kṣīre dadhi bhaved evaṃ dadhni kṣīraṃ ghaṭe paṭaḥ | śaśe śṛṅgaṃ pṛthivyādau caitanyaṃ mūrtir ātmani ||
apsu gandho rasaś cāgnau vāyau rūpeṇa tau saha | vyomni saṃsparśitā te ca na ced asya pramāṇatā ||
na ca syād vyavahāro 'yaṃ kāraṇādivibhāgataḥ | prāgabhāvādibhedena nābhāvo bhidyate yadi ||
na cāvastuna ete syur bhedās tenāsya vastutā | kāryādīnām abhāvaḥ ko yo 'bhāvaḥ kāraṇāditaḥ ||
yadvānuvṛttivyāvṛttibuddhigrāhyo yatas tv ayam | tasmād gavādivad vastu, prameyatvāc ca gamyate ||
na caupacārikatvaṃ vā bhrāntir vāpi yadṛcchayā | bhavaty ato na sāmānyaviśeṣātmakatā mṛṣā ||
pratyakṣāder anutpattiḥ pramāṇābhāva ucyate | sātmanaḥ pariṇāmo vā vijñānaṃ vākyavastuni ||
svarūpapararūpābhyāṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmake | vastuni jñāyate kaiś cid rūpaṃ kiñ cit kadā cana ||
yasya yatra yadodbhūtir jighṛkṣā vopajāyate | cetyate 'nubhavas tasya tena ca vyapadiśyate ||
tasyopakārakatvena varttate 'śastadetaraḥ | ubhayor api saṃvittāv ubhayānugamo 'sti hi ||
ayam eveti yo hy eṣa bhāve bhavati nirṇayaḥ | naiṣa vastvantarābhāvasaṃvittyanugamād ṛte ||
nāstīty api ca saṃvittir na vastvanugamād ṛte | jñānaṃ na jāyate kiñ cid upaṣṭambhanavarjitam ||
pratyakṣādyavatāras tu bhāvāṃśo gṛhyate yadā | vyāpāras tadanutpatter abhāvāṃśe jighṛkṣite ||
na tāvad indriyair eṣā nāstīty utpadyate matiḥ | bhāvāṃśenaiva saṃyogo yogyatvādindriyasya hi ||
nanu bhāvād abhinnatvāt samprayogo 'sti tena ca | na hy atyantam abhedo 'sti rūpādivad ihāpi naḥ ||
dharmayor bheda iṣṭo hi dharmyabhede 'pi naḥ sthite | udbhavābhibhavātmatvād grahaṇaṃ cāvatiṣṭhate ||
idam eva nimittaṃ ca vivekasya pratīyate | bhāvābhāvadhiyor akṣaiḥ sambandho 'kṣānapekṣaṇam ||
rūpāder api bhedaṃ ca ke cid grāhakabhedataḥ | varṇayanti yathaikasya puṃsaḥ putrādirūpatām ||
buddhimātrakṛto bhedo rūpādau nityam eva hi | na ca deśādyabhinnānāṃ samudāyāvakalpanā ||
sadguṇadravyarūpeṇa rūpāder ekateṣyate | svarūpāpekṣayā caiṣāṃ parasparavibhinnatā ||
yadi tadvadapekṣātra na syād bhedo 'tra naiva hi | sadasadrūpatā buddher bhaved anyataratra naḥ ||
tatsambandhe sad ityevaṃ tadrūpatvaṃ pratīyate | nāsty atredam itīdaṃ tu tadasaṃyogahetukam ||
gṛhītvā vastusadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam | mānasaṃ nāstitājñānaṃ jāyate 'kṣānapekṣaṇāt ||
svarūpamātraṃ dṛṣṭvāpi paścāt kiñ cit smarann api | tatrānyanāstitāṃ pṛṣṭas tadaiva pratipadyate ||
na cāpy atrānumānatvaṃ liṅgābhāvāt pratīyate | bhāvāṃśo nanu liṅgaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ nājighṛkṣaṇāt ||
abhāvāvagater janma bhāvāṃśe hy ajighṛkṣite | tasmin pratīyamāne tu nābhāve jāyate matiḥ ||
na caiṣa prakṣadharmatvaṃ padavat pratipadyate | saha sarvair abhāvaiś ca bhāvo naikāntato gataḥ ||
kva cid bhāve 'pi sadbhāvo jñāto yasya kadā cana | tasyābhāvo 'pi tatraiva kadā cid avagamyate ||
yatrāpy adṛṣṭapūrvatvaṃ yadabhāvasya tatra ca | tadabhāvamatir dṛṣṭā sambandhe 'kṣānapekṣayā ||
kasya cid yadi bhāvasya syād abhāvena kena cit | sambandhadarśanam, tatra sarvamānaṃ prasajyate ||
gṛhīte 'pi ca bhāvāṃśe naivābhāve 'nyavastunaḥ | sarvatra matir ityevaṃ vyabhicārād aliṅgatā ||
sambandhe gṛhyamāṇe ca sambandhigrahaṇaṃ dhruvam | tatrābhāvamatiḥ kena pramāṇenopajāyate ||
tadānīṃ na hi liṅgena sambandhigrahaṇaṃ bhavet | tatrāvaśyam abhāvasya pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
pratyakṣāder anutpattir na tu liṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati | na viśeṣaṇasambandhas tasyāḥ sāmānyato bhavet ||
na cāpy abhāvasāmānye pramāṇam upajāyate | vyabhicārād viśeṣās tu pratīyeran kathaṃ tayā ||
na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhyate ced asāv api | abhāvatvād abhāvena gṛhyetānyena hetunā ||
