sa cānyena grahītavyo nāgṛhīte hi liṅgatā | tadgṛhītir hi liṅgena syād anyenety anantatā ||
liṅgābhāve tathaiva syād anavastheyam ity ataḥ | kvāpy asya syāt pramāṇatvaṃ liṅgatvena vinā dhruvam ||
nāstīti dhīḥ phalaṃ caiṣā pratyakṣāder ajanmanaḥ | tasyaiva ca pramāṇatvam ānantaryāt pratīyate ||
trilakṣaṇena yā buddhir janyate sānumeṣyate | na cānutpattirūpasya kāraṇāpekṣitā kva cit ||
mānaṃ katham abhāvaś cet, prameyaṃ cāsya kīdṛśam | meyo yadvadabhāvo hi mānam apy evam iṣyatām ||
bhāvātmake tathā meye nābhāvasya pramāṇatā | tathābhāvaprameye 'pi na bhāvasya pramāṇatā ||
bhāvātmakasya mānatvaṃ na ca rājājñayā sthitam | paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyaṃ syād dvayor api ||
yadi cāsya pramāṇatvam abhāvatvena neṣyate | vastunaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ hi dṛṣṭam ity abhimānitā ||
na liṅgatvaprameyatve bhavetāṃ tadvad eva hi | tathā sati ca pūrvokto vyavahāro na sidhyati ||
pramāṇānām anutpatter nābhāvasyāpi dharmatā | yatrābhāvo 'sti tenāsyāḥ sambandho naiva vidyate ||
yo na sannihitas tatra tasya dharmo bhaved iyam | na ca tasya prameyatvaṃ dharmadharmitvavarjanāt ||
abhāvena tu sambandho bhavet tadviṣayatvataḥ | tajjānād viṣayatvaṃ ca jñāne meyaṃ na vidyate ||
saṃyogasamavāyādisambandho naiva vidyate | nāgṛhīte hi dharmatvaṃ gṛhīte siddhasādhanam ||
abhāvaśabdavācyatvāt pratyakṣādeś ca bhidyate | pramāṇānām abhāvo hi prameyāṇām abhāvavat ||
abhāvo vā pramāṇena svānurūpeṇa mīyate | prameyatvād yathā bhāvas tasmād bhāvātmakāt pṛthak ||
karmāṇi sarvāṇi phalaiḥ samastaiḥ sarvair yathāvac ca yadaṅgakāṇḍaiḥ | na saṅgatānīha parasparaṃ ca nāṅgaṃ tadetat prabhavaṃ kratūnām ||
yuktyāgamābhyām iti tarkito 'yaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ pravibhajya bhāṣye | tato 'dhikaṃ yad dvayam iṣṭam anyair bhedo na tasyety api siddham etat ||
iha bhavati śatādau sambhavādyāsahasrānmatir aviyutabhāvāt sānumānād abhinnā | jagati bahu na tathyaṃ nityam aitihyam uktaṃ bhavati tu yadi satyaṃ nāgamād bhidyate tat ||

§ 5,10 citrākṣepavāda CAV

paralokaphalāḥ pūrvam ākṣiptāś codanāḥ paraiḥ | idānīm aihikākṣepaḥ, sūtrakāreṇa codyate ||
citrāpaśuphalatvādiviṣayāś codaṇā mṛṣā | pratyakṣādyadhikāre 'pi tair arthāsaṅgatir yataḥ ||
yadīdṛk tanmṛṣā dṛṣṭaṃ vipralipsor yathā vacaḥ | nadītīre phalānīti tatrādṛśyāni tāni cet ||
na vā paśuphalā citrā svakāle tadadānaḥ | snānabhujyādivat te 'pi tatsādhyā na bhavanti vā ||
tadutpattāvasadbhāvāt svarge tṛptisukhādivat | vaidharmyeṇobhayatrāpi bhavetāṃ sukham ardane ||
ānantaryam ayuktaṃ cet, na sāmarthyāvabodhanāt | śabdaikadeśabhūtena tena tat pratipāditam ||
kālāntarānupādānāt karmasvābhāvyato 'pi ca | codyamānasya citrāder ānantaryaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
atra tāvadasaṃvādo virodhaś cottarasya tu | svargayānaviruddho hi bhasmībhāvo 'tra dṛśyate ||
yajñāyudhivaco mithyā pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ | sādharmyeṇa śilāvākyaṃ vaidharmyeṇāptabhāṣitam ||
śarīrād yadi cānyaḥ syān nāsau yajñāyudhī bhavet | na cāsya yajamānatvaṃ sadbhāvo 'pi ca durlabhaḥ ||
yadi syād vidhiśabdo 'tra naivādarśanato bhavet | viśeṣo 'syeti bhedena nopāttaṃ syād idaṃ tataḥ ||
vidhiśabde bhaviṣyattvaṃ phalasya parikalpya hi | virodhaparihāraḥ syād vartamāne 'pi nāsty asau ||
phalaṃ ca na bhaved evaṃ bhasmībhāvād vidhāv api | tatsāmarthyena yā cānyā kalpanā tāṃ niṣedhati ||
prāyaś caivamprakāratvam arthavādeṣu dṛśyate | mantreṣu ceti te sarve pakṣīkāryāḥ prayatnataḥ ||
evaṃ saty agnihotrādivākyeṣv api mṛṣārthatā | vedavākyaikadeśatvāc citrādivacaneṣv api ||

§ 5,11 sambandhākṣepavāda SAV

svapakṣasādhanaṃ tāvat na mṛṣā vaidikaṃ vacaḥ | svārthe vaktranapekṣatvāt padārthapadabuddhivat ||
tatkṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ samyaṅ nityavākyodbhavatvataḥ | vākyabuddhivad eva atra pūrvoktāś cāpi hetavaḥ ||
nityān śabdārthasambandhānāśrityoktena hetunā | svataḥ prāmāṇyasiddhyartham aprāmāṇye nirākṛte ||
asambandhodbhavatvena paro mithyātvam abravīt | sambandho 'sti ca nityaś cety uktam autpattikādinā ||
mithyā tv asya nirāsārthaṃ tatparair neṣyate dvayam | naiva cāsty atra sambandhaḥ kṛtako veti vakṣyate ||
asambhavena śeṣāṇāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ pariśiṣyate | asminn eva ca sambandhe pratītir laukiko dhruvā ||
tanniṣedhamataḥ prāha na śabdo 'rthena saṅgataḥ | taddeśānantarādṛṣṭer vindhyo himavatā yathā ||
evam artho dvayaṃ vāpi sādhanīyam asaṅgatam | kṣuretyādi ca siddhyarthahetor uktam athāparaḥ ||
śaktirūpaṃ gṛhītvāha saṃśleṣo yadi vāryate | sambandhasiddhasādhyatvam atha sambandhamātrakam ||
pitāputrādisambandhair anekāntaḥ prasajyate | ekabhūmyādisambandhād dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
vācyavācakasambandhaniṣedhe lokabādhanam | virodhaś ca svavākyena na hi sambandhavarjitaiḥ ||
pratijñārthaṃ padaiḥ śākyaḥ pratīpādayituṃ paraḥ | abhidhānakriyāyāṃ hi karmatvaṃ vācyasaṃśritam ||
śabdānāṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā kartṛtvaṃ vā nirūpitam | pratipattāv upādānāt sāhitye ca vivakṣite ||
niyamyate yadekasyāṃ sambandhaḥ so 'rthaśabdayoḥ | tatra yady apy asambandhaḥ kārakāṇāṃ parasparam ||
tathāpi yatkriyā tasyām upakāryopakāritā | sa kriyāsaṅgateḥ paścāt sambandhaḥ kīrtyate tayoḥ ||
na cātrāpy avinābhāva upayogīti sādhitam | saṃjñeti gamakatvaṃ cen na tadaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
gamayantīṃ śrutiṃ dṛṣṭvā kalpyate vyavahārataḥ | na caiṣā gamayatyarthaṃ sambandhe 'navadhārite ||
tasmād gamakatā paścād dhūmāder iva jāyate | sānaṅgaṃ tadvad eva syād neyaṃ dhūmādibhiḥ samā ||
nirūpite 'vinābhāve tatra tatkāritā hy asau | gamakatvena pūrvaṃ ca tatra notpadyate matiḥ ||
iha vācakatāyāḥ prāṅ nāvinābhāvitāmatiḥ | yad eva ceha sambandhaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyate ||
tadaiva gamako 'syāyam iti nānyasvarūpataḥ | kathayanti kva cit tāvad boddhavyo 'smād ayaṃ tv iti ||
kva cid vācaka ity evaṃ vācyo 'yam iti cocyate | kva cid uccaritācchabdād dṛṣṭvārthaviṣayāṃ kriyām ||
keṣāñ cit tatra boddhṛtvam anumānāt pratīyate | etenāsmād yataḥ śabdād artho 'yam avadhāritaḥ ||
tena nūnam imau siddhau vācyavācakaśaktikau | itthaṃ vācakatā siddhā saṅkīrṇāpi tataḥ param ||
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ niṣkṛṣṭe 'rthe niyamyate | bahujātiguṇadravyakarmabhedāvalamvinaḥ ||
pratyayāt sahasā jātā śrautalākṣaṇikātmakāt | na lokaḥ kāranābhāvān nirdhārayitum icchati ||
balābalādisiddhyarthaṃ vākyajñāstu viviñcate | kakṣāntaritasāmānyaviśeṣeṣu hi durbalaḥ ||
sāmānyavacanaḥ śabdo jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt | tenāvaśyaṃ vivektavyaṃ jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt ||
kiyad vā nityasambandhād abhidheyena lakṣyate | tatra prayogabāhulyāt tadviśeṣeṣv asatsv api ||
prayogāt parasāmānye sati vācyaprayogataḥ | sāsnādyekārthasambandhigotvamātrasya vācakaḥ ||
gośabda iti vijñānam anvayavyatirekajam | tasmād gamakataivādau abhidhāyakatā punaḥ ||
tannimitteti sambandhaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvalakṣaṇaḥ | sambandhaniyamo 'yaṃ tu yā 'vinābhāvitocyate ||
sambandhagrahaṇāt pūrva yasmān na gamayaty ataḥ | gavāder nābhidhāśaktir devadattapade yathā ||
yathaiva gamakaḥ śabdo vyavahārāt pratīyate | tathaiva śaktivijñānaṃ tasyopāyo 'vagamyate ||
svarūpagrahaṇaṃ cāsya yathā vyāpriyate phale | tathā sambandhivijñānaṃ nāśaktis tatkṛtā bhavet ||
yatsādhakatamatvena kasya cit kiñ cid ucyate | tasyānugrāhakāpekṣā na svaśaktivighātinī ||
na hi tat kāraṇaṃ loke vede vā kiñ cid īdṛśam | itikartavyatāsādhye yasya nānugrahe 'rthitā ||
pratyātmaniyatatvāc ca yathaiva karaṇaṃ bhavet | bāhyāntaravibhāgena kva cit syād vā vivakṣayā ||
udvigno hy andhakāreṇa kaś cid evaṃ bravīty api | kiṃ cakṣuṣā mamaitena dṛṣṭaṃ dīpena yanmayā ||
nityavṛttau tu nāndhānāṃ dṛṣṭir dīpaśatair api | rūpādidarśane yasmāt tasmāc cakṣuḥ prakāśakam ||
śarīrātmamanoyogād asādhāraṇatābalāt | vijñānāsattibhāvāc ca cakṣuḥ kāraṇam iṣyate ||
tathaivehāpi sambandhajñānam aṅgaṃ prasiddhitaḥ | gauravāt karaṇatvena mataṃ cet kena vāryate ||
yathā cakṣur itīdaṃ tu vyabhicāritvam ucyate | devadatte 'pi cāvyaktāṃ śaktim icchanti yuktitaḥ ||
prakāśe 'vasthite bāhye nāndho rūpaṃ pratīyate | phalānantaryataś cāpi cakṣuḥ karaṇam iṣyate ||
puruṣādhīnavijñānas tebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ | yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa ceṣṭaś ced dhruvaṃ kṛtaḥ ||
bhinnadeśādyadhiṣṭhānād yathā rajjughaṭādiṣu | samaṃ nāsty anayoḥ kiñ cit tenāsaṅgatatā svataḥ ||

§ 5,12 sphoṭavāda SPH

ādhārātmani vijñāte sukham ādheyabodhanam | tasyaiva tāvat prastāvād atha gaur ity ato 'bravīt ||
pratyakṣe 'pi visaṃvādo yeṣāṃ kaḥ svayam uttaram | tebhyo dadyād iti jñātvā vṛddhānāṃ matam abravīt ||
tatrārthapratyayadvāraṃ kṛtaṃ śabdanirūpaṇam | yair āsatāṃ tu te tāvat pratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate ||
pratyakṣaṃ nāsamarthaṃ nastena cārthe 'vadhārite | na hetur balavān anyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatas tataḥ ||
tasmāc chrotraparicchinno yady arthaṃ gamayen na vā | sarvathā tasya śabdatvaṃ lokasiddhaṃ na hīyate ||
yadi tv arthagatau śaktir na syād asya tataḥ punaḥ | vastvantaraṃ prakalpyeta vinā śabdaprasiddhitaḥ ||
agnyādīn gamayanto 'pi śabdā dhūmādayo na hi | na vā 'pratyāyakatvāt syād ekavarṇeṣv aśabdatā ||
na ca prāgarthavijñānāś chotragrāhye na śabdadhīḥ | na cārthajñānataḥ paścād aśrautre 'pi ca śabdatā ||
parasparānapekṣāś ca śrotrabuddhyā svarūpataḥ | varṇā evāvagamyante na pūrvāparavastunī ||
alpīyasāpi yatnena śabdam uccaritaṃ matiḥ | yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇaṃ yadi vā sakalaṃ sphuṭam ||
pṛthaṅ na copalabhyante varṇasyāvayavāḥ kva cit | na ca varṇeṣv anusyūtā dṛśyante tantuvat paṭe ||
teṣām anupalabdheś ca na jñātā liṅgasaṅgatiḥ | nāgamas tatparaś cāsti nādṛṣṭe copamā kva cit ||
na cāpy anupapattiḥ syād varṇasyāvayavair vinā | yathānyāvayavānāṃ hi vināpy avayavāntaraiḥ ||
pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhaś ca varṇo 'vayavavarjitaḥ | kiṃ na syād, vyomavac cātra liṅgaṃ tadrahitā matiḥ ||
tadvac cāsyaikabuddhitvād deśabhede 'py abhinnatā | nanu bhedamatir na syāt, tavāpy ekatvadhīḥ kutaḥ ||
sāmānyeṣu mamaikā dhīs tadvyaktiṣu ca bhedadhīḥ | na hīṣṭaṃ bhedamātraṃ hi na syād ekatvadhīr yataḥ ||
vyaktes tāvan na sāmānyaṃ bhinnarūpaṃ pratīyate | varṇeṣv anyatra śabdatvān nānyac ced varṇa eva saḥ ||
sa eveti matir nāpi sādṛśyam, na ca tat kva cit | vināvayavasāmānyād varṇeṣv avayavā na ca ||
pratyakṣaviṣayatvāc ca nānyāpoho 'pi yujyate | vācakaś cātra liṅgaṃ vā na tadānīṃ pratīyate ||
gakārādiṣu sāmānyaṃ śabdatvaṃ kalpyate yathā | gotvaṃ ca śābaleyādau tathaitat kiṃ na kalpyate ||
śābaleyagakārādīn niṣpannān vyaktirūpataḥ | sāmānyadhīr na gṛhṇātīty ato jātir apīṣyate ||
na tu drutādibhede 'pi niṣpannā sampratīyate | gavyaktyantaravyāvṛttā gavyaktir aparā sphuṭā ||
tenaikatvena varṇasya buddhir ekopajāyate | viśeṣabuddhisadbhāvo bhaved vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
yathaiva tava gatvādi gamyamānaṃ drutādibhiḥ | viśeṣair api nānekam evaṃ varṇo 'pi no bhavet ||
tvayāpi vyañjakavyaktibhedād bhedo 'bhyupeyate | mamāpi vyañjakair nādair bhedabuddhir bhaviṣyati ||
tena yat prārthyate jāte tad varṇād eva labhyate | vyaktilabhyaṃ ca nādebhya iti gatvādidhīr yathā ||
kalpayitvāpi tatpaścād vibhutvaikatvanityatāḥ | pratyekavṛttitā cāsya bhaveyur mahataḥ śramāt ||
dvayasiddhas tu varṇātmā nityatvādi yathaiva ca | kalpitasyeṣyate tadvat siddhasyaivābhyupeyatām ||
pratyekasamavāye ca kleśo naiva bhaviṣyati | vyañjaneṣu ca dhībhedo naiva tādṛk pratīyate ||
dṛśyate 'janurāgeṇa bhedo yo nāma, tatra naḥ | vivedo 'sty eva na hy eṣa kevalānāṃ pratīyate ||
akṣv apy evaṃ paropādhir drutādipratyayo yathā | varṇā ''śritatvād varṇatvavyañjanapratyayo yathā ||
gakāro 'tyantaniṣkṛṣṭagatvādhāro na gamyate | gānyabuddhyanirūpyatvāt paraiḥ kalpitagatvavat ||
avastutvena sādhyatvān niṣedhād dhetusādhyayoḥ | sapakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhir na doṣāyātra jāyate ||
varṇatvāc cāpi sādhyo 'yaṃ yakārādivad eva ca | vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer nātra dṛṣṭaṃ nivartakam ||
gotvādivāraṇe tv eva dṛṣṭabādhaḥ sphuṭo bhavet | nānyathā hi matis tatra syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
na cāpy atraikavastutve bhedo vyañjakabhedataḥ | na piṇḍavyatirekeṇa vyañjako 'tra dhvanir yathā ||
piṇḍavyaṅgyaiva gotvādir jātir nityaṃ pratīyate | tena bhinneṣu piṇḍeṣu jātir ekā pratīyate ||
nanu yasya dvayaṃ śrotraṃ tasya buddhidvayaṃ bhavet | bhavato 'tīndriyatvāt tu kathaṃ nādair viśeṣadhīḥ ||
nādena saṃskṛtāc chrotrād yadā śabdaḥ pratīyate | tadupaśleṣas tat asya bodhaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
naiva vā grahaṇaṃ teṣāṃ śabde buddhis tu tadvaśāt | saṃskārānukṛteḥ so 'pi mahatvādyavabudhyate ||
madhuraṃ tiktarūpeṇa śvetaṃ pītatayā tathā | gṛhṇanti pittadoṣeṇa viṣayaṃ bhrāntacetasaḥ ||
tathā vegena dhāvanto nāvyārūḍhāś ca gacchataḥ | parvatādīn vijānanti bhrameṇa bhramataś ca tān ||
maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṃśānuragabuddhibhiḥ | vyaktyalpatvamahattvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ ca tadāśrtayam ||
gṛhṇanti yadvadetāni nimittagrahaṇād vinā | vyañjakasthamabudhvaiva vyaṅgye bhrāntir bhaviṣyati ||
varṇāntaratvam evāhuḥ ke cid dīrghaplutādiṣu | na hi drutādivat tatra prayoho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
tathā ca sati sāmānyaṃ triṣvatvaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate | sāmānyakalpanā tv anyair na yuktety abhidhīyate ||
atvam ity ucyamānaṃ hi na dīrghaplutayor bhavet | ātvaṃ na hrasvaplutayos traimātryaṃ na ca pūrvayoḥ ||
sarvasādhāraṇatvena tad vijñātuṃ na śakyate | pratyekaṃ śābaleyādirūpe gotvaṃ yathā sphuṭam ||
avarṇakulaśabdo 'pi sthānasāmyād vanādivat | samudāyārthavācīti na jātivacano bhavet ||
svato hrasvādibhedas tu nityavāde virudhyate | sarvadā yasya sadbhāvaḥ sa kathaṃ mātrikaḥ svayam ||
tasmād uccāraṇaṃ tasya mātrākālaṃ pratīyate | dvimātraṃ vā trimātraṃ vā na varṇo mātrikaḥ svayam ||
dīrghāder nanv anaṅgatvaṃ vācakādharmato bhavet | itthaṃ pratīyamānāḥ syur varṇā na pratipādakāḥ ||
yādṛśāt pūrvadṛṣṭo 'sāv artho gamyate tādṛśāt | bhrāntyā kathaṃ pratītiś cet, nāsāv artham iti prati ||
yathāśvādijavaḥ puṃsāṃ kāryāṅgatvaṃ prakalpayet | paradharmo 'pi varṇānāṃ dhvanidharmās tathaiva naḥ ||
nanu dīrghādyanityatvād anityo vācako bhavet | ānupūrvīvad evāsya parihāro bhaviṣyati ||
tathodāttādibhedānāṃ saṃskāravaśagā matiḥ | teṣāṃ dīrghādivad bhedo na kadā cit pratīyate ||
tatraikavarṇarūpatve bhedo 'pi syād drutādivat | nātra varṇāntaravyaktir iva dhvanyantarodbhavaḥ ||
ta eva mṛdutīvratvaśīghratvādisamanvitāḥ | abhede cāpi varṇasya dhvanīnāṃ dviprakāratā ||
ke cit svarūpabodhārthāḥ ke cid bodhānuvartinaḥ | yugapatkramarūpeṇa saṃskārotpādahetavaḥ ||
tatra dīrghādibodhaḥ syāt pūrveṣāṃ pracayo yadā | varṇātmaiva hi kālena tāvatā taiḥ pratīyate ||
yugapatpracitais taiś ca syād udāttādikalpanā | pracaye tv itareṣāṃ syād vatibhedo drutādikaḥ ||
varṇātmanyavabuddhe 'pi tadrūpām eva te matim | śanair utpādayanti, iti nānyo varṇaḥ pratīyate ||
vyaktyākṛtikṛto bhedo yady apy ekāntato bhavet | varṇeṣu jaimineḥ pakṣas tathāpi na virudhyate ||
nityatvayatnaḥ sarvo 'pi gatvādiṣu bhaviṣyati | gakārādivacaś caitat teṣv eva na virotsyate ||
vicchinnayatnavyaṅgyaiś ca nityaiḥ sarvagatair api | vyatiriktapadārambho varṇair nātropapadyate ||
anārabdhe ca gośabde gośabdatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet | varṇasāmānyavac cāpi na tatkalpanam arhati ||
varṇātmanām abhedāc ca siddhā sāmānyadhīr api | samudāyo 'pi tebhyo 'syo vāraṇīyo 'nayā diśā ||
abhedasamudāyas tu teṣāṃ dharmo na duṣyati | teṣām asti hi sāmarthyam arthapratyāyanaṃ prati ||
yāvanto yādṛśo ye ca yadarthapratipādane | varṇāḥ prajñātasāmarthyāste tathaivāvabodhakāḥ ||
teṣāṃ tu guṇabhūtānām arthapratyāyanaṃ prati | sāhityam ekakartrādikramaś cāpi vivakṣitaḥ ||
kartraikatve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam | prayuñjānasya yat pūrvaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ kramadarśanam ||
yaugapadyaṃ tv aśakyatvān naiva teṣām ihāśritam | kartṛbhedaś ca tatra syāt, na caivaṃ dṛśyate 'bhidhā ||
yugapad dṛśyasāmarthyā naiva śaktāḥ krame yathā | bhāvās tathā krame śaktā yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ ||
dṛṣṭaś ca pūrṇamāsādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatyakāriṇaḥ | abhyāsānāṃ ca loke 'pi svādhyāyagrahaṇādiṣu ||
sādhanāditrayāṇāṃ ca vyāpārasyaikakālatā | sarvatrāstīti neha syād upālambhaḥ kramaṃ prati ||
niṣpannā eva dṛśyante vyāpārāḥ sarva eva hi | sūkṣmā vyāpārabhedās tu dṛśyate na kadā cana ||
ekasādhanasāṃsthāś ca vyāpārāvayavā yadā | svarūpato nirīkṣyante yaugapadyam asat tadā ||
kiṃ punar bahavo bhinnā bhinnasādhanasaṃśritāḥ | bhaveyur yaugapadyena vyāpārāḥ kramavartinaḥ ||
yadā tv ādyaparispandād prabhṛtyā phalalābhataḥ | kriyā pūrvaparībhūtā lakṣyate varttate tadā ||
tenātrāpi vivakṣātaḥ prabhṛtyā 'rthāvabodhanāt | sākalyenekṣyamāṇe syād vyāpāre varttamānatā ||
pratyekaṃ ye punas tatra vyāpārās tannirūpaṇam | phalāniṣpattito na syān nāstitvaṃ na ca tāvatā ||
phalānumeyatāyāṃ ca vyāpārasya phalaṃ prati | kārakāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ vyāpāre vartamānatā ||
avaśyam bhāvinī nityaṃ pratyāsattiś ca kasya cit | na tāvatā vyapetatvāt itareṣām anaṅgatā ||
dvyantaraikāntaratvena gakārau kārayor dhruvam | arthaṃ pratyāyane śaktis tatra sthau gamakau yataḥ ||
yathā visarjanīyasya vyavadhāne na śaktatā | tathaivetarayoḥ śaktir ānantarye na vidyate ||
na ca yatraikaśo 'śaktis tatra sarveṣv aśaktatā | tathā hy aṅgāni dṛśyante śālyādivahanādiṣu ||
śaktis tatrāsti kā cid dhi vahane sā samṛddhyate | saṅghātena tu varṇānāṃ pratyekaṃ kā cidīkṣyate ||
na hy arthāvayavaḥ kaś cit pratyekaṃ taiḥ pratīyate | samastasyātha vā kaś cid bodhaleśo 'tra jāyate ||
rathasyāpi tu yat kāryaṃ śālyādivahanaṃ na tat | pratyekaṃ dṛśyate kiñ cin manāg api yathehitam ||
atha yatkiñcid ucyeta vahane tad ihāpi naḥ | svātmapratyayahetutvaṃ varṇeṣv arthe 'pi vā kva cit ||
yasyānavayavaḥ sphoṭo vyajyate varṇabuddhibhiḥ | so 'pi paryanuyogena vaivaitena vimucyate ||
tatrāpi prativarṇaṃ hi padasphoṭo na gamyate | na cāvayavaśo vyaktis tadabhāvān na cātra dhīḥ ||
pratyekaṃ cāpy aśaktānāṃ samudāye 'py aśaktayā | tatra yaḥ parihāras te sa no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||
sadbhāvavyatirekau ca tathāvayavavarjanam | tavādhikaṃ bhavet tasmād yatno 'sāv arthabuddhiṣu ||
nānyathānupapattiś ca bhaved arthamatiṃ prati | tad evāsyā nimittaṃ syāj jāyate yadanantaram ||
sā ca varṇadvayajñāne 'tīte 'ntyajñānataḥ parā | bhavatītīdṛg evāsyā nimittam avakalpate ||
vinā saṃskārakalpena tadanantaravṛttitaḥ | kṛtānugrahasāmarthyo varṇo 'ntyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
eṣa eva tu saṃskāra iti ke cit pracakṣate | adṛṣṭakalpanātītaṃ tāvan mātraṃ hi dṛśyate ||
atha vā vāsanaivāstu saṃskāraḥ, sarva eva hi | dṛḍhajñānagṛhīte 'rthe saṃskāro 'stīti manvate ||
tasyārthabuddhihetutve visaṃvādo 'sya nirṇaye | tadbhāvabhāvitāhetur anyatreva pratīyate ||
saṃskāre niṣpramāṇe tu pūrvavṛttattvakalpanam | niṣpramāṇakam eveti nānugrahaphalaṃ bhavet ||
yady api smṛtihetutvaṃ saṃskārasya vyavasthitam | kāryāntareṣu sāmarthyaṃ na tasya pratiṣidhyate ||
tena saṃskārasadbhāvo nānenaivaṃ prakalpyate | tasyārthabuddhihetutvam adṛṣṭaṃ kevalaṃ kṛtam ||
śabdapakṣe 'pi tac caitad adṛṣṭatvān na mucyate | kāryabodhanaśaktatvaṃ tulyaṃ saṃskāraśabdayoḥ ||
kṣīṇārthāpattir evaṃ ca na sphoṭaṃ parikalpayet | saṃskārakalpanā pūrvam avaśyam bhāvinī hi te ||
dhvanibhyo 'py aparas tāvan neṣyetārthamatiṃ prati | te vā yady upalabhyeran varṇāḥ pratyakṣato na ca ||
varṇānāṃ yaugapadyena yadi cāvaśyam arthitā | nityatvāt sarvadā tat syān na tu kāraṇatā tathā ||
itthaṃ kramagṛhītānāṃ yugapad yātha vā parā | sthitiḥ sā kāraṇaṃ tu syān nityam arthadhiyaṃ prati ||
yad vā pratyakṣataḥ pūrvaṃ kramajñāneṣu yat param | samastavarṇavijñānaṃ tadarthajñānakāraṇam ||
tatra jñāne ca varṇānāṃ yaugapadyaṃ pratīyate | nāvaśyaṃ yaugapadyena pratyakṣasthena tad bhavet ||
citrarūpāṃ ca tāṃ buddhiṃ sadasadvarṇagocarām | ke cid āhur yathā varṇo gṛhyate 'ntaḥ pade pade ||
antyavarṇe 'pi vijñāte pūrvasaṃskārakāritam | smaraṇaṃ yaugapadyena sarveṣv anye pracakṣate ||
sarveṣu caivam artheṣu mānasaṃ sarvavādinām | iṣṭaṃ samuccayajñānaṃ kramajñāneṣu satsv api ||
na cet tadābhyupeyeta kramadṛṣṭeṣu naiva hi | śatādirūpaṃ jāyeta tatsamuccayadarśanam ||
tena śrotramanobhyāṃ syāt kramād varṇeṣu yady api | pūrvajñānaṃ parastāt tu yugapat smaraṇaṃ bhavet ||
tadārūḍhās tato varṇā na dūre 'rthāvabodhanāt | śabdādarthamatis tena laukikair abhidhīyate ||
citrabuddhyānayā bhrāntyā varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ | paścād gaur iti vijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate ||
vailakṣaṇyaṃ tu tasyeṣṭam ekaikajñānataḥ sphuṭam | varṇarūpāvabodhāt tu na tadarthāntaraṃ bhavet ||
yadi cārthāntaratvaṃ syād ekaikasmād trayasya tat | varṇatrayaparityāge buddhir nānyatra jāyate ||
gaur ity ekamatitvaṃ tu naivāsmābhir nivāryate | tadgrāhyaikārthatābhyāṃ ca śabde syād ekatāmatiḥ ||
śaidhyād alpāntaratvāc ca gośabde sābhaved api | devadattādiśabdeṣu sphuṭo bhedaḥ pratīyate ||
na gauṇaḥ śabda ity evaṃ granthasambandhanaṃ bhavet | asy akṣareṣu hetutvaṃ tatparaṃ vacanaṃ hi tat ||
śabdād iti ca hetutvaṃ pañcamyātrābhidhīyate | bhavatpakṣe 'pi caikāntāj jñānena vyavadhir bhavet ||
gauṇo 'nyathā prasiddho vā prayujyetānyathā yadi | na cānyādṛṅnimittatvaṃ kasya cit sampratīyate ||
svavyāpāravyavāyo hi sarvasminn eva kārake | dṛṣṭo vyāpāra īdṛk tu śabdasyety avyavetatā ||
gakārāder yadā cānyo na loke śabda ucyate | tadā tasmāt pratīte 'rthe śabdād iti kathaṃ bhavet ||
śabdajñānādisaṃskāravyaktasphoṭakṛte 'tha vā | pratyaye śabdajanyatvam iti gauṇaṃ prasajyate ||
saṃskārajananārthaṃ ca na śabdoccāraṇaṃ matam | arthapratītim uddiśya prayuktasya kramādayam ||
tasmāt tādarthyataḥ śabdaḥ phalena vyapadiśyate | samuccayāvabodhe tu vyavadhānaṃ na kena cit ||
yadi cāpūrvasaṃskāra itikartavyateṣyate | varṇo 'ntyo gamakas tasya śabdatvān mudhyatā bhavet ||
varṇā vā dhvanayo vāpi sphoṭaṃ na padavākyayoḥ | vyañjanti vyañjakatvena yathā dīpaprabhādayaḥ ||
sattvād ghaṭādivac ceti sādhanāni yathāruci | laukikavyatirekeṇa kalpite 'rthe bhavanti hi ||
nārthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭo varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ | ghaṭāvivat, na dṛṣṭena virodho dharmasiddhitaḥ ||
pratiṣedhet tu yo varṇān tajjñānānantarodbhavān | dṛṣṭabādho bhavet tasya śaśicandraniṣedhavat ||
varṇotthā vārthadhīreṣā tajjñānānantarodbhavā | yedṛśī sā tadutthā hi dhūmāder iva bahnidhīḥ ||
dīpavad vā gakārādir gavādeḥ pratipādakaḥ | dhruvaṃ pratīyamānatvāt, tatpūrvaṃ pratipādanāt ||
varṇātiriktaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ padeṣu mandaṃ phalam ādadhāti | kāryāṇi vākyāvayavāśrayāṇi satyāni kartuṃ kṛta eṣa yatnaḥ ||

§ 5,13 ākṛtivāda AKV

ākṛtivyatirikte 'rthe sambandho nityatāsya ca | na sidhyetām iti jñātvā tad vācyatvam ihocyate ||
tatsadbhāvaprasiddhyartham atra tāvat prayatyate | vācyatve vakṣyate yuktir vyaktyā saha balābale ||
jātim evākṛtiṃ prāhur vyaktir ākriyate yayā | sāmānyaṃ tac ca piṇḍānām ekabuddhinibandhanam ||
tannimittaṃ ca yatkiñcit sāmānyaṃ śabdagocaram | sarva evecchatīty evam avirodho 'tra vādinām ||
sarvavastuṣu buddhiś ca vyāvṛttyanugamātmikā | jāyate dvyātmakatvena vinā sā ca na siddhyati ||
viśeṣamātra iṣṭe ca na sāmānyamatir bhavet | sāmānyamātrabodhe tu nirnimittā viśeṣadhīḥ ||
na cāpy anyatarā bhrāntir upacāreṇa ceṣyate | dṛḍhatvāt sarvadā buddher bhrāntis tadbhrāntivādinām ||
mukhyayoś cāpy adṛṣṭatvān nopacāreṇa kalpanā | bāhyārthaviṣayatvaṃ ca buddhīnāṃ pratipāditam ||
anyonyāpekṣitā nityaṃ syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ | viśeṣāṇāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ te ca tasya bhavanti hi ||
nirviśeṣaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhavec chaśaviṣāṇavat | sāmānyarahitatvāc ca viśeṣās tadvad eva hi ||
tadanātmakarūpeṇa hetū vācyāvimau punaḥ | tena tātyantabhedo 'pi syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
sāmānyabuddhiśaktitvaṃ viśeṣeṣv eva yo vadet | vinā vastvantarāt, tena vācyā śaktis tu kīdṛśī ||
grāhyā kiṃ vāpy asambodhā bhinnaikā vā tathaiva ca | gṛhyate yadi saikā ca jātir evānyaśabdikā ||
bhaven nirviṣayā buddhir yadi śaktir na gṛhyate | na hi sadbhāvamātreṇa viśayaḥ kaś cid iṣyate ||
parasparavibhinnatvād viśeṣā naikabuddhibhiḥ | gṛhyante viṣayāsattvāc chaktiś caiṣāṃ na vidyate ||
bhinnatve vāpi śaktīnām ekabuddhir na labhyate | viśeṣaśaktyabhede ca tāvanmātramatir bhavet ||
bhinnā viśeṣaśaktibhyaḥ sarvatrānugatāpi ca | pratyekaṃ samavetā ca tasmāj jātir apīṣyatām ||
tenātmadharmo bhedānām ekadhīviṣayo 'sti naḥ | sāmānyam ākṛtir jātiḥ śaktir vā so 'bhidhīyatām ||
nanu bhinne 'pi sattādau sāmānyam iti jāyate | buddhir vināpi sāmānyād anyasmāt sā kathaṃ bhavet ||
vanopanyāsatulyo 'yam upanyāsaḥ kṛtas tvayā | bhrāntitvena hi naitasyā bhrāntir gotvādidhīr api ||
śabdāt pūrvaṃ hi sarveṣu gavādāv iva naikadhīḥ | vastutvaṃ cātra sāmānyaṃ dharmaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
evaṃ tu kalpyamāne syāt sāmānyānām anantatā | punas tena sahānyeṣu sāmānyamatir asti hi ||
viśeṣeṣv api vastutvāt sāmānyam iti dhīr bhavet | sattādiṣv iva, tenaitat sāmānyaṃ nopapadyate ||
tasmād ekasya bhinneṣu yā vṛttis tannibandhanaḥ | sāmānyaśabdaḥ sattādāv ekadhīkaraṇena vā ||
piṇḍeṣv eva ca sāmānyam, nāntarā gṛhyate yataḥ | na hy ākāśavadicchanti sāmānyaṃ nāma kiñ cana ||
yad vā sarvagatatve 'pi vyaktiḥ śaktyanurodhataḥ | śaktiḥ kāryānumeyā hi vyaktidarśanahetukā ||
tena yatraiva dṛśyeta vyaktiḥ śaktaṃ tad eva tu | tenaiva ca na sarvāsu vyaktiṣv etat pratīyate ||
bhinnatve 'pi hi kāsāñ cic chaktiḥ kāś cid aśaktikāḥ | na ca paryanuyogo 'sti vastuśakteḥ kadā cana ||
vahnir dahati nākāśaṃ ko 'tra paryanuyujyatām | na cānyā mṛgyate yuktir yathā sandṛśyate tathā ||
na hi yuktyantaraṃ nāstīty etaj jñānam anarthakam | dharmaś cāvyabhicāryasya na mṛgya upalakṣaṇe ||
nānumānāvagamyaṃ tat, pratyakṣe lakṣaṇena kim | svābhāvikaś ca sambandho jātivyaktyor na hetumān ||
tenaitasya prasiddhyarthaṃ nānyat sāmānyam iṣyate | śaktisiddhivadetasya svabhāvo 'tra na vāryate ||
yad vā naimittikatve 'pi tāvanmātrapratīkṣaṇāt | viśeṣeṣv eva labdheṣu keṣu cin nānyavāñchanam ||
na vyañjantyapare kasmād, yatas teṣu na dṛśyate | tebhyo 'pi na nivṛttyarthaṃ mṛgyo hetuḥ svabhāvataḥ ||
sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet tasya vṛtter niyāmakam | gotvenāpi vinā kasmād gobuddhir na niyamyate ||
yathā tulye 'pi bhinnatve keṣu cid vṛttyapekṣitā | gotvāder animitte 'pi tathā buddhir bhaviṣyati ||
viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnāṃ vinā notpattir iṣyate | viśeṣād anyad icchanti sāmānyaṃ tena tad dhruvam ||
tā hi tena vinotpannā mithyāḥ syur viṣayād ṛte | na tv anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasyeha duṣyati ||
aniṣyamāṇe sāmānye vṛttiḥ śabdānumānayoḥ | naiva syāt, na hi sambandho bhedair ānantyato bhavet ||
anubhūtatayā vāsau puruṣasyopayujyate | jātivyaktyos tu sambandhe nānubhūtyā prayojanam ||
siddhe viṣayarūpe ca gotvādāv indriyaiḥ punaḥ | arthāpattyupalabdhā syāc chaktir ekā niyāmikā ||
na cātmahetum evāsau siddhaṃ bādhitum arhati | śaktiś ca naitayā buddhyā, nendriyaiḥ sā hi gṛhyate ||
sāmānyāntarayogānām aniṣṭhā yā ca varṇyate | tayā sāmānyanāśaḥ syāt sa ca dṛṣṭena bādhyate ||
sambandhas tasya hetur vā tadgrahe na ca kāraṇam | svarūpato gṛhīte 'rthe paścād etad vikalpyate ||
sāsnādyekārthasambandhi gotvam ity upalakṣaṇam | na ca svasamavāyy eva kevalaṃ cihnam iṣyate ||
sāsnādibhyas tu piṇḍasya bhedo nātyantato yadā | sāmānyasya ca piṇḍebhyas tadā syād etad uttaram ||
kasmāt sāsnādimatsv eva gotvaṃ yasmāt tadātmakam | tādātmyam asya kasmāc cet svabhāvād iti gamyatām ||
upalabdhyanusāreṇa vyavasthāsiddhir īdṛśī | svato gotvādibhedas tu na tu vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
sā bhūd drutādivanmithyā, nyañjakasya tu kiṃkṛtaḥ | bhedo hastyādipiṇḍebhyaḥ, svataś cet, iha tatsamam ||
vyaṅgyajātiviśeṣāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam | tasmāt svābhāviko bhedo jātivyaktyoḥ pratīyate ||
anekānanyavṛttittvān na sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ | ekavastvātmatā yuktā varaṃ tenaupacārikam ||
bhinnebhyaś cāpy abhinnatvād bhedas tat svātmavad bhavet | ekasmād vāpy abhinnatvād vyaktyekatvaṃ pratīyate ||
ekānekatvam ekasya tathānyānanyatā katham | tat sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaś cety evamādi ca duṣkaram ||
virodhas tāvad ekāntād vaktum atra na yujyate | sāmānyānanyavijñāte viśeṣe naikavṛttitā ||
sāmānyānanyavṛttitvaṃ viśeṣātmaikabhāvataḥ | evañ ca parihartavyā bhinnābhinnatvakalpanā ||
kena cid dhy ātmanaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ cāsya kena cit | sāmānyasya tu yo bhedaṃ brūte tasya viśeṣataḥ ||
darśayitvābhyupetavyam, viśeṣaikyaṃ ca jātitaḥ | yathā kalmāṣavarṇasya yatheṣṭaṃ varṇanigrahaḥ ||
citratvād vastuno 'py evaṃ bhedābhedāvadhāraṇam | sāmānyāṃśe tu niṣkṛṣya bhedo yena prasādhyate ||
tasya hetor asiddhatvaṃ siddhaś cet siddhasādhanam | bhedebhyo 'nanyarūpeṇa sāmānyaṃ gṛhyate yadā ||
tadāviśeṣamātreṇa vastu pratyavabhāsate | tadudbhūtyā ca sāmānyaṃ tadbhāvānuguṇaṃ sthitam ||
sad apy agrāhyarūpatvād asadvat pratibhāti naḥ | viśeṣān api sāmānyād yadā bhedena buddhyate ||
tadā sāmānyamātratvam evam eva pratīyate | yadā tu śabalaṃ vastu yugapat pratipadyate ||
tadānyān anyabhedādi sarvam eva pralīyate | na ca tat tādṛśaṃ kaś cic chabdaḥ śaknoti bhāṣitum ||
sāmānyāṃśān apoddhṛtya padaṃ sarvaṃ pravarttate | samastavastvapekṣāṃ ca padārthānām apoddhṛtim ||
ke cid āhur asadrūpam, aṃśatvaṃ tu na vāryate | sārūpyam eva sāmānyaṃ piṇḍānāṃ yena kalpyate ||
tena sārūpyaśabdena kiṃ punaḥ pratipadyate | samānarūpabhāvaś cej jātiḥ sāsmābhir iṣyate ||
sādṛśyam atha sārūpyaṃ kasya keneti kathyatām | na tāvacchālaleyena bāhuleyādayaḥ samāḥ ||
viśeṣarūpataḥ, ye 'pi tatsaṃsthānādibhiḥ samāḥ | śābaleya iveti syāt tatra buddhir na gaur iva ||
śābaleyo 'yam iti vā bhrāntyā gaur iti nāsti dhīḥ | śābaleyasvarūpaṃ ca na gaur ity avatiṣṭhate ||
tadanyeṣu hi gobuddhir na syāt susadṛśeṣv api | dṛśyate sā na cānyatra gorūpaṃ tatra vidyate ||
na cānyo gauḥ prasiddho 'sti tatsādṛśyena dhīr bhavet | na cāpi sa iti jñānaṃ sadṛśeṣv asti sarvadā ||
sarvapuṃsām ato bhrāntir naiṣā bādhakavarjanāt | sarvajñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante 'tra kalpane ||
viśeṣagrahaṇābhāvād eva gauḥ kaś ca kathyatām | babhūva yady asau pūrvam asmadādes tadagrahāt ||
sādṛśyāvadhṛtir nāstīty ato godhīr na labhyate | na cāvayavasāmānyair vinā sādṛśyakalpanā ||
sāmānyapratyayotpādo na viśeṣeṣu jāyate | vyaktitaś cātireko 'sya syān na veti vicārite ||
sāmānyam eva sādṛśyaṃ bhaved vā vyaktimātrakam | tena nātyantabhinno 'rthaḥ sārūpyam iti varṇitam | granthe vindhyanivāsena bhrānteḥ sādṛśyam ucyate ||

§ 5,14 apohavāda APV

agonivṛttiḥ sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ yaiḥ parikalpitam | gotvaṃ vastv eva tair uktam ago 'pohagirā sphuṭam ||
bhāvāntaram abhāvo hi purastāt pratipāditaḥ | tatrāśvādinivṛttyātmā bhāvaḥ ka iti kathyatām ||
neṣṭo 'sādhāraṇas tāvad viṣayo nirvikalpanāt | tathā ca śābaleyādeḥ, asāmānyaprasaṅgataḥ ||
śābaleyādirūpaṃ hi na sāmānyaṃ parasparam | na vaikamitareṣāṃ vastatrānantārthatā bhavet ||
na ca sākṣād viśeṣasya te 'pohyā iti yuktimat | na śābaleyavijñānam agovyāvṛttibandhanam ||
nivṛttyā bāhuleyādes tadvijñānaṃ pravartate | kuryād agonivṛttiṃ cen nāpohetātmavad dhi tān ||
tenāṃśenānapohaś ca svarūpeṇāpy apohanam | kalpyate ced virodhaḥ syāt samamākṣepavāraṇe ||
tasmāt prātyātmikai rūpair ago 'poho na yujyate | samudāye 'pi naiteṣām agovyāvṛttisambhavaḥ ||
sarvopalabdhau tadbuddhir vyāsajyaivaṃ pravartate | na pratyekaṃ bhaved eṣā, na samasteṣv aśaktitaḥ ||
tasmāt sarveṣu yad rūpaṃ pratyekaṃ pariniṣṭhitam | gobuddhis tannimittā syād gotvād anyac ca nāsti tat ||
nanu ca prāgabhāvādau sāmānyaṃ vastu neṣyate | sattaiva hy atra sāmānyam anutpattyādirūṣitā ||
tām utpattyādyanusyūtāṃ satteti pratijānate | anyāpohānuviddhā tu saivābhāvaḥ pratīyate ||
anityatvaṃ vināśākhyakriyāsāmānyam ucyate | abrāhmaṇatvaṃ kin tu syād bhinneṣu kṣattriyādiṣu ||
puruṣatvaṃ catuḥsaṃstham, viśeṣeṣu ca nāstidhīḥ | sāmānyapratyayaś caiṣu pratyekam upajāyate ||
tenātra brāhmaṇābhāvaḥ sāmānyaṃ syād avastu tat | gotvādāv api tenaiva sāmānyapratyayo bhavet ||
kaiś cit tv atraikaśabdatvam akṣādāv iva kalpitam | jātitrayasya, naivaṃ tu sambhavatyaghaṭādiṣu ||
nātra hy anantake bhede sādhāraṇyaṃ nirūpyate | tasmāt kriyāguṇāḥ ke cid dhetavo 'nanyavartinaḥ ||
puruṣatvaṃ nañā caitad brāhmaṇebhyo nivartitam | cāturvarṇyaprasaktaṃ sad gamyate 'rthādibhir yathā ||
yady apy avāntarā nāsti triṣu jātir vyavasthitā | nañsāmārthyān naratvaṃ tu tryādhāraṃ sampratīyate ||
śabdasāmarthyabhedena varṇeṣu matibhinnatā | puṃstve tricaturādhāre paryudāsasvarūpataḥ ||
dūrāntike kṣaṇe śaktir gṛdhravāyasacakṣuṣoḥ | yathā rūpe tathā puṃstve pumabrāhmaṇaśabdayoḥ ||
brāhmaṇavyatiriktārthavṛtti puṃstvam itīdṛśam | vākyaṃ yatra pravarteta tatrābrāhmaṇadhīpade ||
pārthivatvādisāmānyam evam evāghaṭādiṣu | ghaṭatvādivinirmuktaṃ viṣayaḥ sampratīyate ||
asādhāraṇabhāvāc ca nañā śabdo viśeṣitaḥ | tāvanmātreṇa rahite sāmānye vyavatiṣṭhate ||
viśeṣe pratiṣiddhe hi sāmānyaṃ yadanantaram | sāmānyākāṅkṣiṇaṃ śabdaṃ niruṇad dhi tadātmani ||
prathamātikrame tasya kāraṇaṃ naiva vidyate | brāhmaṇatvād ato 'petaṃ naratvam avaśiṣyate ||
vyudasya brāhmaṇatvaṃ ca nañi jāte viśeṣaṇe | naratvodasanaṃ yat tu kalpetāśrutam eva tat ||
tasmād yasyaiva te bhedā niṣiddhyeraṃs tadarthataḥ | bhedāntarasthaṃ sāmānyam, loke 'py evaṃ pratīyate ||
prasaṅginyāṃ ca tadbuddhau niṣedho 'rthād apīṣyate | tanmātrarahite cārthe sādṛśyāt tanmatir bhavet ||
sādṛśyam eva vā vācyam iṣṭam abrāhmaṇādiṣu | tac cāvayavasāmānyād, vināpy etena lakṣyate ||
kva cid vināpi sādṛśyāt sāhacaryādihetukā | nañyuktaśabdavṛttiḥ syād yathā vakṣyaty anīkṣaṇe ||
īkṣaṇavyatiriktā hi kriyā tatrāpy apekṣitā | pratyāsatter na saṅkalpam atikramya pratīyate ||
nāmadhātvarthayogī ca naiva nañ pratiṣedhakaḥ | vadato 'brāhmaṇādharmāv anyamātravirodhinau ||
yatrāpy ākhyātasambandhāt pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate | tatraudāsīnyavastv eva pratipattā 'valambate ||
tasmād vastuny apohāḥ syuḥ, api cāvastukalpane | prāgantyebhyo viśeṣebhyo na kiñ cid vastu labhyate ||
na cāntyair vyavahāro 'sti, śakyaṃ naiṣāṃ nirūpaṇam | apohaśabdavācyātha śūnyatānyaprakārikā ||
tasyāṃ cāśvādibuddhīnām ātmāṃśagrahaṇaṃ bhavet | tatrānyāpohavācyatvaṃ mudhaivābhyupagamyate ||
sāmānyaṃ vasturūpaṃ hi buddhyākāro bhaviṣyati | śabdārtho 'rthānapekṣo hi vṛthāpohaḥ prakalpitaḥ ||
vasturūpā ca sā buddhiḥ śabdārtheṣūpajāyate | tena vastv eva kalpeta vācyaṃ buddhyanapohakam ||
asaty api ca bāhye 'rthe vākyārthapratibhā tathā | padārthe 'pi tathaiva syāt kim apohaḥ prakalpyate ||
buddhyantarād vyavacchedo na ca buddheḥ pratīyate | svarūpotpādamātrāc ca nānyam aṃśaṃ bibharti sā ||
bhinnasāmānyavacanā viśeṣavacanāś ca ye | sarve bhaveyuḥ paryāyā yady apohasya vācyatā ||
nanu bhedād apohānāṃ prasaṅgo 'yaṃ na yujyate | sāmānyāpohakḷptyā ced vastumātre samaṃ tava ||
bhidyante mama vastutvāt sāmānyāni parasparam | asaṅkīrṇasvabhāvāni na caikatvaṃ vitanvate ||
saṃsṛṣṭaikatvanānātvavikalparahitātmanām | avastutvād apohānāṃ tava syād bhinnatā katham ||
yadi vā bhidyamānatvād vastvasādhāraṇāṃśavat | avastutve tv anānātvāt paryāyatvān na mucyate ||
nanu cāpohyabhedena bhedo 'pohasya setsyati | na viśeṣaḥ svatas tasya parataś caupacārikaḥ ||
tenaivādhārabhedenāpy asya bhedo na yujyate | na hi sambandhibhedena bhedo vastuny apīṣyate ||
kim utāvastvasaṃsṛṣṭam anyataś cānivartitam | anavāptaviśeṣāṃśaṃ yat kim apy anirūpitam ||
tasmād yathaiva bhede 'pi piṇḍānāṃ naiva bhidyate | tathaivāpohyabhede 'pi nāneko 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
bhede vā pratipiṇḍaṃ syād ago 'pohaḥ, tathā sati | sāmānyaṃ śābaleyāder iti neṣṭaṃ prasidhyati ||
saṃsargiṇo 'pi cādhārā yaṃ na bhindanti rūpataḥ | apohyaiḥ sa bahirbhūtair bhidyetety atikalpanā ||
agavyaśvātirekaḥ syād anaśvaś ca gavādhikaḥ | śeṣaṃ hastyādyapohyaṃ tu dvayor api na bhidyate ||
tatraikabhedād bhedo 'stu bahvabhedād abhinnatā | bhūyasāṃ syāt sadharmatvam ity abhedaḥ prasajyate ||
gauś ca hastyādyapohena nāśvarūpād viśeṣyate | karoti tadapohaṃ ced aikarūpyaṃ virudhyate ||
sarvaśabdeṣu caikaikam apohyamatiricyate | tatrāsādhāraṇatvena tanmātrāpohyatā bhavet ||
tato 'śvāpoharūpatvāt siṃhādiḥ sarva eva te | tannimittam ago 'pohaṃ bibhrad ucyeta gaur iti ||
sarvāpoho yadīṣyeta, sa vaktavyaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ | yadi pratyekarūpeṇa nāpohyānantatā bhavet ||
bhinnatvāc cāpy apohyānāṃ bhinno 'pohaḥ prasajyate | tatraikasmin bhavet piṇḍe 'nantajātisamanvayaḥ ||
tato gaur iti sāmānyaṃ vācyam ekaṃ na sidhyati | jātyantaramatiś caiṣu bhavej jātyantareṣv iva ||
samudāyātmanā nāpi bhaved eṣām apohyatā | samudāyo hi naikena vinā dharmeṇa jāyate ||
nāpy ekadeśatā teṣām asti nāpy ekakālatā | vyatiriktaś ca saṅghātas teṣāṃ kaś cin na vidyate ||
yadi tv avyatiriktaḥ syād ānanyaṃ tadavasthitam | yadi sāmānyarūpeṇa te 'pohyante, na vastutā ||
kathaṃ vā vastv apohyeta, nābhāvo bhāvamṛcchati | apohyamāne cābhāve bhāva evāvaśiṣyate ||
apohyabhedakḷptiś ca nābhāvābhedato bhavet | tadbhedo 'pohabhedāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||
gosāmānyasya bhinnatvād agaur ity eṣa bhidyate | agaur ity asya bhedena gosāmānyaṃ ca bhidyate ||
agāvo 'śvādayaś ca syus te 'py abhāvātmakāḥ punaḥ | karkādyapekṣayā te 'pi tathety evaṃ na gamyate ||
kim apohyam, kva cāpohaḥ, gopiṇḍeṣv evam eva ca | tatra syād dvayam apy etadantyeṣu paramāṇuṣu ||
na cāntyeṣu dvayor asti vyavahāro bhidāṃ prati | gavāśvaparamāṇūnāṃ viśeṣaś ca na vidyate ||
svarūpajātisaṃsthānaparimāṇādilakṣaṇaḥ | kim apohyaṃ kva cāpohas tatrāpi na viśiṣyate ||
na cāprasiddhasārūpyānapohaviṣayātmanā | śaktaḥ kaś cid api jñātuṃ gavādīnaviśeṣataḥ ||
apohyān api cāśvādīnekadharmānvayād ṛte | na nirūpayituṃ śaktis tatrāpoho na siddhyati ||
na cānvayavinirmukte pravṛttir liṅgaśabdayoḥ | tābhyāṃ ca na vināpoho na cāsādhāraṇe 'nvayaḥ ||
apohaś cāpy aniṣpannaḥ sāhacaryaṃ kva dṛśyatām | tasminn adṛśyamāne ca na tayoḥ syāt pramāṇatā ||
na cādarśanamātreṇa tābhyāṃ pratyāyanaṃ bhavet | sarvatraiva hy adṛṣṭatvāt pratyāyyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
athāsaty api sārūpye syād apohasya kalpanā | gavāśvayor ayaṃ kasmād ago 'poho na kalpyate ||
śābaleyāc ca bhinnatvaṃ bāhuleyāśvayoḥ samam | sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet kvāgo 'pohaḥ pravartatām ||
indriyair nāpy ago 'pohaḥ prathamaṃ vyavasīyate | nānyatra śabdavṛttiś ca kiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa prayujyatām ||
pūrvoktena prabandhena nānumāpy atra vidyate | sambandhānubhavo 'py asya tena naivopapadyate ||
nivṛttivācinaḥ śabdā na prasiddhāś ca yān prati | teṣām agor asiddhatvān na sāmānyanirākriyā ||
agośabdābhidheyatvaṃ gamyatāṃ ca kathaṃ punaḥ | na dṛṣṭo yatra gośabdaḥ sambandhānubhavakṣaṇe ||
ekasmāt tarhi gopiṇḍād yadanyat sarvam eva tat | bhaved apohyam ity evaṃ na sāmānyasya vācyatā ||
siddhaś cāgaur apohyeta goniṣedhātmakaś ca saḥ | tatra gaur eva vaktavyo nañā yaḥ pratiṣidhyate ||
sa ced agonivṛttyātmā bhaved anyonyasaṃśrayaḥ | siddhaś ced gaur apohyārthaṃ vṛthāpohaprakalpanā ||
gavyasiddhe tv agaur nāsti tadabhāve ca gauḥ kutaḥ | nādhārādheyavṛttyādisambandhaś cāpy abhāvayoḥ ||
na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'pohavat tayā | kathaṃ vā parikalpyeta sambandho vastvavastunoḥ ||
svarūpasattvamātreṇa na ca kiñ cid viśeṣaṇam | svabuddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyaṃ tad viśeṣaṇam ||
na cāpy aśvādiśabdebho jāyate 'pohabodhanam | viśiṣṭabuddhir iṣṭeha na cājñātaviśeṣaṇā ||
na cānyarūpam anyādṛk kuryāj jñānaṃ viśeṣaṇam | kathaṃ cānyādṛśe jñāte tad ucyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
athānyathā viśeṣye 'pi syād viśeṣaṇakalpanā | tathā sati hi yatkiñcit prasajyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
abhāvarūpagamye ca na viśeṣye 'sti vastutā | viśeṣitam apohena vastu vācyaṃ na te 'sty ataḥ ||
yady apy apohanirmukte na vṛttiḥ śabdaliṅgayoḥ | yuktā tathāpi buddhis tu jñātur vastvavalambate ||
na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu buddhau viparivarttate | na cāpi nirvikalpatvāt tasya yuktā viśeṣyatā ||
śabdenāgamyamānaṃ ca viśeṣyam iti sāhasam | tena sāmānyam eṣṭavyaṃ viṣayo buddhiśabdayoḥ ||
yadā cāśabdavācyatvān na vyaktīnām apohyatā | tadāpohyeta sāmānyaṃ tasyāpohāc ca vastutā ||
nāpohyatvam abhāvānām abhāvābhāvavarjanāt | vyakto 'pohāntare 'pohas tasmāt sāmānyavastunaḥ ||
abhāvasya ca yo 'bhāvaḥ sa cet tasmād vilakṣaṇaḥ | bhāva eva bhaven no ced gaur agaus te prasajyate ||
yady apy aneṣu śabdeṣu vastunaḥ syād apohyatā | sacchabdasya tv abhāvākhyān nāpohyaṃ bhinnam iṣyate ||
tatrāsato 'pi bhāvatvam itikleśo mahān bhavet | tadasiddhau na sattāsti na cāsattā prasidhyati ||
na cāpi vāsanābhedād bhedaḥ sadrūpatāpi vā | apohānāṃ prakalpyeta, na hy avastuni vāsanā ||
smṛtiṃ muktvā na cāsty asyāḥ śaktiyogaḥ kriyāntare | tasmān nānyādṛśe sārthe karoty anyādṛśīṃ matim ||
bhavadbhiḥ śabdabhedo 'pi tannimitto na labhyate | na hy asādhāraṇaḥ śabdo vācakaḥ prāgadṛṣṭitaḥ ||
bhinnatvāc cāpi naivaikā vāsanā taiḥ prakalpyate | na cāsti śabdavastv ekaṃ vāsanāṃ yat kariṣyati ||
tatra śabdāntarāpohe sāmānye parikalpite | tathaivāvasturūpatvāc chabdabhedo na kalpyate ||
vācakānāṃ yathā caivaṃ vācyavācakayor mithaḥ | na cāpy apohyabhedena bhedo 'stīty upapāditam ||
nāgṛhītaś ca gamakaḥ śabdāpohaḥ kathañ cana | pratyakṣaṃ na ca tacchaktaṃ na ca sto liṅgavācakau ||
yataḥ syād grahaṇaṃ tasya, liṅgādīnāṃ ca kalpane | na vyavastheti vācyaivaṃ vinā pratyakṣamūlataḥ ||
na gamyagamakatvaṃ syād avastutvād apohayoḥ | bhavatpakṣe, yathā loke khapuṣpaśaśaśṛṅgayoḥ ||
vṛṣṭimeghāsator dṛṣṭvā yady anaikāntikaḥ vadet | vastv evātrāpi matpakṣe bhavatpakṣe 'py adaḥ kutaḥ ||
vidhirūpaś ca śabdārtho yena nābhyupagamyate | na bhaved vyatireko 'pi tasya tatpūrvako hy asau ||
niṣedhadvayayogitvād asato yāpy abhāvatā | savastuke bhavet sāpi na tucche buddhyasambhavāt ||
nanu yuktyānayaivāyaṃ vastunāpi na bhidyate | apohas tena doṣo 'tra pūrvokto na bhaviṣyati ||
siddham evaṃ madiṣṭaṃ syāt, naivānyā gatir asti hi | abhāve vastubuddhir vā yad vā vastunyabhāvadhīḥ ||
tatrābhāvātmakatve syān nirnimittaiva vastudhīḥ | vastuny abhāvabodhas tu sidhyaty anyam apekṣya tu ||
apohamātravācyatvaṃ yadi cābhyupagamyate | nīlotpalādiśabdeṣu śabalārthābhidhāyiṣu ||
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvasāmānādhikaraṇyayoḥ | na siddhiḥ, na hy anīlatvavyudāse 'nutpalacyutiḥ ||
nāpi tatretaras tasmān na viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇe | śabdayor nāpi te syātām abhidheyānapekṣayoḥ ||
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na bhinnatvād apohayoḥ | arthataś caitad iṣyeta kīdṛśyādheyatā tayoḥ ||
na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'nyac ca nāsti te | agamyamānam aikārthyaṃ śabdayoḥ kvopayujyate ||
athānyāpohavad vastu vācyam ity abhidhīyate | tatrāpi paratantratvād vyāptiḥ śabdena durbalā ||
khaṇḍe bhinnavyapohyatvād yathaiva madhurādibhiḥ | śuklādivyāptyabhāvena nākṣepo na viśeṣaṇam ||
tathaivāsadvyudāsāṃśāvacchinnārthāvadhāraṇe | nāghaṭādinivṛttyaṃśavyāptiḥ śabdāt pratīyate ||
vyāptiś ced artharūpeṇa sattayaivaṃ hi sā bhavet | na ghaṭatvādimān arthaḥ kaś cin na vyāpyate tayā ||
na ca vastutayā vyāptis tayā śabdasya vāryate | pratītiṃ prati tulyas tu vyāpāro vastvavastunoḥ ||
nirbhāgo 'pi hi vastvātmā śabdair bhāgena gamyate | na hi sacchabdavijñānād ghaṭādyarthaḥ pratīyate ||
tenānākṣepadoṣo 'sti, bhāktadoṣaś ca vidyate | viśeṣaṇatvān mukhyatvam apohasya hi jātivat ||
tasmāt tadvati gauṇatvān nābhidheyatvasambhavaḥ | avastutvān na mukhyaś cet, na syād evaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
bhedāś cāpohavantaḥ syus teṣāṃ cāvācyatoditā | ānantyavyabhicārābhyām, anyo nāsti tv apohavān ||
nāpohavattvam anyad dhi bhedāpohāntare 'sti te | tac cāpi kalpyamānaṃ syād abhāvo bhāva eva vā ||
vastu cej jātir eva syād avastutve 'pi pūrvavat | sambandho vaiṣa kalpyeta tasya ceṣṭā na vācyatā ||
na caiko 'pohavān artho vartate 'rthāntare kva cit | tasmād api na sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ na ca viśeṣaṇam ||
nātmanyavidyamānatvād viśeṣo 'pohasūcakaḥ | tasmān na tair viśeṣyatvaṃ prakṛṣṭatvena nīlavat ||
arthākṣepo 'pi nāsty eva sandehāl liṅgaliṅgivat | na sāmānyātmanāpohas tair vinā na ca siddhyati ||
evam eva tv anākṣepaḥ syād apohena vastunaḥ | yataḥ śaśaviṣāṇe 'pi tadapohasya sambhavaḥ ||
liṅgasaṃkhyādisambandho na vāpohasya vidyate | vyakter avyapadeśyatvāt taddvāreṇāpi nāsty asau ||
na hy asādhāraṇatvena sāpohenāpi gamyate | na cāpy agamyamānasya vastunaḥ syād viśeṣyatā ||
liṅgasaṃkhyādyapohānāṃ nopakāraḥ svarūpataḥ | vastunaś copakāryatvaṃ kathaṃ śabdaiḥ pratīyate ||
na vinānupalabdhyā ca syād abhāvamatiḥ kva cit | na cābhāvaprameyatvaṃ gotvāder iha gamyate ||
ākhyāteṣu ca nānyasya nivṛttiḥ sampratīyate | na paryudāsarūpaṃ hi niṣedhyaṃ tatra vidyate ||
na neti hy ucyamāne 'pi niṣedhasya niṣedhanam | pacatīty aniṣiddhaṃ tu svarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate ||
sādhyatvapratyayaś cātra tathābhūtādirūpaṇam | niṣpannatvād apohasya nirnimittaṃ prasajyate ||
vidhyādāv artharāśau ca nānyāpohanidarśanam | nañaś cāpi nañā yuktād apohaḥ kīdṛśo bhavet ||
cādīnām api nañyogo naivāstīty anapohanam | vākyārtho 'nyanivṛttiś ca vyapadeṣṭuṃ na śakyate ||
ananyāpohaśabdādau vācyaṃ na ca nirūpyate | prameyajñeyaśabdāder apohyaṃ kuta eva tu ||
apohyakalpanāyāṃ tu varaṃ vastv eva kalpitam | jñānākāraniṣedhāc ca nāntarārthābhidheyatā ||
na cāpy apohyatā, tasmān nāpohas teṣu sidhyati | evam ityādiśabdānāṃ na vāpohyaṃ nirūpyate ||
virodhitvena bhedānām apoho yadi kalpyate | virodho 'pohatas tatra virodhāc cāpy apohanam ||
na sāmānyāpahāritvaṃ vidhirūpeṇa tatra te | palaśādīn apohyāto vṛkṣaṃ harati śiṃśapā ||
sāmānyādyanapohaś ca nāvirodhena kalpyate | na hi śabdasvarūpāṇāṃ syād viruddhāviruddhatā ||
na ca vastusvarūpeṇa tasya śabdair asaṅgateḥ | prāk śabdavyāpṛter nāpi sāpohānāṃ pratīyate ||
anyenānavabuddhe 'rthe sadā śabdaḥ pravartate | sāmānyātmakatā tasya kena rūpeṇa gamyate ||
śabdānurūpataś cet syād anyāpohanirūpaṇam | bhinnatvād vṛkṣatarvāder apohaḥ kena vāryate ||
śabdaspṛṣṭer vināpoho na ca liṅgena gamyate | na viruddhāviruddhatvaṃ tasya liṅgāc ca sidhyati ||
adṛṣṭatvād vyudāsas tu purastād eva vāritaḥ | sāmānyaśabdo bhedena neṣyate vācakātmanā ||
vyudāsas tatra durvāraḥ, kathañ cid dṛṣṭatā punaḥ | brāhmaṇe kṣattriyasyāpi paryudāsaḥ prasajyate ||
ākāṅkṣaṇādathātyāgas tulyo dravyakriyādiṣu | vṛkṣeṇāto 'napohaḥ syāt tiṣṭhatyāder asaṃśayam ||
puruṣasya tathā rājño vyudāse na viśeṣyatā | avyudāsatvapakṣe ca syān nīlotpalatulyatā ||
vṛkṣatvapārthivadravyasajjñeyeṣu yaducyate | prātilomyānulomyena vidhau sarvārthabodhanam ||
tadayuktam, na sarvo hi śabdaḥ sarvatra dṛśyate | deśāvibhāgato vṛttir netrasyāpi rasādiṣu ||
grāhakatvena vṛttis tu pratijāti vyavasthitā | cakṣurādivad evātra saṅkaro na bhaviṣyati ||
nivṛttaceṣṭe śabde ca vyāptyavyāptikṛtaṃ punaḥ | sattvāder bodhakatvaṃ syād ekanyūnātirekataḥ ||
tavaiva doṣaḥ syād eṣa viśeṣe yasya varttate | sāmānyaśabdaḥ, vācyānāṃ bhedo nāpy asti vastutaḥ ||
api caikatvanityatvapratyekasamavāyitāḥ | nirupākhyeṣv apoheṣu kurvato 'sūtrakaḥ paṭaḥ ||
tasmād yeṣv eva śabdeṣu nañyogas teṣu kevalam | bhaved anyanivṛttyaṃśaḥ svātmaivānyatra gamyate ||
jñeyārthānyānapohatvaṃ pramāṅgatvāt tvagādivat | yenoktaṃ tasya nañyuktaiḥ śabdaiḥ syād vyabhicāritā ||
pakṣīkuryād yadā sarvāṃs tadāthāvītahetubhiḥ | anaikānto virodhaś ca sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
nāpohata itīdaṃ ca kārakatvena ced bhavet | kevalāpohabuddher vā tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatā ||
athānyāpohavatyarthe vṛttir nāstīti sādhyate | tataḥ prāk pakṣabādhaḥ syād gotve 'thāśvādyabhāvataḥ ||
sādhyahīnaś ca dṛṣṭāntaś cakṣurādy api tasya hi | varttate 'pohavatyeva taṃ yady api na budhyate ||
athānyāpohanirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddhasādhanam | apoharūpam apy etad vastv ity eva hi gamyate ||
athāpohanimittāsya vṛttir arthe niṣidhyate | vyatirekāṅgateṣṭatvāt punaḥ prāk pakṣabādhanam ||
anumāne tathā caitad ity anaikāntiko bhavet | sandehabādhajātena pratyakṣeṇāpi cetasā ||
viruddhatā ca hetoḥ syāt, śabdaḥ śrotrādivad yataḥ | ātmāntaḥ karaṇākāśaiḥ svavācitvaṃ jahāti vāḥ ||
vidhirūpapravṛttir vā śabdo 'pohena varttate | anumānāṅgabhūtatvād yathaiva pratiṣedhakaḥ ||
jātiṃ vā na bravīty eṣa vyaktiṃ vā tadviśeṣitām | pramāyām aṅgabhūtatvāt tvakśrotrādi yathaiva ca ||
evaṃ sādhanamārgeṇa vācyāvācyanirūpaṇā | nāvātiṣṭhata ity atra kathyate lokavartmanā ||

§ 5,15 vanavāda VAV

sāsnādibhir viśiṣṭatvam ākṛter ucyate katham | yadāvayavisambandhi gotvaṃ nāvayave sthitam ||
ekāvayavisambandhas teṣāṃ gotvena vidyate | tenāsādhāraṇatvāt te syur gotvasyopalakṣaṇam ||
piṇḍe sattādijātīnāṃ bahvīnāṃ samavetatā | tābhyo viśiṣyate gotvaṃ sāsnādibhir asaṃśayam ||
na caite vyañjakās tasya guṇavad vā viśeṣaṇam | tathā hi nāgṛhīteṣu teṣu syād gotvabodhanam ||
teṣāṃ ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syāt punargrahaṇakalpanā | tathā satyanavasthā syāt na syād gotvāvadhāraṇam ||
sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavenmatiḥ | gotve, na caiṣu sarveṣu yugapad buddhisambhavaḥ ||
tasmāt sadbhāvamātreṇa mahattvādau yathaiva dhīḥ | kriyate 'vayavaiḥ piṇḍe tathā jātiguṇādiṣu ||
yady evam agṛhīteṣu teṣu kiṃ sā na jāyate | taddeśavyatirekeṇa grāhyaṃ yena na vidyate ||
gṛhyamāṇe tu gotvādau nāntarīyakahetukaḥ | sāsnādeḥ kasya cid bodhas taddeśatvena jāyate ||
tadanatyantabhedād vā tadviśiṣṭeti kīrtyate | bādhaḥ parānumānasya na pratyakṣeti bodhyate ||
pareṣāṃ sādhanaṃ hy atra nākṛtiḥ piṇḍataḥ pṛthak | taddhīhānāv avijñānāt paṅktiyūthavanādivat ||
sarvatra lokasiddhatvān na vācyaṃ sādhanaṃ svayam | niṣedhatāṃ pareṣāṃ tu virodhaṃ lokato vadet ||
visaṃvādo na dṛśyeta yadi pratyakṣatākṛteḥ | pramāṇe 'pi visaṃvādāt tārkikeṣu kuto nv iyam ||
rūpādāv api teṣāṃ hi pratyakṣatvena sammate | vivādaḥ, naiva lokas tu jātau vipratipadyate ||
vyavahārā hi dṛśyante sāmānyārthanibandhanāḥ | dadhitakrādidānādau kauṇḍinyabrāhmaṇādiṣu ||
ākṛtir jātir evātra saṃsthānaṃ na prakalpyate | na hi vāyvagniśabdādau kiñ cit saṃsthānam iṣyate ||
anyadanyac ca saṃsthānaṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ pratīyate | saṃyogātmakatāyāṃ tu vibhāgeṣu vinaśyati ||
atha saṃsthānasāmānyam, aśvādāv api tatsamam | na gotvena vinā hy etad vyavacchinnaṃ pratīyate ||
sarvapratikṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsthāne saty apīdṛśe | na gotvādimatir dṛṣṭā, tasmāj jātiḥ pṛthak tataḥ ||
rucakādiṣu sāmānyaṃ rucakatvād yudāhṛtam | bhinneṣu caiṣu sāmānyaṃ suvarṇatvaṃ pratīyate ||
vardhamānakabhaṅge ca rucakaḥ kriyate yadā | tadā pūrvārthinaḥ śokaḥ prītiś cāpy uttarārthinaḥ ||
hemārthinas tu mādhyasthaṃ tasmād vastu trayātmakam | notpādasthitibhaṅgānām abhāve syān matitrayam ||
na nāśena vinā śoko notpādena vinā sukham | sthityā vinā na mādhyasthyam, tena sāmānyanityatā ||
mudgamāṣatilādau ca yatra bhedo na lakṣyate | tatraikabuddhinirgrāhyā jātir indriyagocaraḥ ||
ārād dṛṣṭe ca puruṣe sandeho brāhmaṇādiṣu | na syād yadi na gṛhyeta sāmānyaṃ cakṣurādinā ||
tasyopalakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kva cit kena cid iṣyate | rūpādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa deśakālādy apekṣayā ||
suvarṇaṃ bhidyate rūpāt tāmratvāder asaṃśayam | tailād ghṛtaṃ vilīnaṃ ca gandhena ca rasena ca ||
bhasmapracchādito vahniḥ sparśanenopalabhyate | aśvatvādau ca dūrasthe niścayo jāyate svanaiḥ ||
saṃsthānena ghaṭatvādi brāhmaṇatvādi yonitaḥ | kva cid ācārataś cāpi samyag rājānupālitāt ||
pratyekasamavetatvaṃ dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate | tathā saty api nānātvaṃ naikabuddher bhaviṣyati ||
na hi sambandhibhedena svarūpaikatvabādhanam | vibhutvāvayavābhāvau pratipādyau ca śabdavat ||
yathā ca vyatirekaiva dṛśyamānā punaḥ punaḥ | kālabhede 'py abhinnaiva jātir bhinnāśrayā satī ||
kārtsyāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ praṣṭuṃ jātau na yujyate | na hi bhedavinirmukte kārtsnyabhāgavikalpanam ||
tasmād vyaktiṣu jātīnāṃ vṛttir astīti gamyate | viśeṣāvasarābhāvāt tanmātraivāvatiṣṭhate ||
yā cāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ sraksūtrādiṣu dṛśyate | bhūtakaṇṭhaguṇādeś ca pratipiṇḍaṃ samāptitaḥ ||
tatrāvayavayogitvam avibhutvaṃca kāraṇam | ākṛtes tadabhāvena na prasaktamado dvayam ||
na ca dvaividhyam eveti vṛtter asti niyāmakam | trividhāpi hi dṛṣṭatvāt sambhaved dvividhā yathā ||
itaratra na dṛṣṭaṃ cet sragādiṣv api tatsamam | naiva hy anyonyatulyatvaṃ tayor nāpy anayā saha ||
na hy anyasminn adṛṣṭatvād vahner auṣṇyaṃ praṇaśyati | na cānumānagamyeyaṃ vāñched yena nidarśanam ||
svarūpataś ca dṛṣṭāyā vṛtter na pararūpataḥ | nirākriyopapadyeta tadviśeṣam apaśyatām ||
aṅgāṅgāsambhavāc cāpi yā pradhānanirākriyā | sā 'yuktaiva, anumānena pratyakṣajñānabādhanāt ||
tasmād asambhavo yasya tanmātrasyaiva bādhanam | yuktaṃ na tāvatānyo 'pi sambhavan bādham arhati ||
tena vaiśeṣikoktāpi jātiḥ sarvagatā satī | vyajyate yatra piṇḍena varṇavat tatra gṛhyate ||
tasmāt piṇḍeṣu gobuddhir ekagotvanibandhanā | gavābhāsaikarūpyābhām ekagopiṇḍabuddhivat ||
na śābaleyād gobuddhis tato 'nyālambanāpi vā | tadabhāve 'pi sadbhāvād ghaṭe pārthivabuddhivat ||
pratyekasamavetārthaviṣayā vāpi gomatiḥ | pratyekaṃ kṛtsnabuddhitvāt pratyekavyaktibuddhivat ||
pratyekasamavetāpi jātir ekaikabuddhitaḥ | nañyukteṣv api vākyeṣu brahmaṇādinivartanam ||
na ca sādṛśyaviṣayā godhīs tādrūpyajanmataḥ | prāmāṇye sati yadvad dhi pratyabhijñaikavastuni ||
naikarūpamatir gotve mithyā vaktuṃ ca śakyate | nātra kāraṇadoṣo 'sti bādhakapratyayo 'pi vā ||
yadā vyaktyatirekeṇa grāhyatvād anyatākṛteḥ | vanavannāsty anaikāntāt tatrāsambaddhatā katham ||
sādhanaṃ cen mayocyeta yujyeta vyabhicāritā | dūṣaṇatvadhiyā tv etad asambaddhatvam ucyate ||
nāstitvahetor uktaiṣā pratyakṣeṇa viruddhatā | parasya sādhanaṃ hy atra yat tat pūrvam udāhṛtam ||
pratyakṣābhāsatā cātra naivāsti vanabuddhivat | kasya cin na hi mithyātvāt sarvaṃ mithyety asaṅgatiḥ ||
yathā vanādibuddhīnāṃ mithyātvān na rasādidhīḥ | mithyaivaṃ jātibuddhiḥ syād viśeṣo vābhidhīyatām ||
vṛkṣebhyo vyatirekeṇa vane yaikamatir bhavet | dūratvadoṣāt tatra syād ākṛtau tu na vidyate ||
sannikṛṣṭasya vṛkṣeṣu buddhyekatvaṃ nivartate | kena cit tu prakāreṇa jātibuddhir na naśyati ||
yaikatvadhīr vinā śabdāt saivaṃ tāvan nirākṛtā | vanaśabdānuraktā tu madhyasthasyāpi jāyate ||
mithyātvakalpanā tv asyāḥ pratyakṣāder asambhavāt | jātiḥ sarvapramāṇais tu tadrūpaivāvagamyate ||
pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭe ca padam arthe prayujyate | tasmād dṛṣṭe prayuktasya mithyātvaṃ syād vanādiṣu ||
ke cin nityaṃ vanaikatvaṃ śabdagamyaṃ samāśritāḥ | anyaiḥ saṅgatyabhāve 'pi satyaṃ tat syād rasādivat ||
mithyātvaṃ yadasaṅgatyā tadajñāne prasajyate | jñāyamānasya doṣas tu na tu kaś cid asaṅgateḥ ||
pramāṇāntaragamye 'rthe padaṃ nityaṃ prayujyate | dharmo 'yaṃ na ca sarveṣāṃ padānām abhyupeyate ||
asty eva saṅgatiś cātra vṛkṣā hi bahavo vanam | te pramāṇāntarāj jñātāḥ, saṃkhyā caiṣānyavastuni ||
nānekasyaikaśabdyaṃ ced, ekaśeṣavad iṣyatām | tatra saṃkhyāvivṛddhiś ced, astu tanmātravarjanam ||
tasmāt sāmānyadṛṣṭena siddhaikatvasya saṅgatiḥ | tenānyānavagamyāpi saṃkhyā syāt sūryayānavat ||
ke cid bahutvasāmānyam āhur vṛkṣasthitaṃ vanam | tatra caikatvam asty eva, vanatvaṃ vāpi vidyate ||
vināpy ekāśrayatvena yathaivāvayavo tathā | asaṃyuktair abhivyaktir dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate ||
anyatrāpi ca tadbuddheḥ sāmānyaṃ tad bhaviṣyati | yathā ca bhramaṇatvādibhaṅgiṣv avayaveṣv api ||
vyaktaṃ nānāśrayatve 'pi gṛhyate vanatā tathā | yadvaikakāryahetutvād ekagośabdavad vanam ||
nityaṃ ye vyastavijñātā vṛkṣā neṣṭā hi te vanam | yad vā lakṣaṇayaikatvaṃ deśakālakriyādibhiḥ ||
dravyaikatvād vināpīṣṭaṃ paṅktiyūthavanādiṣu | vṛkṣāṇāṃ samudāye ca vanadhīr jāyate yathā ||
naivaṃ gosamudāye 'pi gotvadhīr upajāyate | yādṛśī vṛkṣadhīs tatra gotvadhīr api tādṛśī ||
vanavan nāpṛthaksiddheḥ samudāyatvakalpanā | na ca sāsnādisaṅghātas tadbuddhyālambanaṃ bhavet ||
kṣīṇeṣu piṇḍabuddhyaiṣu tatsāmānye hi gotvadhīḥ | tenāvayavyabhāve 'pi sāmānyaṃ vyatiricyate ||
pūrvoktād eva tu nyāyāt sidhyed atrāvayavy api | tasyāpy atyantabhinnatvaṃ na syād avayavaiḥ saha ||
vyaktibhyo jātivac caiṣa na niṣkṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate | kaiś cid avyatiriktatvaṃ kaiś cic ca vyatiriktatā ||
dūṣitā sādhitā vāpi na ca tatra balābalam | kadā cin niścitaṃ kaiś cit tasmān madhyasthatā varam ||
tato 'nyānanyate nasya sto na staś ceti kīrttyate | tasmāc citravadevāsya mṛṣā syād ekarūpatā ||
vastvanekatvavādāc ca na sandindhāpramāṇatā | jñānaṃ sandihyate yatra tatra na syāt pramāṇatā ||
ihānaikāntikaṃ vastv ityevaṃ jñānaṃ suniścitam | niṣkṛṣyāvayavān buddhyā yāvayavyapratītatā ||
buddhisthatvād vināśasya saulūkyasyāpi yujyate | vṛttiś cāvayaveṣv asya vyāsajyaiva pratīyate ||
tataḥ kārtsnyādisampraśnaḥ pratyākhyeyo 'tra jātivat | sāsnādiguṇahetuś cen nānyasmin gotvadhīr bhavet ||
bhinna eva hi sāsnādiḥ piṇḍāt piṇḍāntareyataḥ | na cāvayavasāmānyaṃ pareṣām upapadyate ||
tasmāt sāsnādito 'nyena gotvadhīr upajanyate | vanāntareṣa yā buddhir vanam ity upajāyate ||
tasyās tad eva vṛkṣatvaṃ grāhyaṃ bahvāśrayaṃ viduḥ | ekatve 'py ākṛter yadvad bahutvaṃ vyaktyapekṣayā ||
bahutve hi tathā vyakter ekatvaṃ jātyapekṣayā | ekānekābhidhāne ca śabdā niyataśaktayaḥ ||
ke cid vyaktiṃ tv asaṃkhyākāṃ gamayanty ambarādiṣu | eko vrīhiḥ suniṣpannaḥ iti jātiṃ svasaṃkhyayā ||
patnīsannahanādau tu vyaktim ākṛtisaṃkhyayā | kapiñjalādijātes tu pratītir vyaktisaṃkhyayā ||
vyaktijātī vadanty anye dravyāvayavasaṃkhyayā | asmān iti yathaikasmin pāśānaditir ity api ||
tatra vrīhyādiśabdānāṃ saṃkhyāyogo yathāruci | vanadārādiśabdās tu pravartante vyavasthayā ||
jaṅgame sthāvare cārthe yathā yūthavanādayaḥ | tatra vyaktau ca jātau ca dārādiś cet prayujyate ||
vyakter avayavānāṃ ca saṃkhyām ādāya vartate | vanaśabdaḥ punarvyaktīr jātisaṃkhyāviśeṣitāḥ ||
bahvīrāhātha vā jātiṃ bahuvyaktisamāśrayām | evaṃ paṅktyādiśabdānāṃ saṃyogādi viśeṣaṇam ||
sarveṣāṃ kiñ cid astīti na nirālambanaikadhīḥ | tulyaṃ pratyakṣayā ''kṛtyā vane yat tadasad yadi ||
vṛkṣās tatra tayā tulyā iti śūnyatvavāditā | pratyakṣābhāsagamyatvād vṛkṣebhyo 'nyat tu tadvanam ||
nā''kṛtyā saha tasyāsti sparddhā pratyakṣagamyayā | athā''kṛtyā vanaṃ tulyaṃ sadbhāvena prasajyate | jātipakṣavimokena vanasiddhāntadūṣaṇam ||
iti nigaditam etallokasiddhaiḥ padārthair vyavahṛtir iha śāstre na svatantrābhyupetaiḥ | bhavati ca janadṛṣṭyā jātipaṅktyādibhedo yadi tu na ghaṭate 'sau naiva bādho 'sti kaś cit ||

§ 5,16 sambandhākṣepaparihāra SAP

bhavetāṃ nāma śabdārthau yāvetāvuditau tvayā | yadarthas tu prayāso 'yaṃ sa sambandho nirūpyatām ||
pūrvam evopadiṣṭaḥ san sambandhaḥ kin tu pṛcchyate | svarūpākathanāc caitad uttaraṃ nopapadyate ||
kim auṣadhaṃ jvarasyeti pṛṣṭo yadi vaded idam | yenāsau naśyatīty evaṃ kiṃ tena kathitaṃ bhavet ||
tatra ke cid vadanty eva pūrvatrāparitoṣataḥ | praśnaḥ punarupakrāntaḥ sambandhāntaram icchatā ||
yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa pratītyuttaro yataḥ | sā cānyapūrvikā tasmān nāsya pratyāyanāṅgatā ||
ajānāno 'pi saṃjñātvaṃ sambandhāntaradarśanāt | buddhyate 'rthaṃ tataḥ paścāt kaś cit saṃjñeti manyate ||
tam evānyo 'vinābhāvam atra sambandham icchati | na hi tasmād vinā śabde jñāte syād arthabodhanam ||
tattvayuktam, na bhāṣye 'sti tādṛksambandhakīrtanam | yadi hy etāvatocyeta kiṃ nānuktaḥ pratīyate ||
prayuktaś cāvinābhāvasaṃjñā lokāt tu gamyate | saṃjñetyagamyamāne 'pi gamakatvaṃ pratīyate ||
tasmāt sa eva śabdārthacintāvyavahito 'dhunā | nityānityavicārārthaṃ sambandhaḥ smāryate punaḥ ||
yacchabde jñāta ity evaṃ śaktir evātra kīrtyate | kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā yat tasyārthābhidhāṃ prati ||
svato naivāsti śaktatvaṃ vācyāvācakayor mithaḥ | pratītiḥ samayāt puṃsāṃ bhaved akṣinikocavat ||
samayaḥ pratimartyaṃ yā pratyuccāraṇam eva vā | kriyate jagadādau vā sakṛdekena kena cit ||
pratyekaṃ vāpi sambandho bhidyetaiko 'tha vā bhavet | ekatve kṛtako na syād, bhinnaś ced bhedadhīr bhavet ||
bhinnatve pratisambandhaṃ śaktiḥ kalpyābhidhā prati | ekasmin jñātaśaktau vā nānyenārthamatir bhavet ||
atha yo yasya puṃsaḥ syāt sa tena pratipadyate | yasyānekena sambandhaḥ kṛtas tasya kathaṃ bhavet ||
ekārthānāṃ vikalpaś cet, netarātyantabādhanāt | samuccayo 'pi naiteṣāṃ vyavahāre 'vagamyate ||
kiñ cid evaikamādāya vyavahāro hi dṛśyate | bahubhiḥ kṛtasambandhe na caiko gamako bhavet ||
śabdārthayor abhede 'pi pumbahutve 'pi kartari | nāyaṃ veti matir dṛṣṭā vikalpo 'to na yujyate ||
gośabde sakṛdukte ca bhinneṣu pratipattṛṣu | vikalpyamāne sambandhe kaś cid budhyeta netare ||
samuccayo nṛbhedāc cet, na, vaktraikyād asambhavāt | vaktṛśrotṛdhiyor bhedād vyavahāraś ca duṣyati ||
vaktur anyo hi sambandho buddhau śrotus tathāparaḥ | śrotuḥ kartuṃ ca sambandhaṃ vaktā kaṃ pratipadyatām ||
pūrvadṛṣṭo hi yas tena śrotur naiva karoti tam | yaṃ karoti navaṃ so 'pi na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
sarvathā śrotṛsiddhiś ced, asiddhaṃ netaro vadet | ghaṭādāv api tulyaṃ cet, na, sāmānyaprasiddhitaḥ ||
yady api jñātasāmarthyā vyaktiḥ kartuṃ na śakyate | kriyate yā na tasyāś ca śaktiḥ kārye 'vadhāritā ||
tathāpy ākṛtitaḥ siddhā śaktir utpādanādiṣu | tasyā na cādimattāsti, sambandhas tvādimāṃs tava ||
yadi tatrāpi sāmānyaṃ nityam abhyupagamyate | tathāpy asmanmataṃ siddham, na tu dvyākārasambhavaḥ ||
śaktir eva hi sambandho bhedaś cāsyā na vidyate | sā hi kāryānumeyatvāt tadbhedam anuvartate ||
anyathānupapattyā ca śaktisadbhāvakalpanam | na caikayaiva siddhe 'rthe bahvīnāṃ kalpaneṣyate ||
sambandhākhyānakāle ca gośabdādāv udīrite | ke cit sambandhabuddhyārthaṃ buddhyante nāpare tathā ||
tatra sambandhanāstitve sarvo 'rthaṃ nāvadhārayet | astitve sarvabodhaś cet, na kaiś cid anupagrahāt ||
jñāpakatvād dhi sambandhaḥ svātmajñānam apekṣate | tenāsau vidyamāno 'pi nāgṛhītaḥ prakāśakaḥ ||
vidyamānasya cārthasya dṛṣṭam agrahaṇaṃ kva cit | na tv atyantāsato 'stitvaṃ kāṃś cit pratyupapadyate ||
viruddhau sadasadbhāvau na syātām ekavastuni | nanu tulyaṃ virodhitvaṃ jñātājñātatvayor api ||
jñānaṃ hi puruṣādhāraṃ tadbhedān na virotsyate | puruṣāntarasaṃsthaṃ ca nājñānaṃ tena bādhyate ||
sambandhādhāratāyāṃ ca virodhaḥ sadasattvayoḥ | pratyuktatvāc ca bhedasya tadvaśān nāvirodhitā ||
andhānandhasamīpasthaḥ śuklo 'ndhair nāvagamyate | gamyate cetarais tasya sadasattvena tāvatā ||
śaktyaśaktyor narāṇāṃ tu bhedāt tatrāvirodhitā | na hy anyo darśanasyāsti sambandhād dhetur atra hi ||
evam evendriyais tulyaṃ vyavahāropalambhanam | yeṣāṃ syāt te 'vabhotsyante tato 'rthaṃ netare 'ndhavat ||
ādhānavat sakṛś caitat tantreṇopakariṣyati | smaraṇaṃ bhetsyate cāsya vahnipraṇayanādivat ||
sarveṣām anabhijñānāṃ pūrvapūrvaprasiddhitaḥ | siddhaḥ sambandha ity evaṃ sambandhādir na vidyate ||
pratyuccāraṇanirvṛttir bhāṣya eva nirākṛtā | sargādau ca kriyā nāsti, tādṛkkālo hi neṣyate ||
yadi tv ādau jagat sṛṣṭvā dharmādharmau sasādhanau | yathā śabdārthasambandhān vedān kaś cit pravartayet ||
jagaddhitāya vedasya tathā kiñ cin na duṣyati | sarvajñavat tu dussādham ity atraitan na saṃśritam ||
yadā sarvam idaṃ nāsīt kvāvasthā tatra gamyatām | prajāpateḥ kva vā sthānaṃ kiṃ rūpaṃ ca pratīyatām ||
jñātā ca kas tadā tasya yo janān bodhayiṣyati | upalabdher vinā caitat katham adhyavasīyatām ||
pravṛttiḥ katham ādyā ca jagataḥ sampratīyate | śarīrāder vinā cāsya katham icchāpi sarjane ||
śarīrādy atha tasya syāt, tasyotpattir na tatkṛtā | tadvadanyaprasaṅgo 'pi, nityaṃ yadi tad iṣyate ||
pṛthivyādāv anutpanne kimmayaṃ tatpunarbhavet | prāṇināṃ prāyaduḥkhā ca sisṛkṣāsya na yujyate ||
sādhanaṃ cāsya dharmādi tadā kiñ canna vidyate | na ca nissādhanaḥ kartā kaś cit sṛjati kiñ cana ||
nādhāreṇa vinā sṛṣṭirūrṇanābher apīṣyate | prāṇināṃ bhakṣaṇāc cāpi tasya lālā pravarttate ||
abhāvāc cānukampyānāṃ nānukampāsya jāyate | sṛjec ca śubham evaikam anukampāprayojitaḥ ||
athāśubhād vinā sṛṣṭiḥ sthitir vā nopapadyate | ātmādhīnābhyupāye hi bhavet kiṃ nāma dṛṣkaram ||
tathā cāpekṣamāṇasya svātantryaṃ pratihanyate | jagac cāsṛjatas tasya kiṃ nāmeṣṭaṃ na sidhyati ||
prayojanam anuddiśya na mando 'pi pravartate | evam eva pravṛttiś cec caitanyenāsya kiṃ bhavet ||
krīḍārthāyāṃ pravṛttau ca vihanyeta kṛtārthatā | bahuvyāpāratāyāṃ ca kleśo bahutaro bhavet ||
saṃhārecchāpi caitasya bhaved apratyayāt punaḥ | na cakaiś cid asau jñātuṃ kādā cid api śakyate ||
svarūpeṇopalabdhe 'pi sraṣṭṛtvaṃ nāvagamyate | sṛṣṭyādyāḥ praṇino ye ca budhyantāṃ kiṃ nu te tadā ||
kuto vayam ihotpannāḥ iti tāvan na jānate | prāgavasthāṃ ca jagataḥ sraṣṭṛtvaṃ ca prajāpateḥ ||
na ca tadvacanenaiṣāṃ pratipattiḥ suniścitā | asṛṣṭvāpi hy asau brūyād ātmaiśvaryaprakāśanāt ||
evaṃ vedo 'pi tatpūrvastatsadbhāvādibodhane | sāśaṅko na pramāṇaṃ syāt, nityasya vyāpṛtiḥ kutaḥ ||
yadi prāg apy asau tasmād arthādāsīn na tena saḥ | sambaddha iti tasyānyas tadartho 'nyaprarocanā ||
stutivākyakṛtaś caiṣa janānāṃ mativibhramaḥ | paurvāparyāparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdo 'nyāṃ kurute matim ||
upākhyānādirūpeṇa vṛttir vedavad eva naḥ | dharmādau bhāratādīnāṃ bhrāntis tebhyo 'py ato bhavet ||
ākhyānānupayogitvāt teṣu sarveṣu vidyate | stutinindāśrayaḥ kaś cid vedas tac codito 'pi vā ||
vedasyādipravṛttau ca nākṛtatvamatir bhavet | pralayeṣu sthitiś cāsya sāśaṅkā syāt prajāpatau ||
kartṛsargavināśānām athānāditvakalpanā | saivaṃ yuktāyathedānīṃ bhūtānāṃ dṛśyate kramāt ||
pralaye 'pi pramāṇaṃ naḥ sarvocchedātmake na hi | na ca prayojanaṃ tena syāt prajāpatikarmaṇā ||
na ca karmavatāṃ yuktā sthitis tadbhogavarjitā | karmāntaraniruddhaṃ hi phalaṃ na syāt kriyāntarāt ||
sarveṣāṃ tu phalāpetaṃ na sthānam upapadyate | na cāpy anupabhogo 'sau kasya cit karmaṇaḥ phalam ||
aśeṣakarmanāśe vā punaḥ sṛṣṭir na yujyate | karmāṇāṃ vāpy abhivyaktau kiṃ nimittaṃ tadā bhavet ||
īśvarecchā yadīṣyeta, saiva syāl lokakāraṇam | īśvarecchāvaśitve hi niṣphalā karmakalpanā ||
na cānimittayā yuktam utpattuṃ hīśvarecchayā | yad vā tasyā nimittaṃ yat tad bhūtānāṃ bhaviṣyati ||
sanniveśaviśiṣṭānām utpattiṃ yo gṛhādivat | sādhayec cetanādhiṣṭhāṃ dehānāṃ tasya cottaram ||
kasya cid dhetumātratvaṃ yady adhiṣṭhātṛteṣyate | karmabhiḥ sarvajīvānāṃ tatsiddheḥ siddhasādhanam ||
icchāpūrvakapakṣe 'pi, tatpūrvatvena karmaṇām | icchānantarasiddhis tu dṛṣṭānte 'pi na vidyate ||
anekāntaś ca hetus te taccharīrādinā bhavet | utpattimāṃś ca taddeho dehatvād asmadādivat ||
atha tasyāpy adhiṣṭhānaṃ tenaivety avipakṣatā | aśarīro hy adhiṣṭhātā nātmā muktātmavad bhavet ||
kumbhakārādyadhiṣṭhānaṃ ghaṭādau yadi ceṣyate | neśvarādhiṣṭhitatvaṃ syād, asti cet sādhyahīnatā ||
yathāsiddhe ca dṛṣṭānte bhaved dhetor viruddhatā | anīśvaravināśyādikartṛmattvaṃ prasajyate ||
kulālavac ca naitasya vyāpāro yadi kalpate | acetanaḥ kathaṃ bhāvas tadicchām anurudhyate ||
tasmān na paramāṇvāder ārambhaḥ syāt tadicchayā | puruṣasya ca śuddhasya nāśuddhā vikṛtir bhavet ||
svādhīnatvāc ca dharmādes tena kleśo na yujyate | tadvaśena pravṛttau vā vyatirekaḥ prasajyate ||
svayaṃ ca śuddharūpatvād asattvāc cānyavastunaḥ | svapnādivadavidyāyāḥ pravṛttis tasya kiṃ kṛtā ||
anyenopaplave 'bhīṣṭe dvaitavādaḥ prasajyate | svābhāvikīm avidyāṃ tu nocchettuṃ kaś cid arhati ||
vilakṣaṇopapāte hi naśyet svābhāvikī kva cit | na tv ekātmābhyupāyānāṃ hetur asti vilakṣaṇaḥ ||
pumānakartā yeṣāṃ tu teṣām api guṇaiḥ kriyā | katham ādau bhavet, tatra karma tāvan na vidyate ||
mithyājñānaṃ na trāsti rāgadveṣādayo 'pi vā | manovṛttir hi sarveṣāṃ na cotpannaṃ tadā manaḥ ||
karmaṇāṃ śaktyavasthānāṃ yair uktā bandhahetutā | sā na yuktā na kāryaṃ hi śaktisthāt kāraṇād bhavet ||
dadhiśaktir na hi kṣīre dādhikārambham arhati | dadhyārambhasya sā hetus tato 'nyā dādhikasya tu ||
kāraṇāc chaktyavasthāc ca yadi kāryaṃ prajāyate | bandhaḥ punaḥ prasajyeta phale datte 'pi karmaṇā ||
śaktyavasthatvam eveṣṭaṃ vināśe 'pi hi karmaṇām | prāk cāpi śaktisadbhāvād anuṣṭhānaṃ vṛthā bhavet ||
śaktyavasthaṃ ca rāgādi kiṃ neṣṭaṃ bandhakāraṇam | karmādattaphalatvāc cet, nāvyaktim api tad vrajet ||
tacchaktyapratiyogitvān na jñānaṃ mokṣakāraṇam | karmaśaktyā na hi jñānaṃ virodham upagacchati ||
yady apy ajñānajanyatvaṃ karmaṇām avagamyate | rāgādivat tathāpy eṣāṃ na jñānena nirākriyā ||
karmakṣayo hi vijñānād ity etac cāpramāṇavat | phalasyālpasya vā dānaṃ rājaputrāparādhavat ||
adyatve 'pi hi śaktisthaṃ yadi syāt karmakāraṇam | tataḥ pradhānakāle 'pi yujyate kāraṇābhidhā ||
manovṛttir idānīṃ tu hetur nāsti ca sā tadā | manasāṃ saṅkarāc cāpi tadā syāt karmasaṅkaraḥ ||
gasmān naiṣo 'dhikārākhyo bandhahetuḥ prakalpate | yogyatve 'py adhikārākhye viprayogo na yujyate ||
caitanyaṃ yogyatā puṃsaḥ prakṛtes tadanātmatā | bhoktṛbhogyatvayos te ca na tābhyām apagacchataḥ ||
utpattau karmaṇāṃ ceṣṭam ajñānaṃ kāraṇaṃ yadi | tannāśāt syād anutpattis teṣāṃ na phalavarjanam ||
jñānaṃ mokṣanimittaṃ ca gamyate nendriyādinā | na ca sāṅkhyādivijñānān mokṣo vedena codyate ||
ātmā jñātavya ity etanmokṣārthaṃ na ca coditam | karmapravṛttihetutvam ātmajñānasya lakṣyate ||
vijñāte cāsya pārārthye yāpi nāma phalaśrutiḥ | sārthavādo bhaved eva na svargādeḥ phalāntaram ||
sukhopabhogarūpaś ca yadi mokṣaḥ prakalpyate | svarga eva bhaved eṣa paryāyeṇa, kṣayo ca saḥ ||
na hi kāraṇavat kiñ cid akṣayitvena gamyate | tasmāt karmakṣayād eva hetvabhāve na mucyate ||
na hy abhāvātmakaṃ muktvā mokṣanityatvakāraṇam | na ca kriyāyāḥ kasyāś cid abhāvaḥ phalam iṣyate ||
tatra jñātātmatattvānāṃ bhogāt pūrvakriyākṣaye | uttarapracayāsattvād deho notpadyate punaḥ ||
karmajanyopabhogārthaṃ śarīraṃ na pravartate | tadabhāve na kaś cid dhi hetus tatrāvatiṣṭhate ||
mokṣārthī na pravarteta tatra kāmyaniṣiddhayoḥ | nityanaimittike kuryāt pratyavāyajihāsayā ||
prārthyamānaṃ phalaṃ jñātaṃ na cānicchor bhaviṣyati | ātmajñe caitad astīti tajjñānam upayujyate ||
sargapralayavijñānaṃ samastajagadāśrayam | svaśarīravidāṃ puṃsāṃ nādhikyenopayujyate ||
tasmād adyavad evātra sargapralayakalpanā | samastakṣayajanmabhyāṃ na sidhyatyapramāṇikā ||
sarvajñavanniṣedhyā ca sraṣṭuḥ sadbhāvakalpanā | na ca dharmādṛte tasya bhavel lokād viśiṣṭhatā ||
na cānanuṣṭhito dharmo nānuṣṭhānam ṛte mateḥ | na ca vedādṛte sā syād vedo na ca padādibhiḥ ||
tasmāt prāg api sarve 'mī sraṣṭurāsan padādayaḥ | syāt tatpūrvakatā cāsya caitanyād asmadādivat ||
evaṃ ye yuktibhiḥ prāhus teṣāṃ durlabham uttaram | aneṣyo vyavahāro 'yam anādir vedavādibhiḥ ||
pratyakṣādāv upakṣīṇe yo 'numānena ḍitthavat | sambandhitvān niyoktāraṃ gavādāv api kalpayet ||
gavādiśabdasambandhaṃ sarvo 'nyasmāt prapadyate | madvat tadvyavahāritvāt tasyaitat pratisādhanam ||
devadattādiśabde 'pi prasaktaivam anāditā | sambandhasya, balīyastvād dṛṣṭabādhān nivartate ||
tatrāpi śaktinityatvam, niyogasya tv anityatā | tadgatāc cāpy anityatvāc chaktau bhrāntiḥ pravartate ||
gavādiṣu tu na bhrāntir niyogānāditā yataḥ | yo yo gṛhītaḥ sarvasmāt pūrvaṃ sambandhadarśanāt ||
siddhaḥ sambandha ity evaṃ sambandhādir na vidyate | yadā cāptapraṇītatvāc chabdo 'rthaṃ pratipādayet ||
na svaśaktyā tadāptatvaṃ mitau na smaryate katham | yathā bauddhādayo yāvad buddhādyuktaṃ na jānate ||
na tāvat pratipadyante bodhe vākyena saty api | samaye kathyamāne 'nyair asmaranto 'pi pāṇinim ||
ādaicaḥ pratipadyante vṛddhiṃ kartuṃ smṛtir vṛthā | sūtrasthaḥ pāṇinis tatra svasaṃjñāṃ pratipādayet ||
gauḥ sāsnādimatīty evaṃ vākyaṃ tv atra na vidyate | asambandhāc ca sarveṣām evaṃ kartum asambhavaḥ ||
tasmān na pratipattiḥ syāt kathañ cit kartṛvarjitā | dṛṣārthavyavahāratvād vṛddhyādau sambhaved api ||
dharmāya niyamo 'trāpi na vinā pāṇiner bhavet | ākārānugamo yo hi vṛddhyā syād āśvalāyane ||
nāsāv apāṇinīyatve sādhur ity avagamyate | dṛṣṭe bhavatu mā vā bhūt kartṛsampratipannatā ||
vaidido vyavahāras tu na kartṛsmaraṇād ṛte | burgeṣu gavi gośabdaprayogo gamyate katham ||
gatvā cet kena cid dṛṣṭaḥ, sambanddhā kiṃ na gacchati | īśvaratvād gatiś cāsya na kva cit pratibadhyate ||
bahūnāṃ kāryataś cāpi saṅgānaṃ kena vāryate | ekatra kathitaṃ cāpi lokenānyatra nīyate ||
vṛddhyādiva, ato vyākhyā dvitīyaivātra śobhanā | kāṃś cit prasiddhasambandhān abhyupetya vaded yadi ||
sambandhakaraṇam, tatra ke siddhā iti durvadam | na tāvad anya evāsan śabdā iti hi yuktimat ||
viśeṣo 'dyatanānāṃ ca gavādīnāṃ na dṛśyate | śabdārthānāditāṃ muktvā sambandhānādikāraṇam ||
na syād anyad, ato vede sambandhādir na vidyate | upāyarahitatvena sambandhakaraṇānumā ||
anākhyānānumānaṃ tu dṛṣṭenaiva viruddhyate | buddhānāṃ dṛśyamānā ca pratipattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||
upāya iti taddhānirasiddhāvagatiṃ prati | hastasaṃjñādyupāyo hi siddho nādyakriyāsu naḥ ||
na hy asau jñātasāmarthyo vinānyair vyavahartṛbhiḥ | śabdavṛddhābhidheyāṃś ca pratyakṣeṇātra paśyati ||
śrotuś ca pratipannatvam anumānena ceṣṭayā | anyathā 'nupapattyā ca buddhyec chaktiṃ dvayāśritām | arthāpattyāvabuddhyante sambandhaṃ tripramāṇakam ||

§ 5,17 citrākṣepaparihāra CAP

citrādiniṣphalatve 'pi yaduktaṃ sādhanadvayam | tatra hetor asiddhatvam ānantaryaṃ hy acoditam ||
ānantaryaśrutiś cātra sāmārthyād api neṣyate | nāviśeṣā phalotpattiḥ karmaṇā nopapadyate ||
karmaṇāṃ cāpi vaicitryād deśakālādyapekṣaṇāt | kasya cic cārddhabhuktatvāt karmānyat pratibadhyate ||
tenānantaryaniṣpattiḥ phalasyehāpramāṇikā | pratyakṣādivisaṃvādo na śabde doṣamāsajet ||
ānantaryavisaṃvādo nāviśeṣapravartinīm | codanāṃ bādhituṃ śaktaḥ sphuṭād viṣayabhedataḥ ||
yā tu mardanasādharmyād ānantaryā 'numā kṛtā | bādhyate 'nupalabdhyāsau samānaviṣayā yataḥ ||
dṛṣṭārthasyāpi sevāder āyātam api satphalam | utpadyate cireṇaiva pratibandhena kena cit ||
uptamātre na hi vrīhau phalam utpadyate kva cit | athāṅkuro 'pi tatra syāt, svargo 'py astīti gamyatām ||
sthūlībhūtaś cireṇaiṣa bhogyatvaṃ pratipadyate | sarvasyotpadyamānasya kramaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sthitaḥ ||
anantaraphalatvaṃ tu citrāder yadi sādhyate | tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatvam anyadā na phalaṃ bhavet ||
vyabhicārāc ca sevādeḥ paśvādeḥ sādhanāntaram | kim apy adṛṣṭam asty eva tatrānyanniṣpramāṇakam ||
īśvarecchādhikārādiśabdaliṅgādivarjanāt | kṛtaṃ kadā cic citrādiśabdena tv avagamyate ||
nirnimittā na cotpattiḥ, na hi sarvāpramāṇatā | bodhayan na ca śabdo 'tra prāmāṇyād ativarttate ||
yeṣāṃ tv iha phalāny eva citrādīnīti kalpanā | nirnimittaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ syād ihākṛtakarmaṇām ||
citrādīnāṃ phalaṃ tāvat kṣīṇaṃ tatraiva janmani | na ca svargaphalasyeha kaś cid aṃśo 'nuvartate ||
naiva hy anyaphalaṃ karma sādhayen naḥ phalāntaram | gautamīye 'pi taccheṣas tasmāc citrādyapekṣayā ||
svābhāvikatve siddhe ca karmānantarabhāvy api | phalaṃ kriyānimittatvaṃ na kathañ cit prapadyate ||
tatra mlecchādivat sarve karmākṛtvāpi vaidikam | palaṃ labhanta ity evaṃ naṣṭā vedapramāṇatā ||
anantaraṃ niyogena paśvādi ca bhaved yadi | pratyakṣaphalataiva syāt trivṛtpānavirekavat ||
janmāntarānubhūtaṃ ca na smaryata itīdṛśam | na bhāṣyaṃ na ca sūtraṃ syād aprāpte śāstram arthavat ||
tasmāt kālāviśeṣeṇa codanārtho yathā sthitaḥ | sa tathaivānugantavyo nādhiko niṣpramāṇakaḥ ||
sarveṣāṃ karmavaiguṇyāt phalābhāvaṃ vadanti ye | ānantaryam upetyaiva te svābhāvikavādinaḥ ||
svargasyāmuṣmikatvaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhādye sthāpayiṣyate | paśvāder niyamābhāvo yogasiddhir itīha tu ||
yadā kadā cid bhavad etad iṣyate phalaṃ hi paśvādi na sāmparāyikam | tathā sthitasyaiva hi tasya sādhanaṃ vidhīyate yo 'pi bhṛśaṃ tvarānvitaḥ ||
sādhāraṇaṃ yat tu palaṃ bahūnāṃ svabhāvatas tādṛśam eva ceṣṭam | sarvasya vā ''san na tayaiva kāmyaṃ vṛṣṭyādi tac caihikam eva yuktam ||
kamipadam aviśiṣṭaṃ yady api śrūyate vā bhavati phalaviśeṣī nānyathā kāmyate hi | phalati yadi na sarvaṃ tat kadā cit tadaiva dhruvam aparam abhuktaṃ karma śāstrīyamās te ||

§ 5,18 ātmavāda ATV

sākṣād yady api sambandho nātmano yajñasādhanaiḥ | tathāpi lakṣaṇāvṛttyā śarīradvārako bhavet ||
pratyakṣatvaṃ ca dehasthaṃ bhāktam ātmani kalpitam | ātmanaḥ svargayānaṃ vā śarīrasyopacaryyate ||
nairātmyenātra cākṣiptāḥ sarvā eva hi codanāḥ | sādhyasādhanasambandhas tadukto na hi siddhyati ||
tā hi kartuḥ phalenāhuḥ sambandhaṃ kvāpi janmani | na ca vijñānamātratve bhoktṛkartṛtvasambhavaḥ ||
śarīravinipātāc ca paraṃ nānyad yadeṣyate | adattaphalaïṣṭyādau tadā tadvacanaṃ mṛṣā ||
tasmād vedapramāṇārtham ātmātra pratipādyate | yady api prakṛtaṃ vākyaṃ vyākhyāyetārthavādataḥ ||
śarīrendriyabuddhibhyo vyatiriktatvam ātmanaḥ | nityatvaṃ ceṣyate, śeṣaṃ śarīrādi vinaśyate ||
nityaḥ kartṛtvabhoktṛtve pratipanno 'pi san yadā | na karmaphalasambandhaṃ bhogakāle 'vabudhyate ||
mayā yat tu kṛtaṃ karma tasyedaṃ bhujyate phalam | śubhāśubhaṃ mayaiveti tadā ko 'sya raso bhavet ||
aparāmṛśyamāne hi svakarmapratyaye phale | na viśeṣo bhavet kaś cit svaparātmopabhogayoḥ ||
kurvann apy aśubhaṃ karma tenaivaṃ cintayen naraḥ | na smariṣyāmi bhoge 'ham iti naitad vivarjayet ||
tatra nityatvapakṣe 'pi kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau | phalatas tulyarūpau ced vṛthā tatpratipādanam ||
naiṣa doṣaḥ, na bhoge hi smṛtir na upayujyate | na pravṛttir nivṛttir vā bhogakāle smṛter bhavet ||
tadaṅgaṃ yaḥ parāmarśas tadastitvaṃ ca mṛgyate | prāk pravṛttes tu so 'sty eva viduṣāṃ śāstrataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
paścād api ca śāstrajñā vimṛśanty eva ke cana | teṣām evādhikāraś ca mā bhūd aviduṣāṃ tu saḥ ||
parāmarśaś ca sarvatra nāsti sarvapramāṇakaḥ | na cānyenāparāmṛṣṭe syād anyasyāpramāṇatā ||
nāvabudhyeta yas tv evaṃ mamāsmāt karmaṇaḥ phalam | bhaviṣyatīty avidvattvād daivād evātra na kriyā ||
aparāmṛśyamāne 'pi svāpakāle sukhāśraye | sambhoge mṛduśayyādau prākpravṛttiś ca dṛśyate ||
bhogakāle 'nusandadhyāt phalaṃ yadi tu kaś cana | rathādikarmavad yāge śāstraṃ syād aprakalpakam ||
tava nityavibhutvābhyām ātmāno niṣkriyā yadi | sukhaduḥkhāvikāryāś ca kīdṛśo kartṛbhoktṛtā ||
atha kartṛtvavelāyāṃ duḥkhādeś cāpi janmani | prāgrūpād anyathātvaṃ syān nityatāsya virudhyate ||
nānityaśabdavācyatvam ātmano vinivāryate | vikriyāmātravācitve na hy ucchedo 'sya tāvatā ||
syātām atyantanāśe 'sya kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau | na tv avasthāntaraprāptau loke bālayuvādivat ||
avasthāntarabhāvyetat phalaṃ mama śubhāśubham | iti jñātvānutiṣṭhaṃś ca vijahac ceṣṭate janaḥ ||
anavasthāntaraprāptir dṛśyate na ca kasya cit | anucchedāt tu nānyatvaṃ bhoktur loko 'vagacchati ||
sukhaduḥkhādyavasthāś ca gacchann api naro mama | caitanyadravyasattādirūpaṃ naiva vimuñcati ||
duḥkhinaḥ sukhyavasthāyāṃ naśyeyuḥ sarva eva te | duḥkhitvaṃ cānuvarteta vināśe vikriyātmake ||
tasmād ubhayahānena vyāvṛttyanugamātmakaḥ | puruṣo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ kuṇḍalādiṣu svarṇavat ||
na ca kartṛtvabhoktṛtve puṃso 'vasthāsam āśrite | tenāvasthāvatas tattvāt karttaivāpnoti tatphalam ||
na cāvasthāntarotpāde pūrvātyantaṃ vinaśyati | uttarānuguṇatvāt tu sāmānyātmani līyate ||
svarūpeṇa hy avasthānām anyonyasya virodhitā | aviruddhas tu sarvāsu sāmānyātmā pravartate ||
nairātmyavādapakṣe tu pūrvam evāvabudhyate | madvināśāt phalaṃ nasyānmatto 'nyasyātha vā bhavet ||
iti naiva pravṛttiḥ syān na ca vedapramāṇatā | janmānare 'bhyupete 'pi jñānamātrātmavādinām ||
jñānānāṃ kṣaṇikatvād dhi kartṛbhoktranyatā bhavet | niṣkriyatvāvibhutvābhyāṃ na ca dehāntarāśritiḥ ||
kartā ya eva santāno nanu bhoktā sa eva naḥ | vijñānakṣaṇabhedas tu tvadavasthāntaraiḥ samaḥ ||
kartṛtvam eva duḥsādhaṃ dīrghakāleṣu karmasu | satsu jñānasahastreṣu kulakalpopamaṃ hi tat ||
vyatirikto hi santāno yadi nābhyupagamyate | santāninām anityatvāt kartā kaś cin na labhyate ||
bhoktur atyantabhedāc ca prasajyetākṛtāgamaḥ | kṛtanāśaṃ tu na brūmaḥ kṛtaṃ naiva hi kena cit ||
santānānanyatāyāṃ tu vācoyuktyantareṇa te | tatra coktam, na cāvastu santānaḥ kartṛtāṃ vrajet ||
santānakṣaṇikatve ca tad eva, akṣaṇikas tv atha | siddhāntahāniḥ, evaṃ ca so 'pi dravyāntaraṃ bhavet ||
ekā cāvyatiriktā ca santānibhyo 'tha santatiḥ | bhedābhedau prasaṅktavyau grāhyagrāhakayor yathā ||
tasmād atyantabhedo vā kathañ cid vāpi bhinnatā | santānasyety ayaṃ cātmā syād vaiśeṣikasāṃkhyayoḥ ||
santāno 'yaṃ sa eveti na tv abhedād vinā bhavet | vāyudopādisantāne vāyutvādir na bhidyate ||
jñānatvenāpy abhinnatvaṃ śūnyavāde nirākṛtam | tathaiva karmabhir veṣṭā phalārthaṃ cittavāsanā ||
na cātra vāsanākālaṃ kiñ cic cittam avasthitam | avastutvāc ca santānaḥ karmabhirnaiva vāsyate ||
tatpāramparyajāte 'pi bhuñjāne karmaṇaḥ phalam | tādātmyena vinā spaṣṭau kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau ||
santānāntarajebhyaś ca yo hetuphalabhāvataḥ | viśeṣaḥ so 'pi dussādhaḥ, parihāro na cānayoḥ ||
tasminn asaty api brūyāḥ parihāraṃ tvam anyathā | samānapṛthivīvāsajñānatvādyaviśeṣataḥ ||
samāna iti nāpy etadekatvānugamād vinā | tena yaccittajaṃ tasya santāna iti vo mṛṣā ||
na hi yacchabdatacchabdau vartete bhinnavastuni | tenaikātmakataiṣṭavyā tatsantānātmavādibhiḥ ||
nanv anyatvaṃ vidanto 'pi putrādiphalasiddhaye | pravartante yathā tadvajjñānasantānino 'pi naḥ ||
anyatve ca samāne 'pi yathā vaṃśāntarodbhavāḥ | na labhante phalaṃ tadvat santānāntarajāḥ kṣaṇāḥ ||
na tāvad buddhir atraivam, api cātmaphalecchayā | putrādibharaṇe vṛttiḥ syāt tad apy atra nāsti te ||
phalāntaram anuddiśya na ca putrādi bibhrati | vinaṣṭasya tu nātmīyasantānabharaṇāt phalam ||
yas tv anenaiva mārgeṇa phalāntaram apīcchati | svasantānyantarair bhogyaṃ tatsantānāny upakārakam ||
anavasthedṛśī tasya svopabhogād ṛte bhavet | naiva hy anyo 'pi santānī kaś cit tasyātmavanmataḥ ||
yāvad yāvac ca dūrasthe santānini phalaṃ bhavet | tāvat tāvac ca tannaśyet sutarāṃ viprakarṣataḥ ||
bharaṇaṃ yadapatyānāṃ tiryagādiṣu dṛśyate | ajñānaṃ śaraṇaṃ tatra prājñānāṃ tu na yujyate ||
dehāntare ca buddhīnāṃ sañcāro nopapadyate | pūrvadehād bahir bhāvo na ca tāsāṃ pratīyate ||
vāyunā preryamāṇaṃ hi jvālādyanyatra sañcaret | buddheḥ kāraṇadeśāt tu preraṇaṃ nāsti kena cit ||
amūrtatvāt svayaṃ nāsāvutplutyā 'nyatra gacchati | jīvaddehe 'pi tenāsyā gamanaṃ nopapadyate ||
antarābhavadehas tu niṣiddho vindhyavāsinā | tadastitve pramāṇaṃ hi na kiñ cid avagamyate ||
sahasā jāyate tac ca sahasaiva vinaśyati | sūkṣmarūpādiyuktaṃ cety utprekṣāmātram eva tat ||
saty api jñānasañcāras tatra syān niṣpramāṇakaḥ | tena cānyaśarīreṣu punarnikṣepakalpanā ||
kalalādiṣu vijñānam astīty etac ca sāhasam | asañjātendriyatvād dhi na tatrārtho 'vagamyate ||
na cārthāvagater anyad rūpaṃ jñānasya yujyate | mūrcchādāv api tenāsya sadbhāvo nopapadyate ||
na cāpi śaktirūpeṇa tadā dhīr avatiṣṭhate | nirāśrayatvāc chaktīnāṃ sthitir na hy avakalpate ||
yadi bhūtendriyādhārā jñānaśaktir bhavet tataḥ | tac caitanyaṃ prasajyeta na ca janmāntaraṃ bhavet ||
pariṇāmavivekādyaiḥ śaktyabhivyaktyanugrahāt | tebhya eva bhaved buddhir na buddhyantarapūrvikā ||
tathaivottarakāle 'pi pūrvabuddher yad ucyate | buddhyantaraprasūtatvaṃ dṛṣṭānto 'tra na vidyate ||
athādhāravinirmuktā śaktiḥ syāt kalalādiṣu | paścād vijñānasiddhyartham ātmā śaktyabhidho bhavet ||
śaktyādhāraprakḷptau vā nātmano 'nyaḥ prakalpyate | jvālābudbudavad vṛttir na cādhārād vinā dhiyām ||
jñānaśaktisvabhāvo 'to nityaḥ sarvagataḥ pumān | dehāntarakṣamaḥ kalpyaḥ so 'gacchann eva yokṣyate ||
yajamānatvam apy ātmā sakriyatvāt prapadyate | na parispanda evaikaḥ kriyā naḥ kaṇabhojivat ||
na ca svasamavetaiva kartṛbhiḥ kriyate kriyā | kriyā dhātvarthamātraṃ syād anyādhāre 'pi kartṛtā ||
sattājñānādirūpāṇāṃ kartā tāvat svayaṃ pumān | yo 'pi bhūtaparispandas tatrādhiṣṭānato bhavet ||
taduddeśapravṛtteś ca yā yā dehendriyaiḥ kriyā | kriyate puruṣeṇaiva sā sā sarvā kṛtocyate ||
naiva hy eṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ syāt puruṣeṇāparigrahe | asvātantryād ato naiṣāṃ parispande 'pi kartṛtā ||
tatkarmopārjitaiś cetaiḥ kriyamāṇeṣu karmasu | kartṛtā yajamānānām ṛtvikparaśukarmavat ||
yathā parikrayāmnānād ṛtvigdvārā kriyeṣyate | gamanādividhes tadvad bhūtadvāratvam āśritam ||
krayo yathātmano nāsti gamanādi tathaiva hi | vidhīyate ca tenātra paradvārāsya kartṛtā ||
yathā vā devadattasya cchedane kāṣṭhasaṃśrite | kartṛtvam evaṃ puṃsaḥ syāc charīragamanādiṣu ||
vyāpārāntaratas tatra kartṛtvaṃ ced ihāpi naḥ | saṅkalpasattvavattvābhyāṃ pumāniṣṭaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
sādhāraṇyena kartṛtvaṃ sattvavattvena karmasu | saṅkalpanaiḥ punarbhedāt pratikarmāsya kartṛtā ||
